00001 subroutine qag ( f, a, b, epsabs, epsrel, key, result, abserr, neval, ier )
00002 
00003 !*****************************************************************************80
00004 !
00005 !! QAG approximates an integral over a finite interval.
00006 !
00007 !  Discussion:
00008 !
00009 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral   
00010 !      I = integral of F over (A,B),
00011 !    hopefully satisfying
00012 !      || I - RESULT || <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * ||I|| ).
00013 !
00014 !    QAG is a simple globally adaptive integrator using the strategy of 
00015 !    Aind (Piessens, 1973).  It is possible to choose between 6 pairs of
00016 !    Gauss-Kronrod quadrature formulae for the rule evaluation component. 
00017 !    The pairs of high degree of precision are suitable for handling
00018 !    integration difficulties due to a strongly oscillating integrand.
00019 !
00020 !  Author:
00021 !
00022 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
00023 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
00024 !
00025 !  Reference:
00026 !
00027 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
00028 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
00029 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
00030 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
00031 !
00032 !  Parameters:
00033 !
00034 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
00035 !      function f ( x )
00036 !      real f
00037 !      real x
00038 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
00039 !
00040 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
00041 !
00042 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
00043 !
00044 !    Input, integer KEY, chooses the order of the local integration rule:
00045 !    1,  7 Gauss points, 15 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00046 !    2, 10 Gauss points, 21 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00047 !    3, 15 Gauss points, 31 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00048 !    4, 20 Gauss points, 41 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00049 !    5, 25 Gauss points, 51 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00050 !    6, 30 Gauss points, 61 Gauss-Kronrod points.
00051 !
00052 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
00053 !
00054 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
00055 !
00056 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
00057 !
00058 !    Output, integer IER, return code.
00059 !    0, normal and reliable termination of the routine.  It is assumed that the 
00060 !      requested accuracy has been achieved.
00061 !    1, maximum number of subdivisions allowed has been achieved.  One can 
00062 !      allow more subdivisions by increasing the value of LIMIT in QAG. 
00063 !      However, if this yields no improvement it is advised to analyze the
00064 !      integrand to determine the integration difficulties.  If the position
00065 !      of a local difficulty can be determined, such as a singularity or
00066 !      discontinuity within the interval) one will probably gain from 
00067 !      splitting up the interval at this point and calling the integrator 
00068 !      on the subranges.  If possible, an appropriate special-purpose 
00069 !      integrator should be used which is designed for handling the type 
00070 !      of difficulty involved.
00071 !    2, the occurrence of roundoff error is detected, which prevents the
00072 !      requested tolerance from being achieved.
00073 !    3, extremely bad integrand behavior occurs at some points of the
00074 !      integration interval.
00075 !    6, the input is invalid, because EPSABS < 0 and EPSREL < 0.
00076 !
00077 !  Local parameters:
00078 !
00079 !    LIMIT is the maximum number of subintervals allowed in
00080 !    the subdivision process of QAGE.
00081 !
00082   implicit none
00083 
00084   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
00085 
00086   real a
00087   real abserr
00088   real alist(limit)
00089   real b
00090   real blist(limit)
00091   real elist(limit)
00092   real epsabs
00093   real epsrel
00094   real, external :: f
00095   integer ier
00096   integer iord(limit)
00097   integer key
00098   integer last
00099   integer neval
00100   real result
00101   real rlist(limit)
00102 
00103   call qage ( f, a, b, epsabs, epsrel, key, limit, result, abserr, neval, &
00104     ier, alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, last )
00105 
00106   return
00107 end
00108 subroutine qage ( f, a, b, epsabs, epsrel, key, limit, result, abserr, neval, &
00109   ier, alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, last )
00110 
00111 !*****************************************************************************80
00112 !
00113 !! QAGE estimates a definite integral.
00114 !
00115 !  Discussion:
00116 !
00117 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral   
00118 !      I = integral of F over (A,B),
00119 !    hopefully satisfying
00120 !      || I - RESULT || <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * ||I|| ).
00121 !
00122 !  Author:
00123 !
00124 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
00125 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
00126 !
00127 !  Reference:
00128 !
00129 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
00130 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
00131 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
00132 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
00133 !
00134 !  Parameters:
00135 !
00136 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
00137 !      function f ( x )
00138 !      real f
00139 !      real x
00140 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
00141 !
00142 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
00143 !
00144 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
00145 !
00146 !    Input, integer KEY, chooses the order of the local integration rule:
00147 !    1,  7 Gauss points, 15 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00148 !    2, 10 Gauss points, 21 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00149 !    3, 15 Gauss points, 31 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00150 !    4, 20 Gauss points, 41 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00151 !    5, 25 Gauss points, 51 Gauss-Kronrod points,
00152 !    6, 30 Gauss points, 61 Gauss-Kronrod points.
00153 !
00154 !    Input, integer LIMIT, the maximum number of subintervals that
00155 !    can be used.
00156 !
00157 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
00158 !
00159 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
00160 !
00161 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
00162 !
00163 !    Output, integer IER, return code.
00164 !    0, normal and reliable termination of the routine.  It is assumed that the 
00165 !      requested accuracy has been achieved.
00166 !    1, maximum number of subdivisions allowed has been achieved.  One can 
00167 !      allow more subdivisions by increasing the value of LIMIT in QAG. 
00168 !      However, if this yields no improvement it is advised to analyze the
00169 !      integrand to determine the integration difficulties.  If the position
00170 !      of a local difficulty can be determined, such as a singularity or
00171 !      discontinuity within the interval) one will probably gain from 
00172 !      splitting up the interval at this point and calling the integrator 
00173 !      on the subranges.  If possible, an appropriate special-purpose 
00174 !      integrator should be used which is designed for handling the type 
00175 !      of difficulty involved.
00176 !    2, the occurrence of roundoff error is detected, which prevents the
00177 !      requested tolerance from being achieved.
00178 !    3, extremely bad integrand behavior occurs at some points of the
00179 !      integration interval.
00180 !    6, the input is invalid, because EPSABS < 0 and EPSREL < 0.
00181 !
00182 !    Workspace, real ALIST(LIMIT), BLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 
00183 !    through LAST the left and right ends of the partition subintervals.
00184 !
00185 !    Workspace, real RLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
00186 !    the integral approximations on the subintervals.
00187 !
00188 !    Workspace, real ELIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
00189 !    the absolute error estimates on the subintervals.
00190 !
00191 !    Output, integer IORD(LIMIT), the first K elements of which are pointers 
00192 !    to the error estimates over the subintervals, such that
00193 !    elist(iord(1)), ..., elist(iord(k)) form a decreasing sequence, with
00194 !    k = last if last <= (limit/2+2), and k = limit+1-last otherwise.
00195 !
00196 !    Output, integer LAST, the number of subintervals actually produced 
00197 !    in the subdivision process.
00198 !
00199 !  Local parameters:
00200 !
00201 !    alist     - list of left end points of all subintervals
00202 !                       considered up to now
00203 !    blist     - list of right end points of all subintervals
00204 !                       considered up to now
00205 !    elist(i)  - error estimate applying to rlist(i)
00206 !    maxerr    - pointer to the interval with largest error estimate
00207 !    errmax    - elist(maxerr)
00208 !    area      - sum of the integrals over the subintervals
00209 !    errsum    - sum of the errors over the subintervals
00210 !    errbnd    - requested accuracy max(epsabs,epsrel*abs(result))
00211 !    *****1    - variable for the left subinterval
00212 !    *****2    - variable for the right subinterval
00213 !    last      - index for subdivision
00214 !
00215   implicit none
00216 
00217   integer limit
00218 
00219   real a
00220   real abserr
00221   real alist(limit)
00222   real area
00223   real area1
00224   real area12
00225   real area2
00226   real a1
00227   real a2
00228   real b
00229   real blist(limit)
00230   real b1
00231   real b2
00232   real c
00233   real defabs
00234   real defab1
00235   real defab2
00236   real elist(limit)
00237   real epsabs
00238   real epsrel
00239   real errbnd
00240   real errmax
00241   real error1
00242   real error2
00243   real erro12
00244   real errsum
00245   real, external :: f
00246   integer ier
00247   integer iord(limit)
00248   integer iroff1
00249   integer iroff2
00250   integer key
00251   integer keyf
00252   integer last
00253   integer maxerr
00254   integer neval
00255   integer nrmax
00256   real resabs
00257   real result
00258   real rlist(limit)
00259 !
00260 !  Test on validity of parameters.
00261 !
00262   ier = 0
00263   neval = 0
00264   last = 0
00265   result = 0.0e+00
00266   abserr = 0.0e+00
00267   alist(1) = a
00268   blist(1) = b
00269   rlist(1) = 0.0e+00
00270   elist(1) = 0.0e+00
00271   iord(1) = 0
00272 
00273   if ( epsabs < 0.0e+00 .and. epsrel < 0.0e+00 ) then
00274     ier = 6
00275     return
00276   end if
00277 !
00278 !  First approximation to the integral.
00279 !
00280   keyf = key
00281   keyf = max ( keyf, 1 )
00282   keyf = min ( keyf, 6 )
00283 
00284   c = keyf
00285   neval = 0
00286 
00287   if ( keyf == 1 ) then
00288     call qk15 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
00289   else if ( keyf == 2 ) then
00290     call qk21 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
00291   else if ( keyf == 3 ) then
00292     call qk31 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
00293   else if ( keyf == 4 ) then
00294     call qk41 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
00295   else if ( keyf == 5 ) then
00296     call qk51 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
00297   else if ( keyf == 6 ) then
00298     call qk61 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
00299   end if
00300 
00301   last = 1
00302   rlist(1) = result
00303   elist(1) = abserr
00304   iord(1) = 1
00305 !
00306 !  Test on accuracy.
00307 !
00308   errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs ( result ) )
00309 
00310   if ( abserr <= 5.0e+01 * epsilon ( defabs ) * defabs .and. &
00311     errbnd < abserr ) then
00312     ier = 2
00313   end if
00314 
00315   if ( limit == 1 ) then
00316     ier = 1
00317   end if
00318 
00319   if ( ier /= 0 .or. &
00320     ( abserr <= errbnd .and. abserr /= resabs ) .or. &
00321     abserr == 0.0e+00 ) then
00322 
00323     if ( keyf /= 1 ) then
00324       neval = (10*keyf+1) * (2*neval+1)
00325     else
00326       neval = 30 * neval + 15
00327     end if
00328 
00329     return
00330 
00331   end if
00332 !
00333 !  Initialization.
00334 !
00335   errmax = abserr
00336   maxerr = 1
00337   area = result
00338   errsum = abserr
00339   nrmax = 1
00340   iroff1 = 0
00341   iroff2 = 0
00342 
00343   do last = 2, limit
00344 !
00345 !  Bisect the subinterval with the largest error estimate.
00346 !
00347     a1 = alist(maxerr)
00348     b1 = 0.5E+00 * ( alist(maxerr) + blist(maxerr) )
00349     a2 = b1
00350     b2 = blist(maxerr)
00351 
00352     if ( keyf == 1 ) then
00353       call qk15 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1 )
00354     else if ( keyf == 2 ) then
00355       call qk21 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1 )
00356     else if ( keyf == 3 ) then
00357       call qk31 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1 )
00358     else if ( keyf == 4 ) then
00359       call qk41 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1)
00360     else if ( keyf == 5 ) then
00361       call qk51 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1 )
00362     else if ( keyf == 6 ) then
00363       call qk61 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1 )
00364     end if
00365 
00366     if ( keyf == 1 ) then
00367       call qk15 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
00368     else if ( keyf == 2 ) then
00369       call qk21 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
00370     else if ( keyf == 3 ) then
00371       call qk31 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
00372     else if ( keyf == 4 ) then
00373       call qk41 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
00374     else if ( keyf == 5 ) then
00375       call qk51 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
00376     else if ( keyf == 6 ) then
00377       call qk61 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
00378     end if
00379 !
00380 !  Improve previous approximations to integral and error and
00381 !  test for accuracy.
00382 !
00383     neval = neval + 1
00384     area12 = area1 + area2
00385     erro12 = error1 + error2
00386     errsum = errsum + erro12 - errmax
00387     area = area + area12 - rlist(maxerr)
00388 
00389     if ( defab1 /= error1 .and. defab2 /= error2 ) then
00390 
00391       if ( abs ( rlist(maxerr) - area12 ) <= 1.0e-05 * abs ( area12 ) &
00392         .and. 9.9e-01 * errmax <= erro12 ) then
00393         iroff1 = iroff1 + 1
00394       end if
00395 
00396       if ( 10 < last .and. errmax < erro12 ) then
00397         iroff2 = iroff2 + 1
00398       end if
00399 
00400     end if
00401 
00402     rlist(maxerr) = area1
00403     rlist(last) = area2
00404     errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs ( area ) )
00405 !
00406 !  Test for roundoff error and eventually set error flag.
00407 !
00408     if ( errbnd < errsum ) then
00409 
00410       if ( 6 <= iroff1 .or. 20 <= iroff2 ) then
00411         ier = 2
00412       end if
00413 !
00414 !  Set error flag in the case that the number of subintervals
00415 !  equals limit.
00416 !
00417       if ( last == limit ) then
00418         ier = 1
00419       end if
00420 !
00421 !  Set error flag in the case of bad integrand behavior
00422 !  at a point of the integration range.
00423 !
00424       if ( max ( abs ( a1 ), abs ( b2 ) ) <= ( 1.0e+00 + c * 1.0e+03 * &
00425         epsilon ( a1 ) ) * ( abs ( a2 ) + 1.0e+04 * tiny ( a2 ) ) ) then
00426         ier = 3
00427       end if
00428 
00429     end if
00430 !
00431 !  Append the newly-created intervals to the list.
00432 !
00433     if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
00434       alist(last) = a2
00435       blist(maxerr) = b1
00436       blist(last) = b2
00437       elist(maxerr) = error1
00438       elist(last) = error2
00439     else
00440       alist(maxerr) = a2
00441       alist(last) = a1
00442       blist(last) = b1
00443       rlist(maxerr) = area2
00444       rlist(last) = area1
00445       elist(maxerr) = error2
00446       elist(last) = error1
00447     end if
00448 !
00449 !  Call QSORT to maintain the descending ordering
00450 !  in the list of error estimates and select the subinterval
00451 !  with the largest error estimate (to be bisected next).
00452 !
00453     call qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, errmax, elist, iord, nrmax )
00454  
00455     if ( ier /= 0 .or. errsum <= errbnd ) then
00456       exit
00457     end if
00458 
00459   end do
00460 !
00461 !  Compute final result.
00462 !
00463   result = sum ( rlist(1:last) )
00464 
00465   abserr = errsum
00466 
00467   if ( keyf /= 1 ) then
00468     neval = ( 10 * keyf + 1 ) * ( 2 * neval + 1 )
00469   else
00470     neval = 30 * neval + 15
00471   end if
00472 
00473   return
00474 end
00475 subroutine qagi ( f, bound, inf, epsabs, epsrel, result, abserr, neval, ier )
00476 
00477 !*****************************************************************************80
00478 !
00479 !! QAGI estimates an integral over a semi-infinite or infinite interval.
00480 !
00481 !  Discussion:
00482 !
00483 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral   
00484 !      I = integral of F over (A, +Infinity), 
00485 !    or 
00486 !      I = integral of F over (-Infinity,A)
00487 !    or 
00488 !      I = integral of F over (-Infinity,+Infinity),
00489 !    hopefully satisfying
00490 !      || I - RESULT || <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * ||I|| ).
00491 !
00492 !  Author:
00493 !
00494 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
00495 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
00496 !
00497 !  Reference:
00498 !
00499 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
00500 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
00501 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
00502 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
00503 !
00504 !  Parameters:
00505 !
00506 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
00507 !      function f ( x )
00508 !      real f
00509 !      real x
00510 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
00511 !
00512 !    Input, real BOUND, the value of the finite endpoint of the integration
00513 !    range, if any, that is, if INF is 1 or -1.
00514 !
00515 !    Input, integer INF, indicates the type of integration range.
00516 !    1:  (  BOUND,    +Infinity),
00517 !    -1: ( -Infinity,  BOUND),
00518 !    2:  ( -Infinity, +Infinity).
00519 !
00520 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
00521 !
00522 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
00523 !
00524 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
00525 !
00526 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
00527 !
00528 !    Output, integer IER, error indicator.
00529 !    0, normal and reliable termination of the routine.  It is assumed that 
00530 !      the requested accuracy has been achieved.
00531 !    > 0,  abnormal termination of the routine.  The estimates for result
00532 !      and error are less reliable.  It is assumed that the requested
00533 !      accuracy has not been achieved.
00534 !    1, maximum number of subdivisions allowed has been achieved.  One can 
00535 !      allow more subdivisions by increasing the data value of LIMIT in QAGI
00536 !      (and taking the according dimension adjustments into account).
00537 !      However, if this yields no improvement it is advised to analyze the
00538 !      integrand in order to determine the integration difficulties.  If the
00539 !      position of a local difficulty can be determined (e.g. singularity,
00540 !      discontinuity within the interval) one will probably gain from
00541 !      splitting up the interval at this point and calling the integrator 
00542 !      on the subranges.  If possible, an appropriate special-purpose 
00543 !      integrator should be used, which is designed for handling the type
00544 !      of difficulty involved.
00545 !    2, the occurrence of roundoff error is detected, which prevents the
00546 !      requested tolerance from being achieved.  The error may be
00547 !      under-estimated.
00548 !    3, extremely bad integrand behavior occurs at some points of the
00549 !      integration interval.
00550 !    4, the algorithm does not converge.  Roundoff error is detected in the
00551 !      extrapolation table.  It is assumed that the requested tolerance
00552 !      cannot be achieved, and that the returned result is the best which 
00553 !      can be obtained.
00554 !    5, the integral is probably divergent, or slowly convergent.  It must 
00555 !      be noted that divergence can occur with any other value of IER.
00556 !    6, the input is invalid, because INF /= 1 and INF /= -1 and INF /= 2, or
00557 !      epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0.  result, abserr, neval are set to zero.
00558 !
00559 !  Local parameters:
00560 !
00561 !            the dimension of rlist2 is determined by the value of
00562 !            limexp in QEXTR.
00563 !
00564 !           alist     - list of left end points of all subintervals
00565 !                       considered up to now
00566 !           blist     - list of right end points of all subintervals
00567 !                       considered up to now
00568 !           rlist(i)  - approximation to the integral over
00569 !                       (alist(i),blist(i))
00570 !           rlist2    - array of dimension at least (limexp+2),
00571 !                       containing the part of the epsilon table
00572 !                       which is still needed for further computations
00573 !           elist(i)  - error estimate applying to rlist(i)
00574 !           maxerr    - pointer to the interval with largest error
00575 !                       estimate
00576 !           errmax    - elist(maxerr)
00577 !           erlast    - error on the interval currently subdivided
00578 !                       (before that subdivision has taken place)
00579 !           area      - sum of the integrals over the subintervals
00580 !           errsum    - sum of the errors over the subintervals
00581 !           errbnd    - requested accuracy max(epsabs,epsrel*
00582 !                       abs(result))
00583 !           *****1    - variable for the left subinterval
00584 !           *****2    - variable for the right subinterval
00585 !           last      - index for subdivision
00586 !           nres      - number of calls to the extrapolation routine
00587 !           numrl2    - number of elements currently in rlist2. if an
00588 !                       appropriate approximation to the compounded
00589 !                       integral has been obtained, it is put in
00590 !                       rlist2(numrl2) after numrl2 has been increased
00591 !                       by one.
00592 !           small     - length of the smallest interval considered up
00593 !                       to now, multiplied by 1.5
00594 !           erlarg    - sum of the errors over the intervals larger
00595 !                       than the smallest interval considered up to now
00596 !           extrap    - logical variable denoting that the routine
00597 !                       is attempting to perform extrapolation. i.e.
00598 !                       before subdividing the smallest interval we
00599 !                       try to decrease the value of erlarg.
00600 !           noext     - logical variable denoting that extrapolation
00601 !                       is no longer allowed (true-value)
00602 !
00603   implicit none
00604 
00605   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
00606 
00607   real abseps
00608   real abserr
00609   real alist(limit)
00610   real area
00611   real area1
00612   real area12
00613   real area2
00614   real a1
00615   real a2
00616   real blist(limit)
00617   real boun
00618   real bound
00619   real b1
00620   real b2
00621   real correc
00622   real defabs
00623   real defab1
00624   real defab2
00625   real dres
00626   real elist(limit)
00627   real epsabs
00628   real epsrel
00629   real erlarg
00630   real erlast
00631   real errbnd
00632   real errmax
00633   real error1
00634   real error2
00635   real erro12
00636   real errsum
00637   real ertest
00638   logical extrap
00639   real, external :: f
00640   integer id
00641   integer ier
00642   integer ierro
00643   integer inf
00644   integer iord(limit)
00645   integer iroff1
00646   integer iroff2
00647   integer iroff3
00648   integer jupbnd
00649   integer k
00650   integer ksgn
00651   integer ktmin
00652   integer last
00653   integer maxerr
00654   integer neval
00655   logical noext
00656   integer nres
00657   integer nrmax
00658   integer numrl2
00659   real resabs
00660   real reseps
00661   real result
00662   real res3la(3)
00663   real rlist(limit)
00664   real rlist2(52)
00665   real small
00666 !
00667 !  Test on validity of parameters.
00668 !
00669   ier = 0
00670   neval = 0
00671   last = 0
00672   result = 0.0e+00
00673   abserr = 0.0e+00
00674   alist(1) = 0.0e+00
00675   blist(1) = 1.0e+00
00676   rlist(1) = 0.0e+00
00677   elist(1) = 0.0e+00
00678   iord(1) = 0
00679 
00680   if ( epsabs < 0.0e+00 .and. epsrel < 0.0e+00 ) then
00681     ier = 6
00682     return
00683   end if
00684 !
00685 !  First approximation to the integral.
00686 !
00687 !  Determine the interval to be mapped onto (0,1).
00688 !  If INF = 2 the integral is computed as i = i1+i2, where
00689 !  i1 = integral of f over (-infinity,0),
00690 !  i2 = integral of f over (0,+infinity).
00691 !
00692   if ( inf == 2 ) then
00693     boun = 0.0e+00
00694   else
00695     boun = bound
00696   end if
00697 
00698   call qk15i ( f, boun, inf, 0.0e+00, 1.0e+00, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
00699 !
00700 !  Test on accuracy.
00701 !
00702   last = 1
00703   rlist(1) = result
00704   elist(1) = abserr
00705   iord(1) = 1
00706   dres = abs ( result )
00707   errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * dres )
00708 
00709   if ( abserr <= 100.0E+00 * epsilon ( defabs ) * defabs .and. &
00710     errbnd < abserr ) then
00711     ier = 2
00712   end if
00713 
00714   if ( limit == 1 ) then
00715     ier = 1
00716   end if
00717 
00718   if ( ier /= 0 .or. (abserr <= errbnd .and. abserr /= resabs ) .or. &
00719     abserr == 0.0e+00 ) go to 130
00720 !
00721 !  Initialization.
00722 !
00723   rlist2(1) = result
00724   errmax = abserr
00725   maxerr = 1
00726   area = result
00727   errsum = abserr
00728   abserr = huge ( abserr )
00729   nrmax = 1
00730   nres = 0
00731   ktmin = 0
00732   numrl2 = 2
00733   extrap = .false.
00734   noext = .false.
00735   ierro = 0
00736   iroff1 = 0
00737   iroff2 = 0
00738   iroff3 = 0
00739 
00740   if ( ( 1.0e+00 - 5.0e+01 * epsilon ( defabs ) ) * defabs <= dres ) then
00741     ksgn = 1
00742   else
00743     ksgn = -1
00744   end if
00745 
00746   do last = 2, limit
00747 !
00748 !  Bisect the subinterval with nrmax-th largest error estimate.
00749 !
00750     a1 = alist(maxerr)
00751     b1 = 5.0e-01 * ( alist(maxerr) + blist(maxerr) )
00752     a2 = b1
00753     b2 = blist(maxerr)
00754     erlast = errmax
00755     call qk15i ( f, boun, inf, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1 )
00756     call qk15i ( f, boun, inf, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
00757 !
00758 !  Improve previous approximations to integral and error
00759 !  and test for accuracy.
00760 !
00761     area12 = area1 + area2
00762     erro12 = error1 + error2
00763     errsum = errsum + erro12 - errmax
00764     area = area + area12 - rlist(maxerr)
00765 
00766     if ( defab1 /= error1 .and. defab2 /= error2 ) then
00767 
00768       if ( abs ( rlist(maxerr) - area12 ) <= 1.0e-05 * abs ( area12 ) &
00769         .and. 9.9e-01 * errmax <= erro12 ) then
00770 
00771         if ( extrap ) then
00772           iroff2 = iroff2 + 1
00773         end if
00774 
00775         if ( .not. extrap ) then
00776           iroff1 = iroff1 + 1
00777         end if
00778 
00779       end if
00780 
00781       if ( 10 < last .and. errmax < erro12 ) then
00782         iroff3 = iroff3 + 1
00783       end if
00784 
00785     end if
00786 
00787     rlist(maxerr) = area1
00788     rlist(last) = area2
00789     errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs ( area ) )
00790 !
00791 !  Test for roundoff error and eventually set error flag.
00792 !
00793     if ( 10 <= iroff1 + iroff2 .or. 20 <= iroff3 ) then
00794       ier = 2
00795     end if
00796 
00797     if ( 5 <= iroff2 ) then
00798       ierro = 3
00799     end if
00800 !
00801 !  Set error flag in the case that the number of subintervals equals LIMIT.
00802 !
00803     if ( last == limit ) then
00804       ier = 1
00805     end if
00806 !
00807 !  Set error flag in the case of bad integrand behavior
00808 !  at some points of the integration range.
00809 !
00810     if ( max ( abs(a1), abs(b2) ) <= (1.0e+00 + 1.0e+03 * epsilon ( a1 ) ) * &
00811     ( abs(a2) + 1.0e+03 * tiny ( a2 ) )) then
00812       ier = 4
00813     end if
00814 !
00815 !  Append the newly-created intervals to the list.
00816 !
00817     if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
00818       alist(last) = a2
00819       blist(maxerr) = b1
00820       blist(last) = b2
00821       elist(maxerr) = error1
00822       elist(last) = error2
00823     else
00824       alist(maxerr) = a2
00825       alist(last) = a1
00826       blist(last) = b1
00827       rlist(maxerr) = area2
00828       rlist(last) = area1
00829       elist(maxerr) = error2
00830       elist(last) = error1
00831     end if
00832 !
00833 !  Call QSORT to maintain the descending ordering
00834 !  in the list of error estimates and select the subinterval
00835 !  with NRMAX-th largest error estimate (to be bisected next).
00836 !
00837     call qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, errmax, elist, iord, nrmax )
00838 
00839     if ( errsum <= errbnd ) go to 115
00840 
00841     if ( ier /= 0 ) then
00842       exit
00843     end if
00844 
00845     if ( last == 2 ) then
00846       small = 3.75e-01
00847       erlarg = errsum
00848       ertest = errbnd
00849       rlist2(2) = area
00850       cycle
00851     end if
00852 
00853     if ( noext ) then
00854       cycle
00855     end if
00856 
00857     erlarg = erlarg - erlast
00858 
00859     if ( small < abs ( b1 - a1 ) ) then
00860       erlarg = erlarg + erro12
00861     end if
00862 !
00863 !  Test whether the interval to be bisected next is the
00864 !  smallest interval.
00865 !
00866     if ( .not. extrap ) then
00867 
00868       if ( small < abs ( blist(maxerr) - alist(maxerr) ) ) then
00869         cycle
00870       end if
00871 
00872       extrap = .true.
00873       nrmax = 2
00874 
00875     end if
00876 
00877     if ( ierro == 3 .or. erlarg <= ertest ) then
00878       go to 60
00879     end if
00880 !
00881 !  The smallest interval has the largest error.
00882 !  before bisecting decrease the sum of the errors over the
00883 !  larger intervals (erlarg) and perform extrapolation.
00884 !
00885     id = nrmax
00886     jupbnd = last
00887 
00888     if ( (2+limit/2) < last ) then
00889       jupbnd = limit + 3 - last
00890     end if
00891 
00892     do k = id, jupbnd
00893       maxerr = iord(nrmax)
00894       errmax = elist(maxerr)
00895       if ( small < abs ( blist(maxerr) - alist(maxerr) ) ) then
00896         go to 90
00897       end if
00898       nrmax = nrmax + 1
00899     end do
00900 !
00901 !  Extrapolate.
00902 !
00903 60  continue
00904 
00905     numrl2 = numrl2 + 1
00906     rlist2(numrl2) = area
00907     call qextr ( numrl2, rlist2, reseps, abseps, res3la, nres ) 
00908     ktmin = ktmin+1
00909 
00910     if ( 5 < ktmin .and. abserr < 1.0e-03 * errsum ) then
00911       ier = 5
00912     end if
00913 
00914     if ( abseps < abserr ) then
00915 
00916       ktmin = 0
00917       abserr = abseps
00918       result = reseps
00919       correc = erlarg
00920       ertest = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs(reseps) )
00921 
00922       if ( abserr <= ertest ) then
00923         exit
00924       end if
00925 
00926     end if
00927 !
00928 !  Prepare bisection of the smallest interval.
00929 !
00930     if ( numrl2 == 1 ) then
00931       noext = .true.
00932     end if
00933 
00934     if ( ier == 5 ) then
00935       exit
00936     end if
00937 
00938     maxerr = iord(1)
00939     errmax = elist(maxerr)
00940     nrmax = 1
00941     extrap = .false.
00942     small = small * 5.0e-01
00943     erlarg = errsum
00944 
00945 90  continue
00946 
00947   end do
00948 !
00949 !  Set final result and error estimate.
00950 !
00951   if ( abserr == huge ( abserr ) ) then
00952     go to 115
00953   end if
00954 
00955   if ( ( ier + ierro ) == 0 ) then
00956     go to 110
00957   end if
00958 
00959   if ( ierro == 3 ) then
00960     abserr = abserr + correc
00961   end if
00962 
00963   if ( ier == 0 ) then
00964     ier = 3
00965   end if
00966 
00967   if ( result /= 0.0e+00 .and. area /= 0.0e+00) then
00968     go to 105
00969   end if
00970 
00971   if ( errsum < abserr ) then
00972     go to 115
00973   end if
00974 
00975   if ( area == 0.0e+00 ) then
00976     go to 130
00977   end if
00978 
00979   go to 110
00980 
00981 105 continue
00982 
00983   if ( errsum / abs ( area ) < abserr / abs ( result )  ) then
00984     go to 115
00985   end if
00986 !
00987 !  Test on divergence
00988 !
00989 110 continue
00990 
00991   if ( ksgn == (-1) .and. &
00992   max ( abs(result), abs(area) ) <=  defabs * 1.0e-02) go to 130
00993 
00994   if ( 1.0e-02 > (result/area) .or. &
00995     (result/area) > 1.0e+02 .or. &
00996     errsum > abs(area)) then
00997     ier = 6
00998   end if
00999 
01000   go to 130
01001 !
01002 !  Compute global integral sum.
01003 !
01004   115 continue
01005 
01006   result = sum ( rlist(1:last) )
01007 
01008   abserr = errsum
01009   130 continue
01010 
01011   neval = 30 * last - 15
01012   if ( inf == 2 ) then
01013     neval = 2 * neval
01014   end if
01015 
01016   if ( 2 < ier ) then
01017     ier = ier - 1
01018   end if
01019 
01020   return
01021 end
01022 subroutine qagp ( f, a, b, npts2, points, epsabs, epsrel, result, abserr, &
01023   neval, ier )
01024 
01025 !*****************************************************************************80
01026 !
01027 !! QAGP computes a definite integral.
01028 !
01029 !  Discussion:
01030 !
01031 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral   
01032 !      I = integral of F over (A,B),
01033 !    hopefully satisfying
01034 !      || I - RESULT || <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * ||I|| ).
01035 !
01036 !    Interior break points of the integration interval,
01037 !    where local difficulties of the integrand may occur, such as
01038 !    singularities or discontinuities, are provided by the user.
01039 !
01040 !  Author:
01041 !
01042 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
01043 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
01044 !
01045 !  Reference:
01046 !
01047 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
01048 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
01049 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
01050 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
01051 !
01052 !  Parameters:
01053 !
01054 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
01055 !      function f ( x )
01056 !      real f
01057 !      real x
01058 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
01059 !
01060 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
01061 !
01062 !    Input, integer NPTS2, the number of user-supplied break points within 
01063 !    the integration range, plus 2.  NPTS2 must be at least 2.
01064 !
01065 !    Input/output, real POINTS(NPTS2), contains the user provided interior
01066 !    breakpoints in entries 1 through NPTS2-2.  If these points are not
01067 !    in ascending order on input, they will be sorted.
01068 !
01069 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
01070 !
01071 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
01072 !
01073 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
01074 !
01075 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
01076 !
01077 !    Output, integer IER, return flag.
01078 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
01079 !                             routine. it is assumed that the requested
01080 !                             accuracy has been achieved.
01081 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine.
01082 !                             the estimates for integral and error are
01083 !                             less reliable. it is assumed that the
01084 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
01085 !                     ier = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
01086 !                             has been achieved. one can allow more
01087 !                             subdivisions by increasing the data value
01088 !                             of limit in qagp(and taking the according
01089 !                             dimension adjustments into account).
01090 !                             however, if this yields no improvement
01091 !                             it is advised to analyze the integrand
01092 !                             in order to determine the integration
01093 !                             difficulties. if the position of a local
01094 !                             difficulty can be determined (i.e.
01095 !                             singularity, discontinuity within the
01096 !                             interval), it should be supplied to the
01097 !                             routine as an element of the vector
01098 !                             points. if necessary, an appropriate
01099 !                             special-purpose integrator must be used,
01100 !                             which is designed for handling the type
01101 !                             of difficulty involved.
01102 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is
01103 !                             detected, which prevents the requested
01104 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
01105 !                             the error may be under-estimated.
01106 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
01107 !                             at some points of the integration
01108 !                             interval.
01109 !                         = 4 the algorithm does not converge. roundoff
01110 !                             error is detected in the extrapolation
01111 !                             table. it is presumed that the requested
01112 !                             tolerance cannot be achieved, and that
01113 !                             the returned result is the best which
01114 !                             can be obtained.
01115 !                         = 5 the integral is probably divergent, or
01116 !                             slowly convergent. it must be noted that
01117 !                             divergence can occur with any other value
01118 !                             of ier > 0.
01119 !                         = 6 the input is invalid because
01120 !                             npts2 < 2 or
01121 !                             break points are specified outside
01122 !                             the integration range or
01123 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
01124 !                             or limit < npts2.
01125 !                             result, abserr, neval are set to zero.
01126 !
01127 !  Local parameters:
01128 !
01129 !            the dimension of rlist2 is determined by the value of
01130 !            limexp in QEXTR (rlist2 should be of dimension
01131 !            (limexp+2) at least).
01132 !
01133 !           alist     - list of left end points of all subintervals
01134 !                       considered up to now
01135 !           blist     - list of right end points of all subintervals
01136 !                       considered up to now
01137 !           rlist(i)  - approximation to the integral over
01138 !                       (alist(i),blist(i))
01139 !           rlist2    - array of dimension at least limexp+2
01140 !                       containing the part of the epsilon table which
01141 !                       is still needed for further computations
01142 !           elist(i)  - error estimate applying to rlist(i)
01143 !           maxerr    - pointer to the interval with largest error
01144 !                       estimate
01145 !           errmax    - elist(maxerr)
01146 !           erlast    - error on the interval currently subdivided
01147 !                       (before that subdivision has taken place)
01148 !           area      - sum of the integrals over the subintervals
01149 !           errsum    - sum of the errors over the subintervals
01150 !           errbnd    - requested accuracy max(epsabs,epsrel*
01151 !                       abs(result))
01152 !           *****1    - variable for the left subinterval
01153 !           *****2    - variable for the right subinterval
01154 !           last      - index for subdivision
01155 !           nres      - number of calls to the extrapolation routine
01156 !           numrl2    - number of elements in rlist2. if an appropriate
01157 !                       approximation to the compounded integral has
01158 !                       obtained, it is put in rlist2(numrl2) after
01159 !                       numrl2 has been increased by one.
01160 !           erlarg    - sum of the errors over the intervals larger
01161 !                       than the smallest interval considered up to now
01162 !           extrap    - logical variable denoting that the routine
01163 !                       is attempting to perform extrapolation. i.e.
01164 !                       before subdividing the smallest interval we
01165 !                       try to decrease the value of erlarg.
01166 !           noext     - logical variable denoting that extrapolation is
01167 !                       no longer allowed (true-value)
01168 !
01169   implicit none
01170 
01171   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
01172 
01173   real a
01174   real abseps
01175   real abserr
01176   real alist(limit)
01177   real area
01178   real area1
01179   real area12
01180   real area2
01181   real a1
01182   real a2
01183   real b
01184   real blist(limit)
01185   real b1
01186   real b2
01187   real correc
01188   real defabs
01189   real defab1
01190   real defab2
01191   real dres
01192   real elist(limit)
01193   real epsabs
01194   real epsrel
01195   real erlarg
01196   real erlast
01197   real errbnd
01198   real errmax
01199   real error1
01200   real erro12
01201   real error2
01202   real errsum
01203   real ertest
01204   logical extrap
01205   real, external :: f
01206   integer i
01207   integer id
01208   integer ier
01209   integer ierro
01210   integer ind1
01211   integer ind2
01212   integer iord(limit)
01213   integer iroff1
01214   integer iroff2
01215   integer iroff3
01216   integer j
01217   integer jlow
01218   integer jupbnd
01219   integer k
01220   integer ksgn
01221   integer ktmin
01222   integer last
01223   integer levcur
01224   integer level(limit)
01225   integer levmax
01226   integer maxerr
01227   integer ndin(40)
01228   integer neval
01229   integer nint
01230   logical noext
01231   integer npts
01232   integer npts2
01233   integer nres
01234   integer nrmax
01235   integer numrl2
01236   real points(40)
01237   real pts(40)
01238   real resa
01239   real resabs
01240   real reseps
01241   real result
01242   real res3la(3)
01243   real rlist(limit)
01244   real rlist2(52)
01245   real sign
01246   real temp
01247 !
01248 !  Test on validity of parameters.
01249 !
01250   ier = 0
01251   neval = 0
01252   last = 0
01253   result = 0.0e+00
01254   abserr = 0.0e+00
01255   alist(1) = a
01256   blist(1) = b
01257   rlist(1) = 0.0e+00
01258   elist(1) = 0.0e+00
01259   iord(1) = 0
01260   level(1) = 0
01261   npts = npts2 - 2
01262 
01263   if ( npts2 < 2 ) then
01264     ier = 6
01265     return
01266   else if ( limit <= npts .or. ( epsabs < 0.0e+00 .and. &
01267     epsrel < 0.0e+00) ) then
01268     ier = 6
01269     return
01270   end if
01271 !
01272 !  If any break points are provided, sort them into an
01273 !  ascending sequence.
01274 !
01275   if ( b < a ) then
01276     sign = -1.0e+00
01277   else
01278     sign = +1.0E+00
01279   end if
01280 
01281   pts(1) = min ( a, b )
01282 
01283   do i = 1, npts
01284     pts(i+1) = points(i)
01285   end do
01286 
01287   pts(npts+2) = max ( a, b )
01288   nint = npts+1
01289   a1 = pts(1)
01290 
01291   if ( npts /= 0 ) then
01292 
01293     do i = 1, nint
01294       do j = i+1, nint+1
01295         if ( pts(j) < pts(i) ) then
01296           temp   = pts(i)
01297           pts(i) = pts(j)
01298           pts(j) = temp
01299         end if
01300       end do
01301     end do
01302 
01303     if ( pts(1) /= min ( a, b ) .or. pts(nint+1) /= max ( a, b ) ) then
01304       ier = 6
01305       return
01306     end if
01307 
01308   end if
01309 !
01310 !  Compute first integral and error approximations.
01311 !
01312   resabs = 0.0e+00
01313 
01314   do i = 1, nint
01315 
01316     b1 = pts(i+1)
01317     call qk21 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, defabs, resa )
01318     abserr = abserr + error1
01319     result = result + area1
01320     ndin(i) = 0
01321 
01322     if ( error1 == resa .and. error1 /= 0.0e+00 ) then
01323       ndin(i) = 1
01324     end if
01325 
01326     resabs = resabs + defabs
01327     level(i) = 0
01328     elist(i) = error1
01329     alist(i) = a1
01330     blist(i) = b1
01331     rlist(i) = area1
01332     iord(i) = i
01333     a1 = b1
01334 
01335   end do
01336 
01337   errsum = 0.0e+00
01338 
01339   do i = 1, nint
01340     if ( ndin(i) == 1 ) then
01341       elist(i) = abserr
01342     end if
01343     errsum = errsum + elist(i)
01344   end do
01345 !
01346 !  Test on accuracy.
01347 !
01348   last = nint
01349   neval = 21 * nint
01350   dres = abs ( result )
01351   errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * dres )
01352 
01353   if ( abserr <= 1.0e+02 * epsilon ( resabs ) * resabs .and. &
01354     abserr > errbnd ) then
01355     ier = 2
01356   end if
01357 
01358   if ( nint /= 1 ) then
01359 
01360     do i = 1, npts
01361 
01362       jlow = i+1
01363       ind1 = iord(i)
01364 
01365       do j = jlow, nint
01366         ind2 = iord(j)
01367         if ( elist(ind1) <= elist(ind2) ) then
01368           ind1 = ind2
01369           k = j
01370         end if
01371       end do
01372 
01373       if ( ind1 /= iord(i) ) then
01374         iord(k) = iord(i)
01375         iord(i) = ind1
01376       end if
01377 
01378     end do
01379 
01380     if ( limit < npts2 ) then
01381       ier = 1
01382     end if
01383 
01384   end if
01385 
01386   if ( ier /= 0 .or. abserr <= errbnd ) then
01387     return
01388   end if
01389 !
01390 !  Initialization
01391 !
01392   rlist2(1) = result
01393   maxerr = iord(1)
01394   errmax = elist(maxerr)
01395   area = result
01396   nrmax = 1
01397   nres = 0
01398   numrl2 = 1
01399   ktmin = 0
01400   extrap = .false.
01401   noext = .false.
01402   erlarg = errsum
01403   ertest = errbnd
01404   levmax = 1
01405   iroff1 = 0
01406   iroff2 = 0
01407   iroff3 = 0
01408   ierro = 0
01409   abserr = huge ( abserr )
01410 
01411   if ( dres >= ( 1.0e+00 - 0.5E+00 * epsilon ( resabs ) ) * resabs ) then
01412     ksgn = 1
01413   else
01414     ksgn = -1
01415   end if
01416 
01417   do last = npts2, limit
01418 !
01419 !  Bisect the subinterval with the NRMAX-th largest error estimate.
01420 !
01421     levcur = level(maxerr) + 1
01422     a1 = alist(maxerr)
01423     b1 = 0.5E+00 * ( alist(maxerr) + blist(maxerr) )
01424     a2 = b1
01425     b2 = blist(maxerr)
01426     erlast = errmax
01427     call qk21 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resa, defab1 )
01428     call qk21 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resa, defab2 )
01429 !
01430 !  Improve previous approximations to integral and error
01431 !  and test for accuracy.
01432 !
01433     neval = neval + 42
01434     area12 = area1 + area2
01435     erro12 = error1 + error2
01436     errsum = errsum + erro12 -errmax
01437     area = area + area12 - rlist(maxerr)
01438 
01439     if ( defab1 /= error1 .and. defab2 /= error2 ) then
01440 
01441       if ( abs ( rlist ( maxerr ) - area12 ) <= 1.0e-05 * abs(area12) .and. &
01442         erro12 >= 9.9e-01 * errmax ) then
01443 
01444         if ( extrap ) then
01445           iroff2 = iroff2+1
01446         else
01447           iroff1 = iroff1+1
01448         end if
01449 
01450       end if
01451 
01452       if ( last > 10 .and. erro12 > errmax ) then
01453         iroff3 = iroff3 + 1
01454       end if
01455 
01456     end if
01457 
01458     level(maxerr) = levcur
01459     level(last) = levcur
01460     rlist(maxerr) = area1
01461     rlist(last) = area2
01462     errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs ( area ) )
01463 !
01464 !  Test for roundoff error and eventually set error flag.
01465 !
01466     if ( 10 <= iroff1 + iroff2 .or. 20 <= iroff3 ) then
01467       ier = 2
01468     end if
01469 
01470     if ( 5 <= iroff2 ) then
01471       ierro = 3
01472     end if
01473 !
01474 !  Set error flag in the case that the number of subintervals
01475 !  equals limit.
01476 !
01477     if ( last == limit ) then
01478       ier = 1
01479     end if
01480 !
01481 !  Set error flag in the case of bad integrand behavior
01482 !  at a point of the integration range
01483 !
01484     if ( max ( abs(a1), abs(b2)) <= ( 1.0e+00 + 1.0e+03 * epsilon ( a1 ) )* &
01485     ( abs ( a2 ) + 1.0e+03 * tiny ( a2 ) ) ) then
01486       ier = 4
01487     end if
01488 !
01489 !  Append the newly-created intervals to the list.
01490 !
01491     if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
01492       alist(last) = a2
01493       blist(maxerr) = b1
01494       blist(last) = b2
01495       elist(maxerr) = error1
01496       elist(last) = error2
01497     else
01498       alist(maxerr) = a2
01499       alist(last) = a1
01500       blist(last) = b1
01501       rlist(maxerr) = area2
01502       rlist(last) = area1
01503       elist(maxerr) = error2
01504       elist(last) = error1
01505     end if
01506 !
01507 !  Call QSORT to maintain the descending ordering
01508 !  in the list of error estimates and select the subinterval
01509 !  with nrmax-th largest error estimate (to be bisected next).
01510 !
01511     call qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, errmax, elist, iord, nrmax )
01512 
01513     if ( errsum <= errbnd ) then
01514       go to 190
01515     end if
01516 
01517     if ( ier /= 0 ) then
01518       exit
01519     end if
01520 
01521     if ( noext ) then
01522       cycle
01523     end if
01524 
01525     erlarg = erlarg - erlast
01526 
01527     if ( levcur+1 <= levmax ) then
01528       erlarg = erlarg + erro12
01529     end if
01530 !
01531 !  Test whether the interval to be bisected next is the
01532 !  smallest interval.
01533 !
01534     if ( .not. extrap ) then
01535 
01536       if ( level(maxerr)+1 <= levmax ) then
01537         cycle
01538       end if
01539 
01540       extrap = .true.
01541       nrmax = 2
01542 
01543     end if
01544 !
01545 !  The smallest interval has the largest error.
01546 !  Before bisecting decrease the sum of the errors over the
01547 !  larger intervals (erlarg) and perform extrapolation.
01548 !
01549     if ( ierro /= 3 .and. erlarg > ertest ) then
01550 
01551       id = nrmax
01552       jupbnd = last
01553       if ( last > (2+limit/2) ) then
01554         jupbnd = limit+3-last
01555       end if
01556 
01557       do k = id, jupbnd
01558         maxerr = iord(nrmax)
01559         errmax = elist(maxerr)
01560         if ( level(maxerr)+1 <= levmax ) then
01561           go to 160
01562         end if
01563         nrmax = nrmax + 1
01564       end do
01565 
01566     end if
01567 !
01568 !  Perform extrapolation.
01569 !
01570     numrl2 = numrl2 + 1
01571     rlist2(numrl2) = area
01572 
01573     if ( numrl2 <= 2 ) then
01574       go to 155
01575     end if
01576 
01577     call qextr ( numrl2, rlist2, reseps, abseps, res3la, nres )
01578     ktmin = ktmin+1
01579 
01580     if ( 5 < ktmin .and. abserr < 1.0e-03 * errsum ) then
01581       ier = 5
01582     end if
01583 
01584     if ( abseps < abserr ) then
01585 
01586       ktmin = 0
01587       abserr = abseps
01588       result = reseps
01589       correc = erlarg
01590       ertest = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs(reseps) )
01591 
01592       if ( abserr < ertest ) then
01593         exit
01594       end if
01595 
01596     end if
01597 !
01598 !  Prepare bisection of the smallest interval.
01599 !
01600     if ( numrl2 == 1 ) then
01601       noext = .true.
01602     end if
01603 
01604     if ( 5 <= ier ) then
01605       exit
01606     end if
01607 
01608 155 continue
01609 
01610     maxerr = iord(1)
01611     errmax = elist(maxerr)
01612     nrmax = 1
01613     extrap = .false.
01614     levmax = levmax + 1
01615     erlarg = errsum
01616 
01617 160 continue
01618 
01619   end do
01620 !
01621 !  Set the final result.
01622 !
01623   if ( abserr == huge ( abserr ) ) then
01624     go to 190
01625   end if
01626 
01627   if ( ( ier + ierro ) == 0 ) then
01628     go to 180
01629   end if
01630 
01631   if ( ierro == 3 ) then
01632     abserr = abserr + correc
01633   end if
01634 
01635   if ( ier == 0 ) then
01636     ier = 3
01637   end if
01638 
01639   if ( result /= 0.0e+00 .and. area /= 0.0e+00 ) then
01640     go to 175
01641   end if
01642 
01643   if ( errsum < abserr ) then
01644     go to 190
01645   end if
01646 
01647   if ( area == 0.0e+00 ) then
01648     go to 210
01649   end if
01650 
01651   go to 180
01652 
01653 175 continue
01654 
01655   if ( abserr / abs(result) > errsum / abs(area) ) then
01656     go to 190
01657   end if
01658 !
01659 !  Test on divergence.
01660 !
01661   180 continue
01662 
01663   if ( ksgn == (-1) .and. max ( abs(result),abs(area)) <=  &
01664     resabs*1.0e-02 ) go to 210
01665 
01666   if ( 1.0e-02 > (result/area) .or. (result/area) > 1.0e+02 .or. &
01667     errsum > abs(area) ) then
01668     ier = 6
01669   end if
01670 
01671   go to 210
01672 !
01673 !  Compute global integral sum.
01674 !
01675 190 continue
01676 
01677   result = sum ( rlist(1:last) )
01678 
01679   abserr = errsum
01680 
01681 210 continue
01682 
01683   if ( 2 < ier ) then
01684     ier = ier - 1
01685   end if
01686 
01687   result = result * sign
01688 
01689   return
01690 end
01691 subroutine qags ( f, a, b, epsabs, epsrel, result, abserr, neval, ier )
01692 
01693 !*****************************************************************************80
01694 !
01695 !! QAGS estimates the integral of a function.
01696 !
01697 !  Discussion:
01698 !
01699 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral   
01700 !      I = integral of F over (A,B),
01701 !    hopefully satisfying
01702 !      || I - RESULT || <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * ||I|| ).
01703 !
01704 !  Author:
01705 !
01706 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
01707 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
01708 !
01709 !  Reference:
01710 !
01711 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
01712 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
01713 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
01714 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
01715 !
01716 !  Parameters:
01717 !
01718 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
01719 !      function f ( x )
01720 !      real f
01721 !      real x
01722 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
01723 !
01724 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
01725 !
01726 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
01727 !
01728 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
01729 !
01730 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
01731 !
01732 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
01733 !
01734 !    Output, integer IER, error flag.
01735 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
01736 !                             routine. it is assumed that the requested
01737 !                             accuracy has been achieved.
01738 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine
01739 !                             the estimates for integral and error are
01740 !                             less reliable. it is assumed that the
01741 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
01742 !                         = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
01743 !                             has been achieved. one can allow more sub-
01744 !                             divisions by increasing the data value of
01745 !                             limit in qags (and taking the according
01746 !                             dimension adjustments into account).
01747 !                             however, if this yields no improvement
01748 !                             it is advised to analyze the integrand
01749 !                             in order to determine the integration
01750 !                             difficulties. if the position of a
01751 !                             local difficulty can be determined (e.g.
01752 !                             singularity, discontinuity within the
01753 !                             interval) one will probably gain from
01754 !                             splitting up the interval at this point
01755 !                             and calling the integrator on the sub-
01756 !                             ranges. if possible, an appropriate
01757 !                             special-purpose integrator should be used,
01758 !                             which is designed for handling the type
01759 !                             of difficulty involved.
01760 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is detec-
01761 !                             ted, which prevents the requested
01762 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
01763 !                             the error may be under-estimated.
01764 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
01765 !                             at some  points of the integration
01766 !                             interval.
01767 !                         = 4 the algorithm does not converge. roundoff
01768 !                             error is detected in the extrapolation
01769 !                             table. it is presumed that the requested
01770 !                             tolerance cannot be achieved, and that the
01771 !                             returned result is the best which can be
01772 !                             obtained.
01773 !                         = 5 the integral is probably divergent, or
01774 !                             slowly convergent. it must be noted that
01775 !                             divergence can occur with any other value
01776 !                             of ier.
01777 !                         = 6 the input is invalid, because
01778 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
01779 !                             result, abserr and neval are set to zero.
01780 !
01781 !  Local Parameters:
01782 !
01783 !           alist     - list of left end points of all subintervals
01784 !                       considered up to now
01785 !           blist     - list of right end points of all subintervals
01786 !                       considered up to now
01787 !           rlist(i)  - approximation to the integral over
01788 !                       (alist(i),blist(i))
01789 !           rlist2    - array of dimension at least limexp+2 containing
01790 !                       the part of the epsilon table which is still
01791 !                       needed for further computations
01792 !           elist(i)  - error estimate applying to rlist(i)
01793 !           maxerr    - pointer to the interval with largest error
01794 !                       estimate
01795 !           errmax    - elist(maxerr)
01796 !           erlast    - error on the interval currently subdivided
01797 !                       (before that subdivision has taken place)
01798 !           area      - sum of the integrals over the subintervals
01799 !           errsum    - sum of the errors over the subintervals
01800 !           errbnd    - requested accuracy max(epsabs,epsrel*
01801 !                       abs(result))
01802 !           *****1    - variable for the left interval
01803 !           *****2    - variable for the right interval
01804 !           last      - index for subdivision
01805 !           nres      - number of calls to the extrapolation routine
01806 !           numrl2    - number of elements currently in rlist2. if an
01807 !                       appropriate approximation to the compounded
01808 !                       integral has been obtained it is put in
01809 !                       rlist2(numrl2) after numrl2 has been increased
01810 !                       by one.
01811 !           small     - length of the smallest interval considered
01812 !                       up to now, multiplied by 1.5
01813 !           erlarg    - sum of the errors over the intervals larger
01814 !                       than the smallest interval considered up to now
01815 !           extrap    - logical variable denoting that the routine is
01816 !                       attempting to perform extrapolation i.e. before
01817 !                       subdividing the smallest interval we try to
01818 !                       decrease the value of erlarg.
01819 !           noext     - logical variable denoting that extrapolation
01820 !                       is no longer allowed (true value)
01821 !
01822   implicit none
01823 
01824   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
01825 
01826   real a
01827   real abseps
01828   real abserr
01829   real alist(limit)
01830   real area
01831   real area1
01832   real area12
01833   real area2
01834   real a1
01835   real a2
01836   real b
01837   real blist(limit)
01838   real b1
01839   real b2
01840   real correc
01841   real defabs
01842   real defab1
01843   real defab2
01844   real dres
01845   real elist(limit)
01846   real epsabs
01847   real epsrel
01848   real erlarg
01849   real erlast
01850   real errbnd
01851   real errmax
01852   real error1
01853   real error2
01854   real erro12
01855   real errsum
01856   real ertest
01857   logical extrap
01858   real, external :: f
01859   integer id
01860   integer ier
01861   integer ierro
01862   integer iord(limit)
01863   integer iroff1
01864   integer iroff2
01865   integer iroff3
01866   integer jupbnd
01867   integer k
01868   integer ksgn
01869   integer ktmin
01870   integer last
01871   logical noext
01872   integer maxerr
01873   integer neval
01874   integer nres
01875   integer nrmax
01876   integer numrl2
01877   real resabs
01878   real reseps
01879   real result
01880   real res3la(3)
01881   real rlist(limit)
01882   real rlist2(52)
01883   real small
01884 !
01885 !  The dimension of rlist2 is determined by the value of
01886 !  limexp in QEXTR (rlist2 should be of dimension
01887 !  (limexp+2) at least).
01888 !
01889 !  Test on validity of parameters.
01890 !
01891   ier = 0
01892   neval = 0
01893   last = 0
01894   result = 0.0e+00
01895   abserr = 0.0e+00
01896   alist(1) = a
01897   blist(1) = b
01898   rlist(1) = 0.0e+00
01899   elist(1) = 0.0e+00
01900 
01901   if ( epsabs < 0.0e+00 .and. epsrel < 0.0e+00 ) then
01902     ier = 6
01903     return
01904   end if
01905 !
01906 !  First approximation to the integral.
01907 !
01908   ierro = 0
01909   call qk21 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, defabs, resabs )
01910 !
01911 !  Test on accuracy.
01912 !
01913   dres = abs ( result )
01914   errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * dres )
01915   last = 1
01916   rlist(1) = result
01917   elist(1) = abserr
01918   iord(1) = 1
01919 
01920   if ( abserr <= 1.0e+02 * epsilon ( defabs ) * defabs .and. &
01921     abserr > errbnd ) then
01922     ier = 2
01923   end if
01924 
01925   if ( limit == 1 ) then
01926     ier = 1
01927   end if
01928 
01929   if ( ier /= 0 .or. (abserr <= errbnd .and. abserr /= resabs ) .or. &
01930     abserr == 0.0e+00 ) go to 140
01931 !
01932 !  Initialization.
01933 !
01934   rlist2(1) = result
01935   errmax = abserr
01936   maxerr = 1
01937   area = result
01938   errsum = abserr
01939   abserr = huge ( abserr )
01940   nrmax = 1
01941   nres = 0
01942   numrl2 = 2
01943   ktmin = 0
01944   extrap = .false.
01945   noext = .false.
01946   iroff1 = 0
01947   iroff2 = 0
01948   iroff3 = 0
01949 
01950   if ( dres >= (1.0e+00-5.0e+01* epsilon ( defabs ) ) * defabs ) then
01951     ksgn = 1
01952   else
01953     ksgn = -1
01954   end if
01955 
01956   do last = 2, limit
01957 !
01958 !  Bisect the subinterval with the nrmax-th largest error estimate.
01959 !
01960     a1 = alist(maxerr)
01961     b1 = 5.0e-01 * ( alist(maxerr) + blist(maxerr) )
01962     a2 = b1
01963     b2 = blist(maxerr)
01964     erlast = errmax
01965     call qk21 ( f, a1, b1, area1, error1, resabs, defab1 )
01966     call qk21 ( f, a2, b2, area2, error2, resabs, defab2 )
01967 !
01968 !  Improve previous approximations to integral and error
01969 !  and test for accuracy.
01970 !
01971     area12 = area1+area2
01972     erro12 = error1+error2
01973     errsum = errsum+erro12-errmax
01974     area = area+area12-rlist(maxerr)
01975 
01976     if ( defab1 == error1 .or. defab2 == error2 ) go to 15
01977 
01978     if ( abs ( rlist(maxerr) - area12) > 1.0e-05 * abs(area12) &
01979       .or. erro12 < 9.9e-01 * errmax ) go to 10
01980 
01981     if ( extrap ) then
01982       iroff2 = iroff2+1
01983     else
01984       iroff1 = iroff1+1
01985     end if
01986 
01987 10  continue
01988 
01989     if ( last > 10 .and. erro12 > errmax ) then
01990       iroff3 = iroff3+1
01991     end if
01992 
01993 15  continue
01994 
01995     rlist(maxerr) = area1
01996     rlist(last) = area2
01997     errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel*abs(area) )
01998 !
01999 !  Test for roundoff error and eventually set error flag.
02000 !
02001     if ( iroff1+iroff2 >= 10 .or. iroff3 >= 20 ) then
02002       ier = 2
02003     end if
02004 
02005     if ( iroff2 >= 5 ) then
02006       ierro = 3
02007     end if
02008 !
02009 !  Set error flag in the case that the number of subintervals
02010 !  equals limit.
02011 !
02012     if ( last == limit ) then
02013       ier = 1
02014     end if
02015 !
02016 !  Set error flag in the case of bad integrand behavior
02017 !  at a point of the integration range.
02018 !
02019     if ( max ( abs(a1),abs(b2)) <= (1.0e+00+1.0e+03* epsilon ( a1 ) )* &
02020       (abs(a2)+1.0e+03* tiny ( a2 ) ) ) then
02021       ier = 4
02022     end if
02023 !
02024 !  Append the newly-created intervals to the list.
02025 !
02026     if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
02027       alist(last) = a2
02028       blist(maxerr) = b1
02029       blist(last) = b2
02030       elist(maxerr) = error1
02031       elist(last) = error2
02032     else
02033       alist(maxerr) = a2
02034       alist(last) = a1
02035       blist(last) = b1
02036       rlist(maxerr) = area2
02037       rlist(last) = area1
02038       elist(maxerr) = error2
02039       elist(last) = error1
02040     end if
02041 !
02042 !  Call QSORT to maintain the descending ordering
02043 !  in the list of error estimates and select the subinterval
02044 !  with nrmax-th largest error estimate (to be bisected next).
02045 !
02046     call qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, errmax, elist, iord, nrmax )
02047 
02048     if ( errsum <= errbnd ) go to 115
02049 
02050     if ( ier /= 0 ) then
02051       exit
02052     end if
02053 
02054     if ( last == 2 ) go to 80
02055     if ( noext ) go to 90
02056 
02057     erlarg = erlarg-erlast
02058 
02059     if ( abs(b1-a1) > small ) then
02060       erlarg = erlarg+erro12
02061     end if
02062 !
02063 !  Test whether the interval to be bisected next is the
02064 !  smallest interval.
02065 !
02066     if ( .not. extrap ) then
02067       if ( abs(blist(maxerr)-alist(maxerr)) > small ) go to 90
02068       extrap = .true.
02069       nrmax = 2
02070     end if
02071 
02072 !40  continue
02073 !
02074 !  The smallest interval has the largest error.
02075 !  Before bisecting decrease the sum of the errors over the
02076 !  larger intervals (erlarg) and perform extrapolation.
02077 !
02078     if ( ierro /= 3 .and. erlarg > ertest ) then
02079 
02080       id = nrmax
02081       jupbnd = last
02082 
02083       if ( last > (2+limit/2) ) then
02084         jupbnd = limit+3-last
02085       end if
02086 
02087       do k = id, jupbnd
02088         maxerr = iord(nrmax)
02089         errmax = elist(maxerr)
02090         if ( abs(blist(maxerr)-alist(maxerr)) > small ) then
02091           go to 90
02092         end if
02093         nrmax = nrmax+1
02094       end do
02095 
02096     end if
02097 !
02098 !  Perform extrapolation.
02099 !
02100 !60  continue
02101 
02102     numrl2 = numrl2+1
02103     rlist2(numrl2) = area
02104     call qextr ( numrl2, rlist2, reseps, abseps, res3la, nres )
02105     ktmin = ktmin+1
02106 
02107     if ( ktmin > 5 .and. abserr < 1.0e-03 * errsum ) then
02108       ier = 5
02109     end if
02110 
02111     if ( abseps < abserr ) then
02112 
02113       ktmin = 0
02114       abserr = abseps
02115       result = reseps
02116       correc = erlarg
02117       ertest = max ( epsabs,epsrel*abs(reseps))
02118 
02119       if ( abserr <= ertest ) then
02120         exit
02121       end if
02122 
02123     end if
02124 !
02125 !  Prepare bisection of the smallest interval.
02126 !
02127     if ( numrl2 == 1 ) then
02128       noext = .true.
02129     end if
02130 
02131     if ( ier == 5 ) then
02132       exit
02133     end if
02134 
02135     maxerr = iord(1)
02136     errmax = elist(maxerr)
02137     nrmax = 1
02138     extrap = .false.
02139     small = small * 5.0e-01
02140     erlarg = errsum
02141     go to 90
02142 
02143 80  continue
02144 
02145     small = abs ( b - a ) * 3.75e-01
02146     erlarg = errsum
02147     ertest = errbnd
02148     rlist2(2) = area
02149 
02150 90  continue
02151 
02152   end do
02153 !
02154 !  Set final result and error estimate.
02155 !
02156   if ( abserr == huge ( abserr ) ) then
02157     go to 115
02158   end if
02159 
02160   if ( ier + ierro == 0 ) then
02161     go to 110
02162   end if
02163 
02164   if ( ierro == 3 ) then
02165     abserr = abserr + correc
02166   end if
02167 
02168   if ( ier == 0 ) then
02169     ier = 3
02170   end if
02171 
02172   if ( result /= 0.0e+00.and.area /= 0.0e+00 ) then
02173     go to 105
02174   end if
02175 
02176   if ( abserr > errsum ) go to 115
02177   if ( area == 0.0e+00 ) go to 130
02178   go to 110
02179 
02180 105 continue
02181 
02182   if ( abserr/abs(result) > errsum/abs(area) ) go to 115
02183 !
02184 !  Test on divergence.
02185 !
02186 110 continue
02187 
02188   if ( ksgn == (-1).and.max ( abs(result),abs(area)) <=  &
02189    defabs*1.0e-02 ) go to 130
02190 
02191   if ( 1.0e-02 > (result/area) .or. (result/area) > 1.0e+02 &
02192    .or. errsum > abs(area) ) then
02193     ier = 6
02194   end if
02195 
02196   go to 130
02197 !
02198 !  Compute global integral sum.
02199 !
02200 115 continue
02201 
02202   result = sum ( rlist(1:last) )
02203 
02204   abserr = errsum
02205 
02206 130 continue
02207  
02208   if ( 2 < ier ) then
02209     ier = ier - 1
02210   end if
02211 
02212 140 continue
02213 
02214   neval = 42*last-21
02215 
02216   return
02217 end
02218 subroutine qawc ( f, a, b, c, epsabs, epsrel, result, abserr, neval, ier )
02219 
02220 !*****************************************************************************80
02221 !
02222 !! QAWC computes a Cauchy principal value.
02223 !
02224 !  Discussion:
02225 !
02226 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a Cauchy principal
02227 !    value 
02228 !      I = integral of F*W over (A,B),
02229 !    with
02230 !      W(X) = 1 / (X-C),
02231 !    with C distinct from A and B, hopefully satisfying
02232 !      || I - RESULT || <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * ||I|| ).
02233 !
02234 !  Author:
02235 !
02236 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02237 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
02238 !
02239 !  Reference:
02240 !
02241 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02242 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
02243 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
02244 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
02245 !
02246 !  Parameters:
02247 !
02248 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
02249 !      function f ( x )
02250 !      real f
02251 !      real x
02252 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
02253 !
02254 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
02255 !
02256 !    Input, real C, a parameter in the weight function, which must
02257 !    not be equal to A or B.
02258 !
02259 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
02260 !
02261 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
02262 !
02263 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
02264 !
02265 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
02266 !
02267 !            ier    - integer
02268 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
02269 !                             routine. it is assumed that the requested
02270 !                             accuracy has been achieved.
02271 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine
02272 !                             the estimates for integral and error are
02273 !                             less reliable. it is assumed that the
02274 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
02275 !                     ier = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
02276 !                             has been achieved. one can allow more sub-
02277 !                             divisions by increasing the data value of
02278 !                             limit in qawc (and taking the according
02279 !                             dimension adjustments into account).
02280 !                             however, if this yields no improvement it
02281 !                             is advised to analyze the integrand in
02282 !                             order to determine the integration
02283 !                             difficulties. if the position of a local
02284 !                             difficulty can be determined (e.g.
02285 !                             singularity, discontinuity within the
02286 !                             interval one will probably gain from
02287 !                             splitting up the interval at this point
02288 !                             and calling appropriate integrators on the
02289 !                             subranges.
02290 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is detec-
02291 !                             ted, which prevents the requested
02292 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
02293 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
02294 !                             at some points of the integration
02295 !                             interval.
02296 !                         = 6 the input is invalid, because
02297 !                             c = a or c = b or
02298 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
02299 !                             result, abserr, neval are set to zero.
02300 !
02301 !  Local parameters:
02302 !
02303 !    LIMIT is the maximum number of subintervals allowed in the
02304 !    subdivision process of qawce. take care that limit >= 1.
02305 !
02306   implicit none
02307 
02308   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
02309 
02310   real a
02311   real abserr
02312   real alist(limit)
02313   real b
02314   real blist(limit)
02315   real elist(limit)
02316   real c
02317   real epsabs
02318   real epsrel
02319   real, external :: f
02320   integer ier
02321   integer iord(limit)
02322   integer last
02323   integer neval
02324   real result
02325   real rlist(limit)
02326 
02327   call qawce ( f, a, b, c, epsabs, epsrel, limit, result, abserr, neval, ier, &
02328     alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, last )
02329 
02330   return
02331 end
02332 subroutine qawce ( f, a, b, c, epsabs, epsrel, limit, result, abserr, neval, &
02333   ier, alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, last )
02334 
02335 !*****************************************************************************80
02336 !
02337 !! QAWCE computes a Cauchy principal value.
02338 !
02339 !  Discussion:
02340 !
02341 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a Cauchy principal
02342 !    value   
02343 !      I = integral of F*W over (A,B),
02344 !    with
02345 !      W(X) = 1 / ( X - C ),
02346 !    with C distinct from A and B, hopefully satisfying
02347 !      | I - RESULT | <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * |I| ).
02348 !
02349 !  Author:
02350 !
02351 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02352 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
02353 !
02354 !  Reference:
02355 !
02356 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02357 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
02358 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
02359 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
02360 !
02361 !  Parameters:
02362 !
02363 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
02364 !      function f ( x )
02365 !      real f
02366 !      real x
02367 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
02368 !
02369 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
02370 !
02371 !    Input, real C, a parameter in the weight function, which cannot be
02372 !    equal to A or B.
02373 !
02374 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
02375 !
02376 !    Input, integer LIMIT, the upper bound on the number of subintervals that
02377 !    will be used in the partition of [A,B].  LIMIT is typically 500.
02378 !
02379 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
02380 !
02381 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
02382 !
02383 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
02384 !
02385 !            ier    - integer
02386 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
02387 !                             routine. it is assumed that the requested
02388 !                             accuracy has been achieved.
02389 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine
02390 !                             the estimates for integral and error are
02391 !                             less reliable. it is assumed that the
02392 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
02393 !                     ier = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
02394 !                             has been achieved. one can allow more sub-
02395 !                             divisions by increasing the value of
02396 !                             limit. however, if this yields no
02397 !                             improvement it is advised to analyze the
02398 !                             integrand, in order to determine the
02399 !                             integration difficulties.  if the position
02400 !                             of a local difficulty can be determined
02401 !                             (e.g. singularity, discontinuity within
02402 !                             the interval) one will probably gain
02403 !                             from splitting up the interval at this
