02404 !                             point and calling appropriate integrators
02405 !                             on the subranges.
02406 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is detec-
02407 !                             ted, which prevents the requested
02408 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
02409 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
02410 !                             at some interior points of the integration
02411 !                             interval.
02412 !                         = 6 the input is invalid, because
02413 !                             c = a or c = b or
02414 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
02415 !                             or limit < 1.
02416 !                             result, abserr, neval, rlist(1), elist(1),
02417 !                             iord(1) and last are set to zero.
02418 !                             alist(1) and blist(1) are set to a and b
02419 !                             respectively.
02420 !
02421 !    Workspace, real ALIST(LIMIT), BLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 
02422 !    through LAST the left and right ends of the partition subintervals.
02423 !
02424 !    Workspace, real RLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
02425 !    the integral approximations on the subintervals.
02426 !
02427 !    Workspace, real ELIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
02428 !    the absolute error estimates on the subintervals.
02429 !
02430 !            iord    - integer
02431 !                      vector of dimension at least limit, the first k
02432 !                      elements of which are pointers to the error
02433 !                      estimates over the subintervals, so that
02434 !                      elist(iord(1)), ...,  elist(iord(k)) with
02435 !                      k = last if last <= (limit/2+2), and
02436 !                      k = limit+1-last otherwise, form a decreasing
02437 !                      sequence.
02438 !
02439 !            last    - integer
02440 !                      number of subintervals actually produced in
02441 !                      the subdivision process
02442 !
02443 !  Local parameters:
02444 !
02445 !           alist     - list of left end points of all subintervals
02446 !                       considered up to now
02447 !           blist     - list of right end points of all subintervals
02448 !                       considered up to now
02449 !           rlist(i)  - approximation to the integral over
02450 !                       (alist(i),blist(i))
02451 !           elist(i)  - error estimate applying to rlist(i)
02452 !           maxerr    - pointer to the interval with largest error
02453 !                       estimate
02454 !           errmax    - elist(maxerr)
02455 !           area      - sum of the integrals over the subintervals
02456 !           errsum    - sum of the errors over the subintervals
02457 !           errbnd    - requested accuracy max(epsabs,epsrel*
02458 !                       abs(result))
02459 !           *****1    - variable for the left subinterval
02460 !           *****2    - variable for the right subinterval
02461 !           last      - index for subdivision
02462 !
02463   implicit none
02464 
02465   integer limit
02466 
02467   real a
02468   real aa
02469   real abserr
02470   real alist(limit)
02471   real area
02472   real area1
02473   real area12
02474   real area2
02475   real a1
02476   real a2
02477   real b
02478   real bb
02479   real blist(limit)
02480   real b1
02481   real b2
02482   real c
02483   real elist(limit)
02484   real epsabs
02485   real epsrel
02486   real errbnd
02487   real errmax
02488   real error1
02489   real error2
02490   real erro12
02491   real errsum
02492   real, external :: f
02493   integer ier
02494   integer iord(limit)
02495   integer iroff1
02496   integer iroff2
02497   integer krule
02498   integer last
02499   integer maxerr
02500   integer nev
02501   integer neval
02502   integer nrmax
02503   real result
02504   real rlist(limit)
02505 !
02506 !  Test on validity of parameters.
02507 !
02508   ier = 0
02509   neval = 0
02510   last = 0
02511   alist(1) = a
02512   blist(1) = b
02513   rlist(1) = 0.0e+00
02514   elist(1) = 0.0e+00
02515   iord(1) = 0
02516   result = 0.0e+00
02517   abserr = 0.0e+00
02518 
02519   if ( c == a  ) then
02520     ier = 6
02521     return
02522   else if ( c == b ) then
02523     ier = 6
02524     return
02525   else if ( epsabs < 0.0e+00 .and. epsrel < 0.0e+00 ) then
02526     ier = 6
02527     return
02528   end if
02529 !
02530 !  First approximation to the integral.
02531 !
02532   if ( a <= b ) then
02533     aa = a
02534     bb = b
02535   else
02536     aa = b
02537     bb = a
02538   end if
02539 
02540   krule = 1
02541   call qc25c ( f, aa, bb, c, result, abserr, krule, neval )
02542   last = 1
02543   rlist(1) = result
02544   elist(1) = abserr
02545   iord(1) = 1
02546   alist(1) = a
02547   blist(1) = b
02548 !
02549 !  Test on accuracy.
02550 !
02551   errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs(result) )
02552 
02553   if ( limit == 1 ) then
02554     ier = 1
02555     go to 70
02556   end if
02557 
02558   if ( abserr < min ( 1.0e-02 * abs(result), errbnd)  ) then
02559     go to 70
02560   end if
02561 !
02562 !  Initialization
02563 !
02564   alist(1) = aa
02565   blist(1) = bb
02566   rlist(1) = result
02567   errmax = abserr
02568   maxerr = 1
02569   area = result
02570   errsum = abserr
02571   nrmax = 1
02572   iroff1 = 0
02573   iroff2 = 0
02574 
02575   do last = 2, limit
02576 !
02577 !  Bisect the subinterval with nrmax-th largest error estimate.
02578 !
02579     a1 = alist(maxerr)
02580     b1 = 5.0e-01*(alist(maxerr)+blist(maxerr))
02581     b2 = blist(maxerr)
02582 
02583     if ( c <= b1 .and. a1 < c ) then
02584       b1 = 5.0e-01*(c+b2)
02585     end if
02586 
02587     if ( b1 < c .and. c < b2 ) then
02588       b1 = 5.0e-01 * ( a1 + c )
02589     end if
02590 
02591     a2 = b1
02592     krule = 2
02593 
02594     call qc25c ( f, a1, b1, c, area1, error1, krule, nev )
02595     neval = neval+nev
02596 
02597     call qc25c ( f, a2, b2, c, area2, error2, krule, nev )
02598     neval = neval+nev
02599 !
02600 !  Improve previous approximations to integral and error
02601 !  and test for accuracy.
02602 !
02603     area12 = area1 + area2
02604     erro12 = error1 + error2
02605     errsum = errsum + erro12 - errmax
02606     area = area + area12 - rlist(maxerr)
02607 
02608     if ( abs ( rlist(maxerr)-area12) < 1.0e-05 * abs(area12) &
02609       .and. erro12 >= 9.9e-01 * errmax .and. krule == 0 ) &
02610       iroff1 = iroff1+1
02611 
02612     if ( last > 10.and.erro12 > errmax .and. krule == 0 ) then
02613       iroff2 = iroff2+1
02614     end if
02615 
02616     rlist(maxerr) = area1
02617     rlist(last) = area2
02618     errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs(area) )
02619 
02620     if ( errsum > errbnd ) then
02621 !
02622 !  Test for roundoff error and eventually set error flag.
02623 !
02624       if ( iroff1 >= 6 .and. iroff2 > 20 ) then
02625         ier = 2
02626       end if
02627 !
02628 !  Set error flag in the case that number of interval
02629 !  bisections exceeds limit.
02630 !
02631       if ( last == limit ) then
02632         ier = 1
02633       end if
02634 !
02635 !  Set error flag in the case of bad integrand behavior at
02636 !  a point of the integration range.
02637 !
02638       if ( max ( abs(a1), abs(b2) ) <= ( 1.0e+00 + 1.0e+03 * epsilon ( a1 ) ) &
02639         *( abs(a2)+1.0e+03* tiny ( a2 ) )) then
02640         ier = 3
02641       end if
02642 
02643     end if
02644 !
02645 !  Append the newly-created intervals to the list.
02646 !
02647     if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
02648       alist(last) = a2
02649       blist(maxerr) = b1
02650       blist(last) = b2
02651       elist(maxerr) = error1
02652       elist(last) = error2
02653     else
02654       alist(maxerr) = a2
02655       alist(last) = a1
02656       blist(last) = b1
02657       rlist(maxerr) = area2
02658       rlist(last) = area1
02659       elist(maxerr) = error2
02660       elist(last) = error1
02661     end if
02662 !
02663 !  Call QSORT to maintain the descending ordering
02664 !  in the list of error estimates and select the subinterval
02665 !  with NRMAX-th largest error estimate (to be bisected next).
02666 !
02667     call qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, errmax, elist, iord, nrmax )
02668 
02669     if ( ier /= 0 .or. errsum <= errbnd ) then
02670       exit
02671     end if
02672 
02673   end do
02674 !
02675 !  Compute final result.
02676 !
02677   result = sum ( rlist(1:last) )
02678 
02679   abserr = errsum
02680 
02681 70 continue 
02682 
02683   if ( aa == b ) then
02684     result = - result
02685   end if
02686 
02687   return
02688 end
02689 subroutine qawf ( f, a, omega, integr, epsabs, result, abserr, neval, ier )
02690 
02691 !*****************************************************************************80
02692 !
02693 !! QAWF computes Fourier integrals over the interval [ A, +Infinity ).
02694 !
02695 !  Discussion:
02696 !
02697 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral  
02698 ! 
02699 !      I = integral of F*COS(OMEGA*X) 
02700 !    or 
02701 !      I = integral of F*SIN(OMEGA*X) 
02702 !
02703 !    over the interval [A,+Infinity), hopefully satisfying
02704 !
02705 !      || I - RESULT || <= EPSABS.
02706 !
02707 !    If OMEGA = 0 and INTEGR = 1, the integral is calculated by means 
02708 !    of QAGI, and IER has the meaning as described in the comments of QAGI.
02709 !
02710 !  Author:
02711 !
02712 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02713 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
02714 !
02715 !  Reference:
02716 !
02717 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02718 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
02719 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
02720 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
02721 !
02722 !  Parameters:
02723 !
02724 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
02725 !      function f ( x )
02726 !      real f
02727 !      real x
02728 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
02729 !
02730 !    Input, real A, the lower limit of integration.
02731 !
02732 !    Input, real OMEGA, the parameter in the weight function.
02733 !
02734 !    Input, integer INTEGR, indicates which weight functions is used
02735 !    = 1, w(x) = cos(omega*x)
02736 !    = 2, w(x) = sin(omega*x)
02737 !
02738 !    Input, real EPSABS, the absolute accuracy requested.
02739 !
02740 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
02741 !
02742 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
02743 !
02744 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
02745 !
02746 !            ier    - integer
02747 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
02748 !                             routine. it is assumed that the
02749 !                             requested accuracy has been achieved.
02750 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine.
02751 !                             the estimates for integral and error are
02752 !                             less reliable. it is assumed that the
02753 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
02754 !                    if omega /= 0
02755 !                     ier = 6 the input is invalid because
02756 !                             (integr /= 1 and integr /= 2) or
02757 !                              epsabs <= 0
02758 !                              result, abserr, neval, lst are set to
02759 !                              zero.
02760 !                         = 7 abnormal termination of the computation
02761 !                             of one or more subintegrals
02762 !                         = 8 maximum number of cycles allowed
02763 !                             has been achieved, i.e. of subintervals
02764 !                             (a+(k-1)c,a+kc) where
02765 !                             c = (2*int(abs(omega))+1)*pi/abs(omega),
02766 !                             for k = 1, 2, ...
02767 !                         = 9 the extrapolation table constructed for
02768 !                             convergence acceleration of the series
02769 !                             formed by the integral contributions
02770 !                             over the cycles, does not converge to
02771 !                             within the requested accuracy.
02772 !
02773 !  Local parameters:
02774 !
02775 !    Integer LIMLST, gives an upper bound on the number of cycles, LIMLST >= 3.
02776 !    if limlst < 3, the routine will end with ier = 6.
02777 !
02778 !    Integer MAXP1, an upper bound on the number of Chebyshev moments which 
02779 !    can be stored, i.e. for the intervals of lengths abs(b-a)*2**(-l), 
02780 !    l = 0,1, ..., maxp1-2, maxp1 >= 1.  if maxp1 < 1, the routine will end
02781 !    with ier = 6.
02782 !
02783   implicit none
02784 
02785   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
02786   integer, parameter :: limlst = 50
02787   integer, parameter :: maxp1 = 21
02788 
02789   real a
02790   real abserr
02791   real alist(limit)
02792   real blist(limit)
02793   real chebmo(maxp1,25)
02794   real elist(limit)
02795   real epsabs
02796   real erlst(limlst)
02797   real, external :: f
02798   integer ier
02799   integer integr
02800   integer iord(limit)
02801   integer ierlst(limlst)
02802   integer lst
02803   integer neval
02804   integer nnlog(limit)
02805   real omega
02806   real result
02807   real rlist(limit)
02808   real rslst(limlst)
02809 
02810   ier = 6
02811   neval = 0
02812   result = 0.0e+00
02813   abserr = 0.0e+00
02814 
02815   if ( limlst < 3 .or. maxp1 < 1 ) then
02816     return
02817   end if
02818 
02819   call qawfe ( f, a, omega, integr, epsabs, limlst, limit, maxp1, &
02820     result, abserr, neval, ier, rslst, erlst, ierlst, lst, alist, blist, &
02821     rlist, elist, iord, nnlog, chebmo )
02822 
02823   return
02824 end
02825 subroutine qawfe ( f, a, omega, integr, epsabs, limlst, limit, maxp1, &
02826   result, abserr, neval, ier, rslst, erlst, ierlst, lst, alist, blist, &
02827   rlist, elist, iord, nnlog, chebmo )
02828 
02829 !*****************************************************************************80
02830 !
02831 !! QAWFE computes Fourier integrals.
02832 !
02833 !  Discussion:
02834 !
02835 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral   
02836 !      I = integral of F*COS(OMEGA*X) or F*SIN(OMEGA*X) over (A,+Infinity),
02837 !    hopefully satisfying
02838 !      || I - RESULT || <= EPSABS.
02839 !
02840 !  Author:
02841 !
02842 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02843 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
02844 !
02845 !  Reference:
02846 !
02847 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
02848 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
02849 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
02850 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
02851 !
02852 !  Parameters:
02853 !
02854 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
02855 !      function f ( x )
02856 !      real f
02857 !      real x
02858 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
02859 !
02860 !    Input, real A, the lower limit of integration.
02861 !
02862 !    Input, real OMEGA, the parameter in the weight function.
02863 !
02864 !    Input, integer INTEGR, indicates which weight function is used
02865 !    = 1      w(x) = cos(omega*x)
02866 !    = 2      w(x) = sin(omega*x)
02867 !
02868 !    Input, real EPSABS, the absolute accuracy requested.
02869 !
02870 !    Input, integer LIMLST, an upper bound on the number of cycles.
02871 !    LIMLST must be at least 1.  In fact, if LIMLST < 3, the routine 
02872 !    will end with IER= 6.
02873 !
02874 !    Input, integer LIMIT, an upper bound on the number of subintervals 
02875 !    allowed in the partition of each cycle, limit >= 1.
02876 !
02877 !            maxp1  - integer
02878 !                     gives an upper bound on the number of
02879 !                     Chebyshev moments which can be stored, i.e.
02880 !                     for the intervals of lengths abs(b-a)*2**(-l),
02881 !                     l=0,1, ..., maxp1-2, maxp1 >= 1
02882 !
02883 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
02884 !
02885 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
02886 !
02887 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
02888 !
02889 !            ier    - ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of
02890 !                             the routine. it is assumed that the
02891 !                             requested accuracy has been achieved.
02892 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine
02893 !                             the estimates for integral and error
02894 !                             are less reliable. it is assumed that
02895 !                             the requested accuracy has not been
02896 !                             achieved.
02897 !                    if omega /= 0
02898 !                     ier = 6 the input is invalid because
02899 !                             (integr /= 1 and integr /= 2) or
02900 !                              epsabs <= 0 or limlst < 3.
02901 !                              result, abserr, neval, lst are set
02902 !                              to zero.
02903 !                         = 7 bad integrand behavior occurs within
02904 !                             one or more of the cycles. location
02905 !                             and type of the difficulty involved
02906 !                             can be determined from the vector ierlst.
02907 !                             here lst is the number of cycles actually
02908 !                             needed (see below).
02909 !                             ierlst(k) = 1 the maximum number of
02910 !                                           subdivisions (= limit)
02911 !                                           has been achieved on the
02912 !                                           k th cycle.
02913 !                                       = 2 occurence of roundoff
02914 !                                           error is detected and
02915 !                                           prevents the tolerance
02916 !                                           imposed on the k th cycle
02917 !                                           from being acheived.
02918 !                                       = 3 extremely bad integrand
02919 !                                           behavior occurs at some
02920 !                                           points of the k th cycle.
02921 !                                       = 4 the integration procedure
02922 !                                           over the k th cycle does
02923 !                                           not converge (to within the
02924 !                                           required accuracy) due to
02925 !                                           roundoff in the
02926 !                                           extrapolation procedure
02927 !                                           invoked on this cycle. it
02928 !                                           is assumed that the result
02929 !                                           on this interval is the
02930 !                                           best which can be obtained.
02931 !                                       = 5 the integral over the k th
02932 !                                           cycle is probably divergent
02933 !                                           or slowly convergent. it
02934 !                                           must be noted that
02935 !                                           divergence can occur with
02936 !                                           any other value of
02937 !                                           ierlst(k).
02938 !                         = 8 maximum number of  cycles  allowed
02939 !                             has been achieved, i.e. of subintervals
02940 !                             (a+(k-1)c,a+kc) where
02941 !                             c = (2*int(abs(omega))+1)*pi/abs(omega),
02942 !                             for k = 1, 2, ..., lst.
02943 !                             one can allow more cycles by increasing
02944 !                             the value of limlst (and taking the
02945 !                             according dimension adjustments into
02946 !                             account).
02947 !                             examine the array iwork which contains
02948 !                             the error flags over the cycles, in order
02949 !                             to eventual look for local integration
02950 !                             difficulties.
02951 !                             if the position of a local difficulty can
02952 !                             be determined (e.g. singularity,
02953 !                             discontinuity within the interval)
02954 !                             one will probably gain from splitting
02955 !                             up the interval at this point and
02956 !                             calling appopriate integrators on the
02957 !                             subranges.
02958 !                         = 9 the extrapolation table constructed for
02959 !                             convergence acceleration of the series
02960 !                             formed by the integral contributions
02961 !                             over the cycles, does not converge to
02962 !                             within the required accuracy.
02963 !                             as in the case of ier = 8, it is advised
02964 !                             to examine the array iwork which contains
02965 !                             the error flags on the cycles.
02966 !                    if omega = 0 and integr = 1,
02967 !                    the integral is calculated by means of qagi
02968 !                    and ier = ierlst(1) (with meaning as described
02969 !                    for ierlst(k), k = 1).
02970 !
02971 !            rslst  - real
02972 !                     vector of dimension at least limlst
02973 !                     rslst(k) contains the integral contribution
02974 !                     over the interval (a+(k-1)c,a+kc) where
02975 !                     c = (2*int(abs(omega))+1)*pi/abs(omega),
02976 !                     k = 1, 2, ..., lst.
02977 !                     note that, if omega = 0, rslst(1) contains
02978 !                     the value of the integral over (a,infinity).
02979 !
02980 !            erlst  - real
02981 !                     vector of dimension at least limlst
02982 !                     erlst(k) contains the error estimate
02983 !                     corresponding with rslst(k).
02984 !
02985 !            ierlst - integer
02986 !                     vector of dimension at least limlst
02987 !                     ierlst(k) contains the error flag corresponding
02988 !                     with rslst(k). for the meaning of the local error
02989 !                     flags see description of output parameter ier.
02990 !
02991 !            lst    - integer
02992 !                     number of subintervals needed for the integration
02993 !                     if omega = 0 then lst is set to 1.
02994 !
02995 !            alist, blist, rlist, elist - real
02996 !                     vector of dimension at least limit,
02997 !
02998 !            iord, nnlog - integer
02999 !                     vector of dimension at least limit, providing
03000 !                     space for the quantities needed in the
03001 !                     subdivision process of each cycle
03002 !
03003 !            chebmo - real
03004 !                     array of dimension at least (maxp1,25),
03005 !                     providing space for the Chebyshev moments
03006 !                     needed within the cycles
03007 !
03008 !  Local parameters:
03009 !
03010 !           c1, c2    - end points of subinterval (of length
03011 !                       cycle)
03012 !           cycle     - (2*int(abs(omega))+1)*pi/abs(omega)
03013 !           psum      - vector of dimension at least (limexp+2)
03014 !                       (see routine qextr)
03015 !                       psum contains the part of the epsilon table
03016 !                       which is still needed for further computations.
03017 !                       each element of psum is a partial sum of
03018 !                       the series which should sum to the value of
03019 !                       the integral.
03020 !           errsum    - sum of error estimates over the
03021 !                       subintervals, calculated cumulatively
03022 !           epsa      - absolute tolerance requested over current
03023 !                       subinterval
03024 !           chebmo    - array containing the modified Chebyshev
03025 !                       moments (see also routine qc25o)
03026 !
03027   implicit none
03028 
03029   integer limit
03030   integer limlst
03031   integer maxp1
03032 
03033   real a
03034   real abseps
03035   real abserr
03036   real alist(limit)
03037   real blist(limit)
03038   real chebmo(maxp1,25)
03039   real correc
03040   real cycle
03041   real c1
03042   real c2
03043   real dl
03044 ! real dla
03045   real drl
03046   real elist(limit)
03047   real ep
03048   real eps
03049   real epsa
03050   real epsabs
03051   real erlst(limlst)
03052   real errsum
03053   real, external :: f
03054   real fact
03055   integer ier
03056   integer ierlst(limlst)
03057   integer integr
03058   integer iord(limit)
03059   integer ktmin
03060   integer l
03061   integer ll
03062   integer lst
03063   integer momcom
03064   integer nev
03065   integer neval
03066   integer nnlog(limit)
03067   integer nres
03068   integer numrl2
03069   real omega
03070   real, parameter :: p = 0.9E+00
03071   real, parameter :: pi = 3.1415926535897932E+00
03072   real p1
03073   real psum(52)
03074   real reseps
03075   real result
03076   real res3la(3)
03077   real rlist(limit)
03078   real rslst(limlst)
03079 !
03080 !  The dimension of  psum  is determined by the value of
03081 !  limexp in QEXTR (psum must be
03082 !  of dimension (limexp+2) at least).
03083 !
03084 !  Test on validity of parameters.
03085 !
03086   result = 0.0e+00
03087   abserr = 0.0e+00
03088   neval = 0
03089   lst = 0
03090   ier = 0
03091 
03092   if ( (integr /= 1 .and. integr /= 2 ) .or. &
03093     epsabs <= 0.0e+00 .or. &
03094     limlst < 3 ) then
03095     ier = 6
03096     return
03097   end if
03098 
03099   if ( omega == 0.0e+00 ) then
03100 
03101     if ( integr == 1 ) then
03102       call qagi ( f, 0.0e+00, 1, epsabs, 0.0e+00, result, abserr, neval, ier )
03103     else
03104       result = 0.0E+00
03105       abserr = 0.0E+00
03106       neval = 0
03107       ier = 0
03108     end if
03109 
03110     rslst(1) = result
03111     erlst(1) = abserr
03112     ierlst(1) = ier
03113     lst = 1
03114 
03115     return
03116   end if
03117 !
03118 !  Initializations.
03119 !
03120   l = int ( abs ( omega ) )
03121   dl = 2 * l + 1
03122   cycle = dl * pi / abs ( omega )
03123   ier = 0
03124   ktmin = 0
03125   neval = 0
03126   numrl2 = 0
03127   nres = 0
03128   c1 = a
03129   c2 = cycle+a
03130   p1 = 1.0e+00-p
03131   eps = epsabs
03132 
03133   if ( epsabs > tiny ( epsabs ) / p1 ) then
03134     eps = epsabs * p1
03135   end if
03136 
03137   ep = eps
03138   fact = 1.0e+00
03139   correc = 0.0e+00
03140   abserr = 0.0e+00
03141   errsum = 0.0e+00
03142 
03143   do lst = 1, limlst
03144 !
03145 !  Integrate over current subinterval.
03146 !
03147 !   dla = lst
03148     epsa = eps * fact
03149 
03150     call qfour ( f, c1, c2, omega, integr, epsa, 0.0e+00, limit, lst, maxp1, &
03151       rslst(lst), erlst(lst), nev, ierlst(lst), alist, blist, rlist, elist, &
03152       iord, nnlog, momcom, chebmo )
03153 
03154     neval = neval + nev
03155     fact = fact * p
03156     errsum = errsum + erlst(lst)
03157     drl = 5.0e+01 * abs(rslst(lst))
03158 !
03159 !  Test on accuracy with partial sum.
03160 !
03161     if ((errsum+drl) <= epsabs.and.lst >= 6) then
03162       go to 80
03163     end if
03164 
03165     correc = max ( correc,erlst(lst))
03166 
03167     if ( ierlst(lst) /= 0 ) then
03168       eps = max ( ep,correc*p1)
03169       ier = 7
03170     end if
03171 
03172     if ( ier == 7 .and. (errsum+drl) <= correc*1.0e+01.and. lst > 5) go to 80
03173 
03174     numrl2 = numrl2+1
03175 
03176     if ( lst <= 1 ) then
03177       psum(1) = rslst(1)
03178       go to 40
03179     end if
03180 
03181     psum(numrl2) = psum(ll) + rslst(lst)
03182 
03183     if ( lst == 2 ) then
03184       go to 40
03185     end if
03186 !
03187 !  Test on maximum number of subintervals
03188 !
03189     if ( lst == limlst ) then
03190       ier = 8
03191     end if
03192 !
03193 !  Perform new extrapolation
03194 !
03195     call qextr ( numrl2, psum, reseps, abseps, res3la, nres )
03196 !
03197 !  Test whether extrapolated result is influenced by roundoff
03198 !
03199     ktmin = ktmin + 1
03200 
03201     if ( ktmin >= 15 .and. abserr <= 1.0e-03 * (errsum+drl) ) then
03202       ier = 9
03203     end  if
03204 
03205     if ( abseps <= abserr .or. lst == 3 ) then
03206 
03207       abserr = abseps
03208       result = reseps
03209       ktmin = 0
03210 !
03211 !  If IER is not 0, check whether direct result (partial
03212 !  sum) or extrapolated result yields the best integral
03213 !  approximation
03214 !
03215       if ( ( abserr + 1.0e+01 * correc ) <= epsabs ) then
03216         exit
03217       end if
03218 
03219       if ( abserr <= epsabs .and. 1.0e+01 * correc >= epsabs ) then
03220         exit
03221       end if
03222 
03223     end if
03224 
03225     if ( ier /= 0 .and. ier /= 7 ) then
03226       exit
03227     end if
03228 
03229 40  continue
03230 
03231     ll = numrl2
03232     c1 = c2
03233     c2 = c2+cycle
03234 
03235   end do
03236 !
03237 !  Set final result and error estimate.
03238 !
03239 !60 continue
03240 
03241   abserr = abserr + 1.0e+01 * correc
03242 
03243   if ( ier == 0 ) then
03244     return
03245   end if
03246 
03247   if ( result /= 0.0e+00 .and. psum(numrl2) /= 0.0e+00) go to 70
03248 
03249   if ( abserr > errsum ) then
03250     go to 80
03251   end if
03252 
03253   if ( psum(numrl2) == 0.0e+00 ) then
03254     return
03255   end if
03256 
03257 70 continue
03258 
03259   if ( abserr / abs(result) <= (errsum+drl)/abs(psum(numrl2)) ) then
03260 
03261     if ( ier >= 1 .and. ier /= 7 ) then
03262       abserr = abserr + drl
03263     end if
03264 
03265     return
03266 
03267   end if
03268 
03269 80 continue
03270 
03271   result = psum(numrl2)
03272   abserr = errsum + drl
03273 
03274   return
03275 end
03276 subroutine qawo ( f, a, b, omega, integr, epsabs, epsrel, result, abserr, &
03277   neval, ier )
03278 
03279 !*****************************************************************************80
03280 !
03281 !! QAWO computes the integrals of oscillatory integrands.
03282 !
03283 !  Discussion:
03284 !
03285 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a given
03286 !    definite integral
03287 !      I = Integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) * cos ( OMEGA * X ) dx
03288 !    or 
03289 !      I = Integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) * sin ( OMEGA * X ) dx
03290 !    hopefully satisfying following claim for accuracy
03291 !      | I - RESULT | <= max ( epsabs, epsrel * |I| ).
03292 !
03293 !  Author:
03294 !
03295 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03296 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
03297 !
03298 !  Reference:
03299 !
03300 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03301 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
03302 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
03303 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
03304 !
03305 !  Parameters:
03306 !
03307 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
03308 !      function f ( x )
03309 !      real f
03310 !      real x
03311 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
03312 !
03313 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
03314 !
03315 !    Input, real OMEGA, the parameter in the weight function.
03316 !
03317 !    Input, integer INTEGR, specifies the weight function:
03318 !    1, W(X) = cos ( OMEGA * X )
03319 !    2, W(X) = sin ( OMEGA * X )
03320 !
03321 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
03322 !
03323 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
03324 !
03325 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
03326 !
03327 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
03328 !
03329 !            ier    - integer
03330 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
03331 !                             routine. it is assumed that the
03332 !                             requested accuracy has been achieved.
03333 !                   - ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine.
03334 !                             the estimates for integral and error are
03335 !                             less reliable. it is assumed that the
03336 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
03337 !                     ier = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
03338 !                             (= leniw/2) has been achieved. one can
03339 !                             allow more subdivisions by increasing the
03340 !                             value of leniw (and taking the according
03341 !                             dimension adjustments into account).
03342 !                             however, if this yields no improvement it
03343 !                             is advised to analyze the integrand in
03344 !                             order to determine the integration
03345 !                             difficulties. if the position of a local
03346 !                             difficulty can be determined (e.g.
03347 !                             singularity, discontinuity within the
03348 !                             interval) one will probably gain from
03349 !                             splitting up the interval at this point
03350 !                             and calling the integrator on the
03351 !                             subranges. if possible, an appropriate
03352 !                             special-purpose integrator should
03353 !                             be used which is designed for handling
03354 !                             the type of difficulty involved.
03355 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is
03356 !                             detected, which prevents the requested
03357 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
03358 !                             the error may be under-estimated.
03359 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
03360 !                             at some interior points of the integration
03361 !                             interval.
03362 !                         = 4 the algorithm does not converge. roundoff
03363 !                             error is detected in the extrapolation
03364 !                             table. it is presumed that the requested
03365 !                             tolerance cannot be achieved due to
03366 !                             roundoff in the extrapolation table,
03367 !                             and that the returned result is the best
03368 !                             which can be obtained.
03369 !                         = 5 the integral is probably divergent, or
03370 !                             slowly convergent. it must be noted that
03371 !                             divergence can occur with any other value
03372 !                             of ier.
03373 !                         = 6 the input is invalid, because
03374 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
03375 !                             result, abserr, neval are set to zero.
03376 !
03377 !  Local parameters:
03378 !
03379 !    limit is the maximum number of subintervals allowed in the
03380 !    subdivision process of QFOUR. take care that limit >= 1.
03381 !
03382 !    maxp1 gives an upper bound on the number of Chebyshev moments
03383 !    which can be stored, i.e. for the intervals of lengths
03384 !    abs(b-a)*2**(-l), l = 0, 1, ... , maxp1-2. take care that
03385 !    maxp1 >= 1.
03386 
03387   implicit none
03388 
03389   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
03390   integer, parameter :: maxp1 = 21
03391 
03392   real a
03393   real abserr
03394   real alist(limit)
03395   real b
03396   real blist(limit)
03397   real chebmo(maxp1,25)
03398   real elist(limit)
03399   real epsabs
03400   real epsrel
03401   real, external :: f
03402   integer ier
03403   integer integr
03404   integer iord(limit)
03405   integer momcom
03406   integer neval
03407   integer nnlog(limit)
03408   real omega
03409   real result
03410   real rlist(limit)
03411 
03412   call qfour ( f, a, b, omega, integr, epsabs, epsrel, limit, 1, maxp1, &
03413     result, abserr, neval, ier, alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, nnlog, &
03414     momcom, chebmo )
03415 
03416   return
03417 end
03418 subroutine qaws ( f, a, b, alfa, beta, integr, epsabs, epsrel, result, &
03419   abserr, neval, ier )
03420 
03421 !*****************************************************************************80
03422 !
03423 !! QAWS estimates integrals with algebraico-logarithmic endpoint singularities.
03424 !
03425 !  Discussion:
03426 !
03427 !    This routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a given
03428 !    definite integral   
03429 !      I = integral of f*w over (a,b) 
03430 !    where w shows a singular behavior at the end points, see parameter
03431 !    integr, hopefully satisfying following claim for accuracy
03432 !      abs(i-result) <= max(epsabs,epsrel*abs(i)).
03433 !
03434 !  Author:
03435 !
03436 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03437 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
03438 !
03439 !  Reference:
03440 !
03441 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03442 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
03443 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
03444 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
03445 !
03446 !  Parameters:
03447 !
03448 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
03449 !      function f ( x )
03450 !      real f
03451 !      real x
03452 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
03453 !
03454 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
03455 !
03456 !    Input, real ALFA, BETA, parameters used in the weight function.
03457 !    ALFA and BETA should be greater than -1.
03458 !
03459 !    Input, integer INTEGR, indicates which weight function is to be used
03460 !    = 1  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta
03461 !    = 2  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(x-a)
03462 !    = 3  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(b-x)
03463 !    = 4  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(x-a)*log(b-x)
03464 !
03465 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
03466 !
03467 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
03468 !
03469 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
03470 !
03471 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
03472 !
03473 !            ier    - integer
03474 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
03475 !                             routine. it is assumed that the requested
03476 !                             accuracy has been achieved.
03477 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine
03478 !                             the estimates for the integral and error
03479 !                             are less reliable. it is assumed that the
03480 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
03481 !                     ier = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
03482 !                             has been achieved. one can allow more
03483 !                             subdivisions by increasing the data value
03484 !                             of limit in qaws (and taking the according
03485 !                             dimension adjustments into account).
03486 !                             however, if this yields no improvement it
03487 !                             is advised to analyze the integrand, in
03488 !                             order to determine the integration
03489 !                             difficulties which prevent the requested
03490 !                             tolerance from being achieved. in case of
03491 !                             a jump discontinuity or a local
03492 !                             singularity of algebraico-logarithmic type
03493 !                             at one or more interior points of the
03494 !                             integration range, one should proceed by
03495 !                             splitting up the interval at these points
03496 !                             and calling the integrator on the
03497 !                             subranges.
03498 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is
03499 !                             detected, which prevents the requested
03500 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
03501 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
03502 !                             at some points of the integration
03503 !                             interval.
03504 !                         = 6 the input is invalid, because
03505 !                             b <= a or alfa <= (-1) or beta <= (-1) or
03506 !                             integr < 1 or integr > 4 or
03507 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
03508 !                             result, abserr, neval are set to zero.
03509 !
03510 !  Local parameters:
03511 !
03512 !    LIMIT is the maximum number of subintervals allowed in the
03513 !    subdivision process of qawse. take care that limit >= 2.
03514 !
03515   implicit none
03516 
03517   integer, parameter :: limit = 500
03518 
03519   real a
03520   real abserr
03521   real alfa
03522   real alist(limit)
03523   real b
03524   real blist(limit)
03525   real beta
03526   real elist(limit)
03527   real epsabs
03528   real epsrel
03529   real, external :: f
03530   integer ier
03531   integer integr
03532   integer iord(limit)
03533   integer last
03534   integer neval
03535   real result
03536   real rlist(limit)
03537 
03538   call qawse ( f, a, b, alfa, beta, integr, epsabs, epsrel, limit, result, &
03539     abserr, neval, ier, alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, last )
03540 
03541   return
03542 end
03543 subroutine qawse ( f, a, b, alfa, beta, integr, epsabs, epsrel, limit, &
03544   result, abserr, neval, ier, alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, last )
03545 
03546 !*****************************************************************************80
03547 !
03548 !! QAWSE estimates integrals with algebraico-logarithmic endpoint singularities.
03549 !
03550 !  Discussion:
03551 !
03552 !    This routine calculates an approximation RESULT to an integral
03553 !      I = integral of F(X) * W(X) over (a,b), 
03554 !    where W(X) shows a singular behavior at the endpoints, hopefully 
03555 !    satisfying:
03556 !      | I - RESULT | <= max ( epsabs, epsrel * |I| ).
03557 !
03558 !  Author:
03559 !
03560 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03561 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
03562 !
03563 !  Reference:
03564 !
03565 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03566 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
03567 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
03568 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
03569 !
03570 !  Parameters:
03571 !
03572 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
03573 !      function f ( x )
03574 !      real f
03575 !      real x
03576 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
03577 !
03578 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
03579 !
03580 !    Input, real ALFA, BETA, parameters used in the weight function.
03581 !    ALFA and BETA should be greater than -1.
03582 !
03583 !    Input, integer INTEGR, indicates which weight function is used:
03584 !    = 1  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta
03585 !    = 2  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(x-a)
03586 !    = 3  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(b-x)
03587 !    = 4  (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(x-a)*log(b-x)
03588 !
03589 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
03590 !
03591 !    Input, integer LIMIT, an upper bound on the number of subintervals
03592 !    in the partition of (A,B), LIMIT >= 2.  If LIMIT < 2, the routine 
03593 !     will end with IER = 6.
03594 !
03595 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
03596 !
03597 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
03598 !
03599 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
03600 !
03601 !            ier    - integer
03602 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
03603 !                             routine. it is assumed that the requested
03604 !                             accuracy has been achieved.
03605 !                     ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine
03606 !                             the estimates for the integral and error
03607 !                             are less reliable. it is assumed that the
03608 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
03609 !                         = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
03610 !                             has been achieved. one can allow more
03611 !                             subdivisions by increasing the value of
03612 !                             limit. however, if this yields no
03613 !                             improvement it is advised to analyze the
03614 !                             integrand, in order to determine the
03615 !                             integration difficulties which prevent
03616 !                             the requested tolerance from being
03617 !                             achieved. in case of a jump discontinuity
03618 !                             or a local singularity of algebraico-
03619 !                             logarithmic type at one or more interior
03620 !                             points of the integration range, one
03621 !                             should proceed by splitting up the
03622 !                             interval at these points and calling the
03623 !                             integrator on the subranges.
03624 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is
03625 !                             detected, which prevents the requested
03626 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
03627 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
03628 !                             at some points of the integration
03629 !                             interval.
03630 !                         = 6 the input is invalid, because
03631 !                             b <= a or alfa <= (-1) or beta <= (-1) or
03632 !                             integr < 1 or integr > 4, or
03633 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
03634 !                             or limit < 2.
03635 !                             result, abserr, neval, rlist(1), elist(1),
03636 !                             iord(1) and last are set to zero.
03637 !                             alist(1) and blist(1) are set to a and b
03638 !                             respectively.
03639 !
03640 !    Workspace, real ALIST(LIMIT), BLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 
03641 !    through LAST the left and right ends of the partition subintervals.
03642 !
03643 !    Workspace, real RLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
03644 !    the integral approximations on the subintervals.
03645 !
03646 !    Workspace, real ELIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
03647 !    the absolute error estimates on the subintervals.
03648 !
03649 !            iord   - integer
03650 !                     vector of dimension at least limit, the first k
03651 !                     elements of which are pointers to the error
03652 !                     estimates over the subintervals, so that
03653 !                     elist(iord(1)), ..., elist(iord(k)) with k = last
03654 !                     if last <= (limit/2+2), and k = limit+1-last
03655 !                     otherwise, form a decreasing sequence.
03656 !
03657 !    Output, integer LAST, the number of subintervals actually produced in 
03658 !    the subdivision process.
03659 !
03660 !  Local parameters:
03661 !
03662 !           alist     - list of left end points of all subintervals
03663 !                       considered up to now
03664 !           blist     - list of right end points of all subintervals
03665 !                       considered up to now
03666 !           rlist(i)  - approximation to the integral over
03667 !                       (alist(i),blist(i))
03668 !           elist(i)  - error estimate applying to rlist(i)
03669 !           maxerr    - pointer to the interval with largest error
03670 !                       estimate
03671 !           errmax    - elist(maxerr)
03672 !           area      - sum of the integrals over the subintervals
03673 !           errsum    - sum of the errors over the subintervals
03674 !           errbnd    - requested accuracy max(epsabs,epsrel*
03675 !                       abs(result))
03676 !           *****1    - variable for the left subinterval
03677 !           *****2    - variable for the right subinterval
03678 !           last      - index for subdivision
03679 !
03680   implicit none
03681 
03682   integer limit
03683 
03684   real a
03685   real abserr
03686   real alfa
03687   real alist(limit)
03688   real area
03689   real area1
03690   real area12
03691   real area2
03692   real a1
03693   real a2
03694   real b
03695   real beta
03696   real blist(limit)
03697   real b1
03698   real b2
03699   real centre
03700   real elist(limit)
03701   real epsabs
03702   real epsrel
03703   real errbnd
03704   real errmax
03705   real error1
03706   real erro12
03707   real error2
03708   real errsum
03709   real, external :: f
03710   integer ier
03711   integer integr
03712   integer iord(limit)
03713   integer iroff1
03714   integer iroff2
03715   integer last
03716   integer maxerr
03717   integer nev
03718   integer neval
03719   integer nrmax
03720   real resas1
03721   real resas2
03722   real result
03723   real rg(25)
03724   real rh(25)
03725   real ri(25)
03726   real rj(25)
03727   real rlist(limit)
03728 !
03729 !  Test on validity of parameters.
03730 !
03731   ier = 0
03732   neval = 0
03733   last = 0
03734   rlist(1) = 0.0e+00
03735   elist(1) = 0.0e+00
03736   iord(1) = 0
03737   result = 0.0e+00
03738   abserr = 0.0e+00
03739 
03740   if ( b <= a .or. &
03741     (epsabs < 0.0e+00 .and. epsrel < 0.0e+00) .or. &
03742     alfa <= (-1.0e+00) .or. &
03743     beta <= (-1.0e+00) .or. &
03744     integr < 1 .or. &
03745     integr > 4 .or. &
03746     limit < 2 ) then
03747     ier = 6
03748     return
03749   end if
03750 !
03751 !  Compute the modified Chebyshev moments.
03752 !
03753   call qmomo ( alfa, beta, ri, rj, rg, rh, integr )
03754 !
03755 !  Integrate over the intervals (a,(a+b)/2) and ((a+b)/2,b).
03756 !
03757   centre = 5.0e-01 * ( b + a )
03758 
03759   call qc25s ( f, a, b, a, centre, alfa, beta, ri, rj, rg, rh, area1, &
03760     error1, resas1, integr, nev )
03761 
03762   neval = nev
03763 
03764   call qc25s ( f, a, b, centre, b, alfa, beta, ri, rj, rg, rh, area2, &
03765     error2, resas2, integr, nev )
03766 
03767   last = 2
03768   neval = neval+nev
03769   result = area1+area2
03770   abserr = error1+error2
03771 !
03772 !  Test on accuracy.
03773 !
03774   errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs ( result ) )
03775 !
03776 !  Initialization.
03777 !
03778   if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
03779     alist(1) = a
03780     alist(2) = centre
03781     blist(1) = centre
03782     blist(2) = b
03783     rlist(1) = area1
03784     rlist(2) = area2
03785     elist(1) = error1
03786     elist(2) = error2
03787   else
03788     alist(1) = centre
03789     alist(2) = a
03790     blist(1) = b
03791     blist(2) = centre
03792     rlist(1) = area2
03793     rlist(2) = area1
03794     elist(1) = error2
03795     elist(2) = error1
03796   end if
03797 
03798   iord(1) = 1
03799   iord(2) = 2
03800 
03801   if ( limit == 2 ) then
03802     ier = 1
03803     return
03804   end if
03805 
03806   if ( abserr <= errbnd ) then
03807     return
03808   end if
03809 
03810   errmax = elist(1)
03811   maxerr = 1
03812   nrmax = 1
03813   area = result
03814   errsum = abserr
03815   iroff1 = 0
03816   iroff2 = 0
03817 
03818   do last = 3, limit
03819 !
03820 !  Bisect the subinterval with largest error estimate.
03821 !
03822     a1 = alist(maxerr)
03823     b1 = 5.0e-01 * ( alist(maxerr) + blist(maxerr) )
03824     a2 = b1
03825     b2 = blist(maxerr)
03826 
03827     call qc25s ( f, a, b, a1, b1, alfa, beta, ri, rj, rg, rh, area1, &
03828       error1, resas1, integr, nev )
03829 
03830     neval = neval + nev
03831 
03832     call qc25s ( f, a, b, a2, b2, alfa, beta, ri, rj, rg, rh, area2, &
03833       error2, resas2, integr, nev )
03834 
03835     neval = neval + nev
03836 !
03837 !  Improve previous approximations integral and error and
03838 !  test for accuracy.
03839 !
03840     area12 = area1+area2
03841     erro12 = error1+error2
03842     errsum = errsum+erro12-errmax
03843     area = area+area12-rlist(maxerr)
03844 !
03845 !  Test for roundoff error.
03846 !
03847     if ( a /= a1 .and. b /= b2 ) then
03848 
03849       if ( resas1 /= error1 .and. resas2 /= error2 ) then
03850 
03851         if ( abs ( rlist(maxerr) - area12 ) < 1.0e-05 * abs ( area12 ) &
03852           .and.erro12 >= 9.9e-01*errmax ) then
03853           iroff1 = iroff1 + 1
03854         end if
03855 
03856         if ( last > 10 .and. erro12 > errmax ) then
03857           iroff2 = iroff2 + 1
03858         end if
03859 
03860       end if
03861 
03862     end if
03863 
03864     rlist(maxerr) = area1
03865     rlist(last) = area2
03866 !
03867 !  Test on accuracy.
03868 !
03869     errbnd = max ( epsabs, epsrel * abs ( area ) )
03870 
03871     if ( errsum > errbnd ) then
03872 !
03873 !  Set error flag in the case that the number of interval
03874 !  bisections exceeds limit.
03875 !
03876       if ( last == limit ) then
03877         ier = 1
03878       end if
03879 !
03880 !  Set error flag in the case of roundoff error.
03881 !
03882       if ( iroff1 >= 6 .or. iroff2 >= 20 ) then
03883         ier = 2
03884      end if
03885 !
03886 !  Set error flag in the case of bad integrand behavior
03887 !  at interior points of integration range.
03888 !
03889       if ( max ( abs(a1),abs(b2)) <= (1.0e+00+1.0e+03* epsilon ( a1 ) )* &
03890         ( abs(a2) + 1.0e+03* tiny ( a2) )) then
03891         ier = 3
03892       end if
03893 
03894     end if
03895 !
03896 !  Append the newly-created intervals to the list.
03897 !
03898     if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
03899       alist(last) = a2
03900       blist(maxerr) = b1
03901       blist(last) = b2
03902       elist(maxerr) = error1
03903       elist(last) = error2
03904     else
03905       alist(maxerr) = a2
03906       alist(last) = a1
03907       blist(last) = b1
03908       rlist(maxerr) = area2
03909       rlist(last) = area1
03910       elist(maxerr) = error2
03911       elist(last) = error1
03912     end if
03913 !
03914 !  Call QSORT to maintain the descending ordering
03915 !  in the list of error estimates and select the subinterval
03916 !  with largest error estimate (to be bisected next).
03917 !
03918     call qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, errmax, elist, iord, nrmax )
03919 
03920     if ( ier /= 0 .or. errsum <= errbnd ) then
03921       exit
03922     end if
03923 
03924   end do
03925 !
03926 !  Compute final result.
03927 !
03928   result = sum ( rlist(1:last) )
03929 
03930   abserr = errsum
03931 
03932   return
03933 end
03934 subroutine qc25c ( f, a, b, c, result, abserr, krul, neval )
03935 
03936 !*****************************************************************************80
03937 !
03938 !! QC25C returns integration rules for Cauchy Principal Value integrals.
03939 !
03940 !  Discussion:
03941 !
03942 !    This routine estimates 
03943 !      I = integral of F(X) * W(X) over (a,b) 
03944 !    with error estimate, where 
03945 !      w(x) = 1/(x-c)
03946 !
03947 !  Author:
03948 !
03949 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03950 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
03951 !
03952 !  Reference:
03953 !
03954 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
03955 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
03956 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
03957 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
03958 !
03959 !  Parameters:
03960 !
03961 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
03962 !      function f ( x )
03963 !      real f
03964 !      real x
03965 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
03966 !
03967 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
03968 !
03969 !    Input, real C, the parameter in the weight function.
03970 !
03971 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
03972 !    RESULT is computed by using a generalized Clenshaw-Curtis method if
03973 !    C lies within ten percent of the integration interval.  In the 
03974 !    other case the 15-point Kronrod rule obtained by optimal addition
03975 !    of abscissae to the 7-point Gauss rule, is applied.
03976 !
03977 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
03978 !
03979 !           krul   - integer
03980 !                    key which is decreased by 1 if the 15-point
03981 !                    Gauss-Kronrod scheme has been used
03982 !
03983 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
03984 !
03985 !  Local parameters:
03986 !
03987 !           fval   - value of the function f at the points
03988 !                    cos(k*pi/24),  k = 0, ..., 24
03989 !           cheb12 - Chebyshev series expansion coefficients, for the
03990 !                    function f, of degree 12
03991 !           cheb24 - Chebyshev series expansion coefficients, for the
03992 !                    function f, of degree 24
03993 !           res12  - approximation to the integral corresponding to the
03994 !                    use of cheb12
03995 !           res24  - approximation to the integral corresponding to the
03996 !                    use of cheb24
03997 !           qwgtc  - external function subprogram defining the weight
03998 !                    function
03999 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval
04000 !           centr  - mid point of the interval
04001 !
04002   implicit none
04003 
04004   real a
04005   real abserr
04006   real ak22
04007   real amom0
04008   real amom1
04009   real amom2
04010   real b
04011   real c
04012   real cc
04013   real centr
04014   real cheb12(13)
04015   real cheb24(25)
04016   real, external :: f
04017   real fval(25)
04018   real hlgth
04019   integer i
04020   integer isym
04021   integer k 
04022   integer kp
04023   integer krul
04024   integer neval
04025   real p2
04026   real p3
04027   real p4
04028   real, external :: qwgtc
04029   real resabs
04030   real resasc
04031   real result
04032   real res12
04033   real res24
04034   real u
04035   real, parameter, dimension ( 11 ) :: x = (/ 
04036     9.914448613738104e-01, 9.659258262890683e-01, 
04037     9.238795325112868e-01, 8.660254037844386e-01, 
04038     7.933533402912352e-01, 7.071067811865475e-01, 
04039     6.087614290087206e-01, 5.000000000000000e-01, 
04040     3.826834323650898e-01, 2.588190451025208e-01, 
04041     1.305261922200516e-01 /)
04042 !
04043 !  Check the position of C.
04044 !
04045   cc = ( 2.0e+00 * c - b - a ) / ( b - a )
04046 !
04047 !  Apply the 15-point Gauss-Kronrod scheme.
04048 !
04049   if ( abs ( cc ) >= 1.1e+00 ) then
04050     krul = krul - 1
04051     call qk15w ( f, qwgtc, c, p2, p3, p4, kp, a, b, result, abserr, &
04052       resabs, resasc )
04053     neval = 15
04054     if ( resasc == abserr ) then
04055       krul = krul+1
04056     end if
04057     return
04058   end if
04059 !
04060 !  Use the generalized Clenshaw-Curtis method.
04061 !
04062   hlgth = 5.0e-01 * ( b - a )
04063   centr = 5.0e-01 * ( b + a )
04064   neval = 25
04065   fval(1) = 5.0e-01 * f(hlgth+centr)
04066   fval(13) = f(centr)
04067   fval(25) = 5.0e-01 * f(centr-hlgth)
04068 
04069   do i = 2, 12
04070     u = hlgth * x(i-1)
04071     isym = 26 - i
04072     fval(i) = f(u+centr)
04073     fval(isym) = f(centr-u)
04074   end do
04075 !
04076 !  Compute the Chebyshev series expansion.
04077 !
04078   call qcheb ( x, fval, cheb12, cheb24 )
04079 !
04080 !  The modified Chebyshev moments are computed by forward
04081 !  recursion, using AMOM0 and AMOM1 as starting values.
04082 !
04083   amom0 = log ( abs ( ( 1.0e+00 - cc ) / ( 1.0e+00 + cc ) ) )
04084   amom1 = 2.0e+00 + cc * amom0
04085   res12 = cheb12(1) * amom0 + cheb12(2) * amom1
04086   res24 = cheb24(1) * amom0 + cheb24(2) * amom1
04087 
04088   do k = 3, 13
04089     amom2 = 2.0e+00 * cc * amom1 - amom0
04090     ak22 = ( k - 2 ) * ( k - 2 )
04091     if ( ( k / 2 ) * 2 == k ) then
04092       amom2 = amom2 - 4.0e+00 / ( ak22 - 1.0e+00 )
04093     end if
04094     res12 = res12 + cheb12(k) * amom2
04095     res24 = res24 + cheb24(k) * amom2
04096     amom0 = amom1
04097     amom1 = amom2
04098   end do
04099 
04100   do k = 14, 25
04101     amom2 = 2.0e+00 * cc * amom1 - amom0
04102     ak22 = ( k - 2 ) * ( k - 2 )
04103     if ( ( k / 2 ) * 2 == k ) then
04104       amom2 = amom2 - 4.0e+00 / ( ak22 - 1.0e+00 )
04105     end if
04106     res24 = res24 + cheb24(k) * amom2
04107     amom0 = amom1
04108     amom1 = amom2
04109   end do
04110 
04111   result = res24
04112   abserr = abs ( res24 - res12 )
04113 
04114   return
04115 end
04116 subroutine qc25o ( f, a, b, omega, integr, nrmom, maxp1, ksave, result, &
04117   abserr, neval, resabs, resasc, momcom, chebmo )
04118 
04119 !*****************************************************************************80
04120 !
04121 !! QC25O returns integration rules for integrands with a COS or SIN factor.
04122 !
04123 !  Discussion:
04124 !
04125 !    This routine estimates the integral
04126 !      I = integral of f(x) * w(x) over (a,b)
04127 !    where
04128 !      w(x) = cos(omega*x)
04129 !    or 
04130 !      w(x) = sin(omega*x),
04131 !    and estimates
04132 !      J = integral ( A <= X <= B ) |F(X)| dx.
04133 !
04134 !    For small values of OMEGA or small intervals (a,b) the 15-point
04135 !    Gauss-Kronrod rule is used.  In all other cases a generalized
04136 !    Clenshaw-Curtis method is used, that is, a truncated Chebyshev 
04137 !    expansion of the function F is computed on (a,b), so that the 
04138 !    integrand can be written as a sum of terms of the form W(X)*T(K,X), 
04139 !    where T(K,X) is the Chebyshev polynomial of degree K.  The Chebyshev
04140 !    moments are computed with use of a linear recurrence relation.
04141 !
04142 !  Author:
04143 !
04144 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
04145 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
04146 !
04147 !  Reference:
04148 !
04149 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
04150 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
04151 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
04152 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
04153 !
04154 !  Parameters:
04155 !
04156 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
04157 !      function f ( x )
04158 !      real f
04159 !      real x
04160 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
04161 !
04162 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
04163 !
04164 !    Input, real OMEGA, the parameter in the weight function.
04165 !
04166 !    Input, integer INTEGR, indicates which weight function is to be used
04167 !    = 1, w(x) = cos(omega*x)
04168 !    = 2, w(x) = sin(omega*x)
04169 !
04170 !    ?, integer NRMOM, the length of interval (a,b) is equal to the length
04171 !    of the original integration interval divided by
04172 !    2**nrmom (we suppose that the routine is used in an
04173 !    adaptive integration process, otherwise set
04174 !    nrmom = 0).  nrmom must be zero at the first call.
04175 !
04176 !           maxp1  - integer
04177 !                    gives an upper bound on the number of Chebyshev
04178 !                    moments which can be stored, i.e. for the intervals
04179 !                    of lengths abs(bb-aa)*2**(-l), l = 0,1,2, ...,
04180 !                    maxp1-2.
04181 !
04182 !           ksave  - integer
04183 !                    key which is one when the moments for the
04184 !                    current interval have been computed
04185 !
04186 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
04187 !
04188 !           abserr - real
04189 !                    estimate of the modulus of the absolute
04190 !                    error, which should equal or exceed abs(i-result)
04191 !
04192 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
04193 !
04194 !    Output, real RESABS, approximation to the integral J.
04195 !
04196 !    Output, real RESASC, approximation to the integral of abs(F-I/(B-A)).
04197 !
04198 !         on entry and return
04199 !           momcom - integer
04200 !                    for each interval length we need to compute
04201 !                    the Chebyshev moments. momcom counts the number
04202 !                    of intervals for which these moments have already
04203 !                    been computed. if nrmom < momcom or ksave = 1,
04204 !                    the Chebyshev moments for the interval (a,b)
04205 !                    have already been computed and stored, otherwise
04206 !                    we compute them and we increase momcom.
04207 !
04208 !           chebmo - real
04209 !                    array of dimension at least (maxp1,25) containing
04210 !                    the modified Chebyshev moments for the first momcom
04211 !                    interval lengths
04212 !
04213 !  Local parameters:
04214 !
04215 !    maxp1 gives an upper bound
04216 !           on the number of Chebyshev moments which can be
04217 !           computed, i.e. for the interval (bb-aa), ...,
04218 !           (bb-aa)/2**(maxp1-2).
04219 !           should this number be altered, the first dimension of
04220 !           chebmo needs to be adapted.
04221 !
04222 !    x contains the values cos(k*pi/24)
04223 !           k = 1, ...,11, to be used for the Chebyshev expansion of f
04224 !
04225 !           centr  - mid point of the integration interval
04226 !           hlgth  - half length of the integration interval
04227 !           fval   - value of the function f at the points
04228 !                    (b-a)*0.5*cos(k*pi/12) + (b+a)*0.5
04229 !                    k = 0, ...,24
04230 !           cheb12 - coefficients of the Chebyshev series expansion
04231 !                    of degree 12, for the function f, in the
04232 !                    interval (a,b)
04233 !           cheb24 - coefficients of the Chebyshev series expansion
04234 !                    of degree 24, for the function f, in the
04235 !                    interval (a,b)
04236 !           resc12 - approximation to the integral of
04237 !                    cos(0.5*(b-a)*omega*x)*f(0.5*(b-a)*x+0.5*(b+a))
04238 !                    over (-1,+1), using the Chebyshev series
04239 !                    expansion of degree 12
04240 !           resc24 - approximation to the same integral, using the
04241 !                    Chebyshev series expansion of degree 24
04242 !           ress12 - the analogue of resc12 for the sine
04243 !           ress24 - the analogue of resc24 for the sine
04244 !
04245   implicit none
04246 
04247   integer maxp1
04248 
04249   real a
04250   real abserr
04251   real ac
04252   real an
04253   real an2
04254   real as
04255   real asap
04256   real ass
04257   real b
04258   real centr
04259   real chebmo(maxp1,25)
04260   real cheb12(13)
04261   real cheb24(25)
04262   real conc
04263   real cons
04264   real cospar
04265   real d(28)
04266   real d1(28)
04267   real d2(28)
04268   real d3(28)
04269   real estc
04270   real ests
04271   real, external :: f
04272   real fval(25)
04273   real hlgth
04274   integer i
04275   integer integr
04276   integer isym
04277   integer j
04278   integer k
04279   integer ksave
04280   integer m
04281   integer momcom
04282   integer neval
04283   integer, parameter :: nmac = 28
04284   integer noeq1
04285   integer noequ
04286   integer nrmom
04287   real omega
04288   real parint
04289   real par2
04290   real par22
04291   real p2
04292   real p3
04293   real p4
04294   real, external :: qwgto
04295   real resabs
04296   real resasc
04297   real resc12
04298   real resc24
04299   real ress12
04300   real ress24
04301   real result
04302   real sinpar
04303   real v(28)
04304   real, dimension ( 11 ) :: x = (/ 
04305     9.914448613738104e-01,     9.659258262890683e-01, 
04306     9.238795325112868e-01,     8.660254037844386e-01, 
04307     7.933533402912352e-01,     7.071067811865475e-01, 
04308     6.087614290087206e-01,     5.000000000000000e-01, 
04309     3.826834323650898e-01,     2.588190451025208e-01, 
04310     1.305261922200516e-01 /)
04311 
04312   centr = 5.0e-01 * ( b + a )
04313   hlgth = 5.0e-01 * ( b - a )
04314   parint = omega * hlgth
04315 !
04316 !  Compute the integral using the 15-point Gauss-Kronrod
04317 !  formula if the value of the parameter in the integrand
04318 !  is small or if the length of the integration interval
04319 !  is less than (bb-aa)/2**(maxp1-2), where (aa,bb) is the
04320 !  original integration interval.
04321 !
04322   if ( abs ( parint ) <= 2.0e+00 ) then
04323 
04324     call qk15w ( f, qwgto, omega, p2, p3, p4, integr, a, b, result, &
04325       abserr, resabs, resasc )
04326 
04327     neval = 15
04328     return
04329 
04330   end if
04331 !
04332 !  Compute the integral using the generalized clenshaw-curtis method.
04333 !
04334   conc = hlgth * cos(centr*omega)
04335   cons = hlgth * sin(centr*omega)
04336   resasc = huge ( resasc )
04337   neval = 25
04338 !
04339 !  Check whether the Chebyshev moments for this interval
04340 !  have already been computed.
04341 !
04342   if ( nrmom < momcom .or. ksave == 1 ) then
04343     go to 140
04344   end if
04345 !
04346 !  Compute a new set of Chebyshev moments.
04347 !
04348   m = momcom + 1
04349   par2 = parint * parint
04350   par22 = par2 + 2.0e+00
04351   sinpar = sin(parint)
04352   cospar = cos(parint)
04353 !
04354 !  Compute the Chebyshev moments with respect to cosine.
04355 !
04356   v(1) = 2.0e+00 * sinpar / parint
04357   v(2) = (8.0e+00*cospar+(par2+par2-8.0e+00)*sinpar/ parint)/par2
04358   v(3) = (3.2e+01*(par2-1.2e+01)*cospar+(2.0e+00* &
04359      ((par2-8.0e+01)*par2+1.92e+02)*sinpar)/ &
04360      parint)/(par2*par2)
04361   ac = 8.0e+00*cospar
04362   as = 2.4e+01*parint*sinpar
04363 
04364   if ( abs ( parint ) > 2.4e+01 ) then
04365     go to 70
04366   end if
04367 !
04368 !  Compute the Chebyshev moments as the solutions of a boundary value 
04369 !  problem with one initial value (v(3)) and one end value computed
04370 !  using an asymptotic formula.
04371 !
04372   noequ = nmac-3
04373   noeq1 = noequ-1
04374   an = 6.0e+00
04375 
04376   do k = 1, noeq1
04377     an2 = an*an
04378     d(k) = -2.0e+00*(an2-4.0e+00) * (par22-an2-an2)
04379     d2(k) = (an-1.0e+00)*(an-2.0e+00) * par2
04380     d1(k) = (an+3.0e+00)*(an+4.0e+00) * par2
04381     v(k+3) = as-(an2-4.0e+00) * ac
04382     an = an+2.0e+00
04383   end do
04384 
04385   an2 = an*an
04386   d(noequ) = -2.0e+00*(an2-4.0e+00) * (par22-an2-an2)
04387   v(noequ+3) = as - ( an2 - 4.0e+00 ) * ac
04388   v(4) = v(4) - 5.6e+01 * par2 * v(3)
04389   ass = parint * sinpar
04390   asap = (((((2.10e+02*par2-1.0e+00)*cospar-(1.05e+02*par2 &
04391      -6.3e+01)*ass)/an2-(1.0e+00-1.5e+01*par2)*cospar &
04392      +1.5e+01*ass)/an2-cospar+3.0e+00*ass)/an2-cospar)/an2
04393   v(noequ+3) = v(noequ+3)-2.0e+00*asap*par2*(an-1.0e+00)* &
04394       (an-2.0e+00)
04395 !
04396 !  Solve the tridiagonal system by means of Gaussian
04397 !  elimination with partial pivoting.
04398 !
04399   d3(1:noequ) = 0.0e+00
04400 
04401   d2(noequ) = 0.0e+00
04402 
04403   do i = 1, noeq1
04404 
04405     if ( abs(d1(i)) > abs(d(i)) ) then
04406       an = d1(i)
04407       d1(i) = d(i)
04408       d(i) = an
04409       an = d2(i)
04410       d2(i) = d(i+1)
04411       d(i+1) = an
04412       d3(i) = d2(i+1)
04413       d2(i+1) = 0.0e+00
04414       an = v(i+4)
04415       v(i+4) = v(i+3)
04416       v(i+3) = an
04417     end if
04418 
04419     d(i+1) = d(i+1)-d2(i)*d1(i)/d(i)
04420     d2(i+1) = d2(i+1)-d3(i)*d1(i)/d(i)
04421     v(i+4) = v(i+4)-v(i+3)*d1(i)/d(i)
04422 
04423   end do
04424 
04425   v(noequ+3) = v(noequ+3) / d(noequ)
04426   v(noequ+2) = (v(noequ+2)-d2(noeq1)*v(noequ+3))/d(noeq1)
04427 
04428   do i = 2, noeq1
04429     k = noequ-i
04430     v(k+3) = (v(k+3)-d3(k)*v(k+5)-d2(k)*v(k+4))/d(k)
04431   end do
04432 
04433   go to 90
04434 !
04435 !  Compute the Chebyshev moments by means of forward recursion
04436 !
04437 70 continue
04438 
04439   an = 4.0e+00
04440 
04441   do i = 4, 13
04442     an2 = an*an
04443     v(i) = ((an2-4.0e+00)*(2.0e+00*(par22-an2-an2)*v(i-1)-ac) &
04444      +as-par2*(an+1.0e+00)*(an+2.0e+00)*v(i-2))/ &
04445      (par2*(an-1.0e+00)*(an-2.0e+00))
04446     an = an+2.0e+00
04447   end do
04448 
04449 90 continue
04450 
04451   do j = 1, 13
04452     chebmo(m,2*j-1) = v(j)
04453   end do
04454 !
04455 !  Compute the Chebyshev moments with respect to sine.
04456 !
04457   v(1) = 2.0e+00*(sinpar-parint*cospar)/par2
04458   v(2) = (1.8e+01-4.8e+01/par2)*sinpar/par2 &
04459      +(-2.0e+00+4.8e+01/par2)*cospar/parint
04460   ac = -2.4e+01*parint*cospar
04461   as = -8.0e+00*sinpar
04462   chebmo(m,2) = v(1)
04463   chebmo(m,4) = v(2)
04464 
04465   if ( abs(parint) <= 2.4e+01 ) then
04466 
04467     do k = 3, 12
04468       an = k
04469       chebmo(m,2*k) = -sinpar/(an*(2.0e+00*an-2.0e+00)) &
04470                  -2.5e-01*parint*(v(k+1)/an-v(k)/(an-1.0e+00))
04471     end do
04472 !
04473 !  Compute the Chebyshev moments by means of forward recursion.
04474 !
04475   else
04476 
04477     an = 3.0e+00
04478 
04479     do i = 3, 12
04480       an2 = an*an
04481       v(i) = ((an2-4.0e+00)*(2.0e+00*(par22-an2-an2)*v(i-1)+as) &
04482        +ac-par2*(an+1.0e+00)*(an+2.0e+00)*v(i-2)) &
04483        /(par2*(an-1.0e+00)*(an-2.0e+00))
04484       an = an+2.0e+00
04485       chebmo(m,2*i) = v(i)
04486     end do
04487 
04488   end if
04489 
04490 140 continue
04491 
04492   if ( nrmom < momcom ) then
04493     m = nrmom + 1
04494   end if
04495 
04496   if ( momcom < maxp1 - 1 .and. nrmom >= momcom ) then
04497     momcom = momcom + 1
04498   end if
04499 !
04500 !  Compute the coefficients of the Chebyshev expansions
04501 !  of degrees 12 and 24 of the function F.
04502 !
04503   fval(1) = 5.0e-01 * f(centr+hlgth)
04504   fval(13) = f(centr)
04505   fval(25) = 5.0e-01 * f(centr-hlgth)
04506 
04507   do i = 2, 12
04508     isym = 26-i
04509     fval(i) = f(hlgth*x(i-1)+centr)
04510     fval(isym) = f(centr-hlgth*x(i-1))
04511   end do
04512 
04513   call qcheb ( x, fval, cheb12, cheb24 )
04514 !
04515 !  Compute the integral and error estimates.
04516 !
04517   resc12 = cheb12(13) * chebmo(m,13)
04518   ress12 = 0.0e+00
04519   estc = abs ( cheb24(25)*chebmo(m,25))+abs((cheb12(13)- &
04520     cheb24(13))*chebmo(m,13) )
04521   ests = 0.0e+00
04522   k = 11
04523 
04524   do j = 1, 6
04525     resc12 = resc12+cheb12(k)*chebmo(m,k)
04526     ress12 = ress12+cheb12(k+1)*chebmo(m,k+1)
04527     estc = estc+abs((cheb12(k)-cheb24(k))*chebmo(m,k))
04528     ests = ests+abs((cheb12(k+1)-cheb24(k+1))*chebmo(m,k+1))
04529     k = k-2
04530   end do
04531 
04532   resc24 = cheb24(25)*chebmo(m,25)
04533   ress24 = 0.0e+00
04534   resabs = abs(cheb24(25))
04535   k = 23
04536 
04537   do j = 1, 12
04538 
04539     resc24 = resc24+cheb24(k)*chebmo(m,k)
04540     ress24 = ress24+cheb24(k+1)*chebmo(m,k+1)
04541     resabs = resabs+abs(cheb24(k))+abs(cheb24(k+1))
04542 
04543     if ( j <= 5 ) then
04544       estc = estc+abs(cheb24(k)*chebmo(m,k))
04545       ests = ests+abs(cheb24(k+1)*chebmo(m,k+1))
04546     end if
04547 
04548     k = k-2
04549 
04550   end do
04551 
04552   resabs = resabs * abs ( hlgth )
04553 
04554   if ( integr == 1 ) then
04555     result = conc * resc24-cons*ress24
04556     abserr = abs ( conc * estc ) + abs ( cons * ests )
04557   else
04558     result = conc*ress24+cons*resc24
04559     abserr = abs(conc*ests)+abs(cons*estc)
04560   end if
04561 
04562   return
04563 end
04564 subroutine qc25s ( f, a, b, bl, br, alfa, beta, ri, rj, rg, rh, result, &
04565   abserr, resasc, integr, neval )
04566 
04567 !*****************************************************************************80
04568 !
04569 !! QC25S returns rules for algebraico-logarithmic end point singularities.
04570 !
04571 !  Discussion:
04572 !
04573 !    This routine computes 
04574 !      i = integral of F(X) * W(X) over (bl,br), 
04575 !    with error estimate, where the weight function W(X) has a singular
04576 !    behavior of algebraico-logarithmic type at the points
04577 !    a and/or b. 
04578 !
04579 !    The interval (bl,br) is a subinterval of (a,b).
04580 !
04581 !  Author:
04582 !
04583 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
04584 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
04585 !
04586 !  Reference:
04587 !
04588 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
04589 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
04590 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
04591 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
04592 !
04593 !  Parameters:
04594 !
04595 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
04596 !      function f ( x )
04597 !      real f
04598 !      real x
04599 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
04600 !
04601 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
04602 !
04603 !    Input, real BL, BR, the lower and upper limits of integration.
04604 !    A <= BL < BR <= B.
04605 !
04606 !    Input, real ALFA, BETA, parameters in the weight function.
04607 !
04608 !    Input, real RI(25), RJ(25), RG(25), RH(25), modified Chebyshev moments 
04609 !    for the application of the generalized Clenshaw-Curtis method,
04610 !    computed in QMOMO.
04611 !
04612 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral, computed by 
04613 !    using a generalized clenshaw-curtis method if b1 = a or br = b.
04614 !    In all other cases the 15-point Kronrod rule is applied, obtained by
04615 !    optimal addition of abscissae to the 7-point Gauss rule.
04616 !
04617 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
04618 !
04619 !    Output, real RESASC, approximation to the integral of abs(F*W-I/(B-A)).
04620 !
04621 !    Input, integer INTEGR,  determines the weight function
04622 !    1, w(x) = (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta
