04623 !    2, w(x) = (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(x-a)
04624 !    3, w(x) = (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(b-x)
04625 !    4, w(x) = (x-a)**alfa*(b-x)**beta*log(x-a)*log(b-x)
04626 !
04627 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
04628 !
04629 !  Local Parameters:
04630 !
04631 !           fval   - value of the function f at the points
04632 !                    (br-bl)*0.5*cos(k*pi/24)+(br+bl)*0.5
04633 !                    k = 0, ..., 24
04634 !           cheb12 - coefficients of the Chebyshev series expansion
04635 !                    of degree 12, for the function f, in the interval
04636 !                    (bl,br)
04637 !           cheb24 - coefficients of the Chebyshev series expansion
04638 !                    of degree 24, for the function f, in the interval
04639 !                    (bl,br)
04640 !           res12  - approximation to the integral obtained from cheb12
04641 !           res24  - approximation to the integral obtained from cheb24
04642 !           qwgts  - external function subprogram defining the four
04643 !                    possible weight functions
04644 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval (bl,br)
04645 !           centr  - mid point of the interval (bl,br)
04646 !
04647 !           the vector x contains the values cos(k*pi/24)
04648 !           k = 1, ..., 11, to be used for the computation of the
04649 !           Chebyshev series expansion of f.
04650 !
04651   implicit none
04652 
04653   real a
04654   real abserr
04655   real alfa
04656   real b
04657   real beta
04658   real bl
04659   real br
04660   real centr
04661   real cheb12(13)
04662   real cheb24(25)
04663   real dc
04664   real, external :: f
04665   real factor
04666   real fix
04667   real fval(25)
04668   real hlgth
04669   integer i
04670   integer integr
04671   integer isym
04672   integer neval
04673   real, external :: qwgts
04674   real resabs
04675   real resasc
04676   real result
04677   real res12
04678   real res24
04679   real rg(25)
04680   real rh(25)
04681   real ri(25)
04682   real rj(25)
04683   real u
04684   real, dimension ( 11 ) :: x = (/ 
04685     9.914448613738104e-01,     9.659258262890683e-01, 
04686     9.238795325112868e-01,     8.660254037844386e-01, 
04687     7.933533402912352e-01,     7.071067811865475e-01, 
04688     6.087614290087206e-01,     5.000000000000000e-01, 
04689     3.826834323650898e-01,     2.588190451025208e-01, 
04690     1.305261922200516e-01 /)
04691 
04692   neval = 25
04693 
04694   if ( bl == a .and. (alfa /= 0.0e+00 .or. integr == 2 .or. integr == 4)) then
04695     go to 10
04696   end if
04697 
04698   if ( br == b .and. (beta /= 0.0e+00 .or. integr == 3 .or. integr == 4)) &
04699     go to 140
04700 !
04701 !  If a > bl and b < br, apply the 15-point Gauss-Kronrod scheme.
04702 !
04703   call qk15w ( f, qwgts, a, b, alfa, beta, integr, bl, br, result, abserr, &
04704     resabs, resasc )
04705 
04706   neval = 15
04707   return
04708 !
04709 !  This part of the program is executed only if a = bl.
04710 !
04711 !  Compute the Chebyshev series expansion of the function
04712 !  f1 = (0.5*(b+b-br-a)-0.5*(br-a)*x)**beta*f(0.5*(br-a)*x+0.5*(br+a))
04713 !
04714 10 continue
04715 
04716   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(br-bl)
04717   centr = 5.0e-01*(br+bl)
04718   fix = b-centr
04719   fval(1) = 5.0e-01*f(hlgth+centr)*(fix-hlgth)**beta
04720   fval(13) = f(centr)*(fix**beta)
04721   fval(25) = 5.0e-01*f(centr-hlgth)*(fix+hlgth)**beta
04722 
04723   do i = 2, 12
04724     u = hlgth*x(i-1)
04725     isym = 26-i
04726     fval(i) = f(u+centr)*(fix-u)**beta
04727     fval(isym) = f(centr-u)*(fix+u)**beta
04728   end do
04729 
04730   factor = hlgth**(alfa+1.0e+00)
04731   result = 0.0e+00
04732   abserr = 0.0e+00
04733   res12 = 0.0e+00
04734   res24 = 0.0e+00
04735 
04736   if ( integr > 2 ) go to 70
04737 
04738   call qcheb ( x, fval, cheb12, cheb24 )
04739 !
04740 !  integr = 1  (or 2)
04741 !
04742   do i = 1, 13
04743     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*ri(i)
04744     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*ri(i)
04745   end do
04746 
04747   do i = 14, 25
04748     res24 = res24 + cheb24(i) * ri(i)
04749   end do
04750 
04751   if ( integr == 1 ) go to 130
04752 !
04753 !  integr = 2
04754 !
04755   dc = log ( br - bl )
04756   result = res24 * dc
04757   abserr = abs((res24-res12)*dc)
04758   res12 = 0.0e+00
04759   res24 = 0.0e+00
04760 
04761   do i = 1, 13
04762     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*rg(i)
04763     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rg(i)
04764   end do
04765 
04766   do i = 14, 25
04767     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rg(i)
04768   end do
04769 
04770   go to 130
04771 !
04772 !  Compute the Chebyshev series expansion of the function
04773 !  F4 = f1*log(0.5*(b+b-br-a)-0.5*(br-a)*x)
04774 !
04775 70 continue
04776 
04777   fval(1) = fval(1) * log ( fix - hlgth )
04778   fval(13) = fval(13) * log ( fix )
04779   fval(25) = fval(25) * log ( fix + hlgth )
04780 
04781   do i = 2, 12
04782     u = hlgth*x(i-1)
04783     isym = 26-i
04784     fval(i) = fval(i) * log ( fix - u )
04785     fval(isym) = fval(isym) * log ( fix + u )
04786   end do
04787 
04788   call qcheb ( x, fval, cheb12, cheb24 )
04789 !
04790 !  integr = 3  (or 4)
04791 !
04792   do i = 1, 13
04793     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*ri(i)
04794     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*ri(i)
04795   end do
04796 
04797   do i = 14, 25
04798     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*ri(i)
04799   end do
04800 
04801   if ( integr == 3 ) then
04802     go to 130
04803   end if
04804 !
04805 !  integr = 4
04806 !
04807   dc = log ( br - bl )
04808   result = res24*dc
04809   abserr = abs((res24-res12)*dc)
04810   res12 = 0.0e+00
04811   res24 = 0.0e+00
04812 
04813   do i = 1, 13
04814     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*rg(i)
04815     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rg(i)
04816   end do
04817 
04818   do i = 14, 25
04819     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rg(i)
04820   end do
04821 
04822 130 continue
04823 
04824   result = (result+res24)*factor
04825   abserr = (abserr+abs(res24-res12))*factor
04826   go to 270
04827 !
04828 !  This part of the program is executed only if b = br.
04829 !
04830 !  Compute the Chebyshev series expansion of the function
04831 !  f2 = (0.5*(b+bl-a-a)+0.5*(b-bl)*x)**alfa*f(0.5*(b-bl)*x+0.5*(b+bl))
04832 !
04833 140 continue
04834 
04835   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(br-bl)
04836   centr = 5.0e-01*(br+bl)
04837   fix = centr-a
04838   fval(1) = 5.0e-01*f(hlgth+centr)*(fix+hlgth)**alfa
04839   fval(13) = f(centr)*(fix**alfa)
04840   fval(25) = 5.0e-01*f(centr-hlgth)*(fix-hlgth)**alfa
04841 
04842   do i = 2, 12
04843     u = hlgth*x(i-1)
04844     isym = 26-i
04845     fval(i) = f(u+centr)*(fix+u)**alfa
04846     fval(isym) = f(centr-u)*(fix-u)**alfa
04847   end do
04848 
04849   factor = hlgth**(beta+1.0e+00)
04850   result = 0.0e+00
04851   abserr = 0.0e+00
04852   res12 = 0.0e+00
04853   res24 = 0.0e+00
04854 
04855   if ( integr == 2 .or. integr == 4 ) then
04856     go to 200
04857   end if
04858 !
04859 !  integr = 1  (or 3)
04860 !
04861   call qcheb ( x, fval, cheb12, cheb24 )
04862 
04863   do i = 1, 13
04864     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*rj(i)
04865     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rj(i)
04866   end do
04867 
04868   do i = 14, 25
04869     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rj(i)
04870   end do
04871 
04872   if ( integr == 1 ) go to 260
04873 !
04874 !  integr = 3
04875 !
04876   dc = log ( br - bl )
04877   result = res24*dc
04878   abserr = abs((res24-res12)*dc)
04879   res12 = 0.0e+00
04880   res24 = 0.0e+00
04881 
04882   do i = 1, 13
04883     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*rh(i)
04884     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rh(i)
04885   end do
04886 
04887   do i = 14, 25
04888     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rh(i)
04889   end do
04890 
04891   go to 260
04892 !
04893 !  Compute the Chebyshev series expansion of the function
04894 !  f3 = f2*log(0.5*(b-bl)*x+0.5*(b+bl-a-a))
04895 !
04896 200 continue
04897 
04898   fval(1) = fval(1) * log ( hlgth + fix )
04899   fval(13) = fval(13) * log ( fix )
04900   fval(25) = fval(25) * log ( fix - hlgth )
04901 
04902   do i = 2, 12
04903     u = hlgth*x(i-1)
04904     isym = 26-i
04905     fval(i) = fval(i) * log(u+fix)
04906     fval(isym) = fval(isym) * log(fix-u)
04907   end do
04908 
04909   call qcheb ( x, fval, cheb12, cheb24 )
04910 !
04911 !  integr = 2  (or 4)
04912 !
04913   do i = 1, 13
04914     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*rj(i)
04915     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rj(i)
04916   end do
04917 
04918   do i = 14, 25
04919     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rj(i)
04920   end do
04921 
04922   if ( integr == 2 ) go to 260
04923 
04924   dc = log(br-bl)
04925   result = res24*dc
04926   abserr = abs((res24-res12)*dc)
04927   res12 = 0.0e+00
04928   res24 = 0.0e+00
04929 !
04930 !  integr = 4
04931 !
04932   do i = 1, 13
04933     res12 = res12+cheb12(i)*rh(i)
04934     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rh(i)
04935   end do
04936 
04937   do i = 14, 25
04938     res24 = res24+cheb24(i)*rh(i)
04939   end do
04940 
04941 260 continue
04942 
04943   result = (result+res24)*factor
04944   abserr = (abserr+abs(res24-res12))*factor
04945 
04946 270 continue
04947 
04948   return
04949 end
04950 subroutine qcheb ( x, fval, cheb12, cheb24 )
04951 
04952 !*****************************************************************************80
04953 !
04954 !! QCHEB computes the Chebyshev series expansion.
04955 !
04956 !  Discussion:
04957 !
04958 !    This routine computes the Chebyshev series expansion
04959 !    of degrees 12 and 24 of a function using a fast Fourier transform method
04960 !
04961 !      f(x) = sum(k=1, ...,13) (cheb12(k)*t(k-1,x)),
04962 !      f(x) = sum(k=1, ...,25) (cheb24(k)*t(k-1,x)),
04963 !
04964 !    where T(K,X) is the Chebyshev polynomial of degree K.
04965 !
04966 !  Author:
04967 !
04968 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
04969 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
04970 !
04971 !  Reference:
04972 !
04973 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
04974 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
04975 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
04976 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
04977 !
04978 !  Parameters:
04979 !
04980 !    Input, real X(11), contains the values of COS(K*PI/24), for K = 1 to 11.
04981 !
04982 !    Input/output, real FVAL(25), the function values at the points
04983 !    (b+a+(b-a)*cos(k*pi/24))/2, k = 0, ...,24, where (a,b) is the 
04984 !    approximation interval.  FVAL(1) and FVAL(25) are divided by two
04985 !    These values are destroyed at output.
04986 !
04987 !    Output, real CHEB12(13), the Chebyshev coefficients for degree 12.
04988 !
04989 !    Output, real CHEB24(25), the Chebyshev coefficients for degree 24.
04990 !
04991   implicit none
04992 
04993   real alam
04994   real alam1
04995   real alam2
04996   real cheb12(13)
04997   real cheb24(25)
04998   real fval(25)
04999   integer i
05000   integer j
05001   real part1
05002   real part2
05003   real part3
05004   real v(12)
05005   real x(11)
05006 
05007   do i = 1, 12
05008     j = 26-i
05009     v(i) = fval(i)-fval(j)
05010     fval(i) = fval(i)+fval(j)
05011   end do
05012 
05013   alam1 = v(1)-v(9)
05014   alam2 = x(6)*(v(3)-v(7)-v(11))
05015   cheb12(4) = alam1+alam2
05016   cheb12(10) = alam1-alam2
05017   alam1 = v(2)-v(8)-v(10)
05018   alam2 = v(4)-v(6)-v(12)
05019   alam = x(3)*alam1+x(9)*alam2
05020   cheb24(4) = cheb12(4)+alam
05021   cheb24(22) = cheb12(4)-alam
05022   alam = x(9)*alam1-x(3)*alam2
05023   cheb24(10) = cheb12(10)+alam
05024   cheb24(16) = cheb12(10)-alam
05025   part1 = x(4)*v(5)
05026   part2 = x(8)*v(9)
05027   part3 = x(6)*v(7)
05028   alam1 = v(1)+part1+part2
05029   alam2 = x(2)*v(3)+part3+x(10)*v(11)
05030   cheb12(2) = alam1+alam2
05031   cheb12(12) = alam1-alam2
05032   alam = x(1)*v(2)+x(3)*v(4)+x(5)*v(6)+x(7)*v(8) &
05033     +x(9)*v(10)+x(11)*v(12)
05034   cheb24(2) = cheb12(2)+alam
05035   cheb24(24) = cheb12(2)-alam
05036   alam = x(11)*v(2)-x(9)*v(4)+x(7)*v(6)-x(5)*v(8) &
05037     +x(3)*v(10)-x(1)*v(12)
05038   cheb24(12) = cheb12(12)+alam
05039   cheb24(14) = cheb12(12)-alam
05040   alam1 = v(1)-part1+part2
05041   alam2 = x(10)*v(3)-part3+x(2)*v(11)
05042   cheb12(6) = alam1+alam2
05043   cheb12(8) = alam1-alam2
05044   alam = x(5)*v(2)-x(9)*v(4)-x(1)*v(6) &
05045     -x(11)*v(8)+x(3)*v(10)+x(7)*v(12)
05046   cheb24(6) = cheb12(6)+alam
05047   cheb24(20) = cheb12(6)-alam
05048   alam = x(7)*v(2)-x(3)*v(4)-x(11)*v(6)+x(1)*v(8) &
05049     -x(9)*v(10)-x(5)*v(12)
05050   cheb24(8) = cheb12(8)+alam
05051   cheb24(18) = cheb12(8)-alam
05052 
05053   do i = 1, 6
05054     j = 14-i
05055     v(i) = fval(i)-fval(j)
05056     fval(i) = fval(i)+fval(j)
05057   end do
05058 
05059   alam1 = v(1)+x(8)*v(5)
05060   alam2 = x(4)*v(3)
05061   cheb12(3) = alam1+alam2
05062   cheb12(11) = alam1-alam2
05063   cheb12(7) = v(1)-v(5)
05064   alam = x(2)*v(2)+x(6)*v(4)+x(10)*v(6)
05065   cheb24(3) = cheb12(3)+alam
05066   cheb24(23) = cheb12(3)-alam
05067   alam = x(6)*(v(2)-v(4)-v(6))
05068   cheb24(7) = cheb12(7)+alam
05069   cheb24(19) = cheb12(7)-alam
05070   alam = x(10)*v(2)-x(6)*v(4)+x(2)*v(6)
05071   cheb24(11) = cheb12(11)+alam
05072   cheb24(15) = cheb12(11)-alam
05073 
05074   do i = 1, 3
05075     j = 8-i
05076     v(i) = fval(i)-fval(j)
05077     fval(i) = fval(i)+fval(j)
05078   end do
05079 
05080   cheb12(5) = v(1)+x(8)*v(3)
05081   cheb12(9) = fval(1)-x(8)*fval(3)
05082   alam = x(4)*v(2)
05083   cheb24(5) = cheb12(5)+alam
05084   cheb24(21) = cheb12(5)-alam
05085   alam = x(8)*fval(2)-fval(4)
05086   cheb24(9) = cheb12(9)+alam
05087   cheb24(17) = cheb12(9)-alam
05088   cheb12(1) = fval(1)+fval(3)
05089   alam = fval(2)+fval(4)
05090   cheb24(1) = cheb12(1)+alam
05091   cheb24(25) = cheb12(1)-alam
05092   cheb12(13) = v(1)-v(3)
05093   cheb24(13) = cheb12(13)
05094   alam = 1.0e+00/6.0e+00
05095 
05096   do i = 2, 12
05097     cheb12(i) = cheb12(i)*alam
05098   end do
05099 
05100   alam = 5.0e-01*alam
05101   cheb12(1) = cheb12(1)*alam
05102   cheb12(13) = cheb12(13)*alam
05103 
05104   do i = 2, 24
05105     cheb24(i) = cheb24(i)*alam
05106   end do
05107 
05108   cheb24(1) = 0.5E+00 * alam*cheb24(1)
05109   cheb24(25) = 0.5E+00 * alam*cheb24(25)
05110 
05111   return
05112 end
05113 subroutine qextr ( n, epstab, result, abserr, res3la, nres )
05114 
05115 !*****************************************************************************80
05116 !
05117 !! QEXTR carries out the Epsilon extrapolation algorithm.
05118 !
05119 !  Discussion:
05120 !
05121 !    The routine determines the limit of a given sequence of approximations, 
05122 !    by means of the epsilon algorithm of P. Wynn.  An estimate of the 
05123 !    absolute error is also given.  The condensed epsilon table is computed.
05124 !    Only those elements needed for the computation of the next diagonal
05125 !    are preserved.
05126 !
05127 !  Author:
05128 !
05129 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
05130 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
05131 !
05132 !  Reference:
05133 !
05134 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
05135 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
05136 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
05137 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
05138 !
05139 !  Parameters:
05140 !
05141 !    Input, integer N, indicates the entry of EPSTAB which contains
05142 !    the new element in the first column of the epsilon table.
05143 !
05144 !    Input/output, real EPSTAB(52), the two lower diagonals of the triangular
05145 !    epsilon table.  The elements are numbered starting at the right-hand 
05146 !    corner of the triangle.
05147 !
05148 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
05149 !
05150 !    Output, real ABSERR, estimate of the absolute error computed from
05151 !    RESULT and the 3 previous results.
05152 !
05153 !    ?, real RES3LA(3), the last 3 results.
05154 !
05155 !    Input/output, integer NRES, the number of calls to the routine.  This
05156 !    should be zero on the first call, and is automatically updated
05157 !    before return.
05158 !
05159 !  Local Parameters:
05160 !
05161 !           e0     - the 4 elements on which the
05162 !           e1       computation of a new element in
05163 !           e2       the epsilon table is based
05164 !           e3                 e0
05165 !                        e3    e1    new
05166 !                              e2
05167 !           newelm - number of elements to be computed in the new
05168 !                    diagonal
05169 !           error  - error = abs(e1-e0)+abs(e2-e1)+abs(new-e2)
05170 !           result - the element in the new diagonal with least value
05171 !                    of error
05172 !           limexp is the maximum number of elements the epsilon table
05173 !           can contain. if this number is reached, the upper diagonal
05174 !           of the epsilon table is deleted.
05175 !
05176   implicit none
05177 
05178   real abserr
05179   real delta1
05180   real delta2
05181   real delta3
05182   real epsinf
05183   real epstab(52)
05184   real error
05185   real err1
05186   real err2
05187   real err3
05188   real e0
05189   real e1
05190   real e1abs
05191   real e2
05192   real e3
05193   integer i
05194   integer ib
05195   integer ib2
05196   integer ie
05197   integer indx
05198   integer k1
05199   integer k2
05200   integer k3
05201   integer limexp
05202   integer n
05203   integer newelm
05204   integer nres
05205   integer num
05206   real res
05207   real result
05208   real res3la(3)
05209   real ss
05210   real tol1
05211   real tol2
05212   real tol3
05213 
05214   nres = nres+1
05215   abserr = huge ( abserr )
05216   result = epstab(n)
05217 
05218   if ( n < 3 ) then
05219     abserr = max ( abserr,0.5e+00* epsilon ( result ) *abs(result))
05220     return
05221   end if
05222 
05223   limexp = 50
05224   epstab(n+2) = epstab(n)
05225   newelm = (n-1)/2
05226   epstab(n) = huge ( epstab(n) )
05227   num = n
05228   k1 = n
05229 
05230   do i = 1, newelm
05231 
05232     k2 = k1-1
05233     k3 = k1-2
05234     res = epstab(k1+2)
05235     e0 = epstab(k3)
05236     e1 = epstab(k2)
05237     e2 = res
05238     e1abs = abs(e1)
05239     delta2 = e2-e1
05240     err2 = abs(delta2)
05241     tol2 = max ( abs(e2),e1abs)* epsilon ( e2 )
05242     delta3 = e1-e0
05243     err3 = abs(delta3)
05244     tol3 = max ( e1abs,abs(e0))* epsilon ( e0 )
05245 !
05246 !  If e0, e1 and e2 are equal to within machine accuracy, convergence 
05247 !  is assumed.
05248 !
05249     if ( err2 <= tol2 .and. err3 <= tol3 ) then
05250       result = res
05251       abserr = err2+err3
05252       abserr = max ( abserr,0.5e+00* epsilon ( result ) *abs(result))
05253       return
05254     end if
05255 
05256     e3 = epstab(k1)
05257     epstab(k1) = e1
05258     delta1 = e1-e3
05259     err1 = abs(delta1)
05260     tol1 = max ( e1abs,abs(e3))* epsilon ( e3 )
05261 !
05262 !  If two elements are very close to each other, omit a part
05263 !  of the table by adjusting the value of N.
05264 !
05265     if ( err1 <= tol1 .or. err2 <= tol2 .or. err3 <= tol3 ) go to 20
05266 
05267     ss = 1.0e+00/delta1+1.0e+00/delta2-1.0e+00/delta3
05268     epsinf = abs ( ss*e1 )
05269 !
05270 !  Test to detect irregular behavior in the table, and
05271 !  eventually omit a part of the table adjusting the value of N.
05272 !
05273     if ( epsinf > 1.0e-04 ) go to 30
05274 
05275 20  continue
05276 
05277     n = i+i-1
05278     exit
05279 !
05280 !  Compute a new element and eventually adjust the value of RESULT.
05281 !
05282 30  continue
05283 
05284     res = e1+1.0e+00/ss
05285     epstab(k1) = res
05286     k1 = k1-2
05287     error = err2+abs(res-e2)+err3
05288 
05289     if ( error <= abserr ) then
05290       abserr = error
05291       result = res
05292     end if
05293 
05294   end do
05295 !
05296 !  Shift the table.
05297 !
05298   if ( n == limexp ) then
05299     n = 2*(limexp/2)-1
05300   end if
05301 
05302   if ( (num/2)*2 == num ) then
05303     ib = 2
05304   else
05305     ib = 1
05306   end if
05307 
05308   ie = newelm+1
05309 
05310   do i = 1, ie
05311     ib2 = ib+2
05312     epstab(ib) = epstab(ib2)
05313     ib = ib2
05314   end do
05315 
05316   if ( num /= n ) then
05317 
05318     indx = num-n+1
05319 
05320     do i = 1, n
05321       epstab(i)= epstab(indx)
05322       indx = indx+1
05323     end do
05324 
05325   end if
05326 
05327   if ( nres < 4 ) then
05328     res3la(nres) = result
05329     abserr = huge ( abserr )
05330   else
05331     abserr = abs(result-res3la(3))+abs(result-res3la(2)) &
05332       +abs(result-res3la(1))
05333     res3la(1) = res3la(2)
05334     res3la(2) = res3la(3)
05335     res3la(3) = result
05336   end if
05337 
05338   abserr = max ( abserr,0.5e+00* epsilon ( result ) *abs(result))
05339 
05340   return
05341 end
05342 subroutine qfour ( f, a, b, omega, integr, epsabs, epsrel, limit, icall, &
05343   maxp1, result, abserr, neval, ier, alist, blist, rlist, elist, iord, &
05344   nnlog, momcom, chebmo )
05345 
05346 !*****************************************************************************80
05347 !
05348 !! QFOUR estimates the integrals of oscillatory functions.
05349 !
05350 !  Discussion:
05351 !
05352 !    This routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral
05353 !      I = integral of F(X) * COS(OMEGA*X) 
05354 !    or
05355 !      I = integral of F(X) * SIN(OMEGA*X) 
05356 !    over (A,B), hopefully satisfying:
05357 !      | I - RESULT | <= max ( epsabs, epsrel * |I| ) ).
05358 !
05359 !    QFOUR is called by QAWO and QAWF.  It can also be called directly in 
05360 !    a user-written program.  In the latter case it is possible for the 
05361 !    user to determine the first dimension of array CHEBMO(MAXP1,25).
05362 !    See also parameter description of MAXP1.  Additionally see
05363 !    parameter description of ICALL for eventually re-using
05364 !    Chebyshev moments computed during former call on subinterval
05365 !    of equal length abs(B-A).
05366 !
05367 !  Author:
05368 !
05369 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
05370 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
05371 !
05372 !  Reference:
05373 !
05374 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
05375 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
05376 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
05377 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
05378 !
05379 !  Parameters:
05380 !
05381 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
05382 !      function f ( x )
05383 !      real f
05384 !      real x
05385 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
05386 !
05387 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
05388 !
05389 !    Input, real OMEGA, the multiplier of X in the weight function.
05390 !
05391 !    Input, integer INTEGR, indicates the weight functions to be used.
05392 !    = 1, w(x) = cos(omega*x)
05393 !    = 2, w(x) = sin(omega*x)
05394 !
05395 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
05396 !
05397 !    Input, integer LIMIT, the maximum number of subintervals of [A,B]
05398 !    that can be generated.
05399 !
05400 !    icall  - integer
05401 !                     if qfour is to be used only once, ICALL must
05402 !                     be set to 1.  assume that during this call, the
05403 !                     Chebyshev moments (for clenshaw-curtis integration
05404 !                     of degree 24) have been computed for intervals of
05405 !                     lenghts (abs(b-a))*2**(-l), l=0,1,2,...momcom-1.
05406 !                     the Chebyshev moments already computed can be
05407 !                     re-used in subsequent calls, if qfour must be
05408 !                     called twice or more times on intervals of the
05409 !                     same length abs(b-a). from the second call on, one
05410 !                     has to put then ICALL > 1.
05411 !                     if ICALL < 1, the routine will end with ier = 6.
05412 !
05413 !            maxp1  - integer
05414 !                     gives an upper bound on the number of
05415 !                     Chebyshev moments which can be stored, i.e.
05416 !                     for the intervals of lenghts abs(b-a)*2**(-l),
05417 !                     l=0,1, ..., maxp1-2, maxp1 >= 1.
05418 !                     if maxp1 < 1, the routine will end with ier = 6.
05419 !                     increasing (decreasing) the value of maxp1
05420 !                     decreases (increases) the computational time but
05421 !                     increases (decreases) the required memory space.
05422 !
05423 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
05424 !
05425 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
05426 !
05427 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
05428 !
05429 !            ier    - integer
05430 !                     ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
05431 !                             routine. it is assumed that the
05432 !                             requested accuracy has been achieved.
05433 !                   - ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine.
05434 !                             the estimates for integral and error are
05435 !                             less reliable. it is assumed that the
05436 !                             requested accuracy has not been achieved.
05437 !                     ier = 1 maximum number of subdivisions allowed
05438 !                             has been achieved. one can allow more
05439 !                             subdivisions by increasing the value of
05440 !                             limit (and taking according dimension
05441 !                             adjustments into account). however, if
05442 !                             this yields no improvement it is advised
05443 !                             to analyze the integrand, in order to
05444 !                             determine the integration difficulties.
05445 !                             if the position of a local difficulty can
05446 !                             be determined (e.g. singularity,
05447 !                             discontinuity within the interval) one
05448 !                             will probably gain from splitting up the
05449 !                             interval at this point and calling the
05450 !                             integrator on the subranges. if possible,
05451 !                             an appropriate special-purpose integrator
05452 !                             should be used which is designed for
05453 !                             handling the type of difficulty involved.
05454 !                         = 2 the occurrence of roundoff error is
05455 !                             detected, which prevents the requested
05456 !                             tolerance from being achieved.
05457 !                             the error may be under-estimated.
05458 !                         = 3 extremely bad integrand behavior occurs
05459 !                             at some points of the integration
05460 !                             interval.
05461 !                         = 4 the algorithm does not converge. roundoff
05462 !                             error is detected in the extrapolation
05463 !                             table. it is presumed that the requested
05464 !                             tolerance cannot be achieved due to
05465 !                             roundoff in the extrapolation table, and
05466 !                             that the returned result is the best which
05467 !                             can be obtained.
05468 !                         = 5 the integral is probably divergent, or
05469 !                             slowly convergent. it must be noted that
05470 !                             divergence can occur with any other value
05471 !                             of ier > 0.
05472 !                         = 6 the input is invalid, because
05473 !                             epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
05474 !                             or (integr /= 1 and integr /= 2) or
05475 !                             ICALL < 1 or maxp1 < 1.
05476 !                             result, abserr, neval, last, rlist(1),
05477 !                             elist(1), iord(1) and nnlog(1) are set to
05478 !                             zero. alist(1) and blist(1) are set to a
05479 !                             and b respectively.
05480 !
05481 !    Workspace, real ALIST(LIMIT), BLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 
05482 !    through LAST the left and right ends of the partition subintervals.
05483 !
05484 !    Workspace, real RLIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
05485 !    the integral approximations on the subintervals.
05486 !
05487 !    Workspace, real ELIST(LIMIT), contains in entries 1 through LAST
05488 !    the absolute error estimates on the subintervals.
05489 !
05490 !            iord   - integer
05491 !                     vector of dimension at least limit, the first k
05492 !                     elements of which are pointers to the error
05493 !                     estimates over the subintervals, such that
05494 !                     elist(iord(1)), ..., elist(iord(k)), form
05495 !                     a decreasing sequence, with k = last
05496 !                     if last <= (limit/2+2), and
05497 !                     k = limit+1-last otherwise.
05498 !
05499 !            nnlog  - integer
05500 !                     vector of dimension at least limit, indicating the
05501 !                     subdivision levels of the subintervals, i.e.
05502 !                     iwork(i) = l means that the subinterval numbered
05503 !                     i is of length abs(b-a)*2**(1-l)
05504 !
05505 !         on entry and return
05506 !            momcom - integer
05507 !                     indicating that the Chebyshev moments have been
05508 !                     computed for intervals of lengths
05509 !                     (abs(b-a))*2**(-l), l=0,1,2, ..., momcom-1,
05510 !                     momcom < maxp1
05511 !
05512 !            chebmo - real
05513 !                     array of dimension (maxp1,25) containing the
05514 !                     Chebyshev moments
05515 !
05516 !  Local Parameters:
05517 !
05518 !           alist     - list of left end points of all subintervals
05519 !                       considered up to now
05520 !           blist     - list of right end points of all subintervals
05521 !                       considered up to now
05522 !           rlist(i)  - approximation to the integral over
05523 !                       (alist(i),blist(i))
05524 !           rlist2    - array of dimension at least limexp+2 containing
05525 !                       the part of the epsilon table which is still
05526 !                       needed for further computations
05527 !           elist(i)  - error estimate applying to rlist(i)
05528 !           maxerr    - pointer to the interval with largest error
05529 !                       estimate
05530 !           errmax    - elist(maxerr)
05531 !           erlast    - error on the interval currently subdivided
05532 !           area      - sum of the integrals over the subintervals
05533 !           errsum    - sum of the errors over the subintervals
05534 !           errbnd    - requested accuracy max(epsabs,epsrel*
05535 !                       abs(result))
05536 !           *****1    - variable for the left subinterval
05537 !           *****2    - variable for the right subinterval
05538 !           last      - index for subdivision
05539 !           nres      - number of calls to the extrapolation routine
05540 !           numrl2    - number of elements in rlist2. if an appropriate
05541 !                       approximation to the compounded integral has
05542 !                       been obtained it is put in rlist2(numrl2) after
05543 !                       numrl2 has been increased by one
05544 !           small     - length of the smallest interval considered
05545 !                       up to now, multiplied by 1.5
05546 !           erlarg    - sum of the errors over the intervals larger
05547 !                       than the smallest interval considered up to now
05548 !           extrap    - logical variable denoting that the routine is
05549 !                       attempting to perform extrapolation, i.e. before
05550 !                       subdividing the smallest interval we try to
05551 !                       decrease the value of erlarg
05552 !           noext     - logical variable denoting that extrapolation
05553 !                       is no longer allowed (true value)
05554 !
05555   implicit none
05556 
05557   integer limit
05558   integer maxp1
05559 
05560   real a
05561   real abseps
05562   real abserr
05563   real alist(limit)
05564   real area
05565   real area1
05566   real area12
05567   real area2
05568   real a1
05569   real a2
05570   real b
05571   real blist(limit)
05572   real b1
05573   real b2
05574   real chebmo(maxp1,25)
05575   real correc
05576   real defab1
05577   real defab2
05578   real defabs
05579   real domega
05580   real dres
05581   real elist(limit)
05582   real epsabs
05583   real epsrel
05584   real erlarg
05585   real erlast
05586   real errbnd
05587   real errmax
05588   real error1
05589   real erro12
05590   real error2
05591   real errsum
05592   real ertest
05593   logical extall
05594   logical extrap
05595   real, external :: f
05596   integer icall
05597   integer id
05598   integer ier
05599   integer ierro
05600   integer integr
05601   integer iord(limit)
05602   integer iroff1
05603   integer iroff2
05604   integer iroff3
05605   integer jupbnd
05606   integer k
05607   integer ksgn
05608   integer ktmin
05609   integer last
05610   integer maxerr
05611   integer momcom
05612   integer nev
05613   integer neval
05614   integer nnlog(limit)
05615   logical noext
05616   integer nres
05617   integer nrmax
05618   integer nrmom
05619   integer numrl2
05620   real omega
05621   real resabs
05622   real reseps
05623   real result
05624   real res3la(3)
05625   real rlist(limit)
05626   real rlist2(52)
05627   real small
05628   real width
05629 !
05630 !  the dimension of rlist2 is determined by  the value of
05631 !  limexp in QEXTR (rlist2 should be of dimension
05632 !  (limexp+2) at least).
05633 !
05634 !  Test on validity of parameters.
05635 !
05636   ier = 0
05637   neval = 0
05638   last = 0
05639   result = 0.0e+00
05640   abserr = 0.0e+00
05641   alist(1) = a
05642   blist(1) = b
05643   rlist(1) = 0.0e+00
05644   elist(1) = 0.0e+00
05645   iord(1) = 0
05646   nnlog(1) = 0
05647 
05648   if ( (integr /= 1.and.integr /= 2) .or. (epsabs < 0.0e+00.and. &
05649     epsrel < 0.0e+00) .or. icall < 1 .or. maxp1 < 1 ) then
05650     ier = 6
05651     return
05652   end if
05653 !
05654 !  First approximation to the integral.
05655 !
05656   domega = abs ( omega )
05657   nrmom = 0
05658 
05659   if ( icall <= 1 ) then
05660     momcom = 0
05661   end if
05662 
05663   call qc25o ( f, a, b, domega, integr, nrmom, maxp1, 0, result, abserr, &
05664     neval, defabs, resabs, momcom, chebmo )
05665 !
05666 !  Test on accuracy.
05667 !
05668   dres = abs(result)
05669   errbnd = max ( epsabs,epsrel*dres)
05670   rlist(1) = result
05671   elist(1) = abserr
05672   iord(1) = 1
05673   if ( abserr <= 1.0e+02* epsilon ( defabs ) *defabs .and. &
05674     abserr > errbnd ) ier = 2
05675 
05676   if ( limit == 1 ) then
05677     ier = 1
05678   end if
05679 
05680   if ( ier /= 0 .or. abserr <= errbnd ) then
05681     go to 200
05682   end if
05683 !
05684 !  Initializations
05685 !
05686   errmax = abserr
05687   maxerr = 1
05688   area = result
05689   errsum = abserr
05690   abserr = huge ( abserr )
05691   nrmax = 1
05692   extrap = .false.
05693   noext = .false.
05694   ierro = 0
05695   iroff1 = 0
05696   iroff2 = 0
05697   iroff3 = 0
05698   ktmin = 0
05699   small = abs(b-a)*7.5e-01
05700   nres = 0
05701   numrl2 = 0
05702   extall = .false.
05703 
05704   if ( 5.0e-01*abs(b-a)*domega <= 2.0e+00) then
05705     numrl2 = 1
05706     extall = .true.
05707     rlist2(1) = result
05708   end if
05709 
05710   if ( 2.5e-01 * abs(b-a) * domega <= 2.0e+00 ) then
05711     extall = .true.
05712   end if
05713 
05714   if ( dres >= (1.0e+00-5.0e+01* epsilon ( defabs ) )*defabs ) then
05715     ksgn = 1
05716   else
05717     ksgn = -1
05718   end if
05719 !
05720 !  main do-loop
05721 !
05722   do last = 2, limit
05723 !
05724 !  Bisect the subinterval with the nrmax-th largest error estimate.
05725 !
05726     nrmom = nnlog(maxerr)+1
05727     a1 = alist(maxerr)
05728     b1 = 5.0e-01*(alist(maxerr)+blist(maxerr))
05729     a2 = b1
05730     b2 = blist(maxerr)
05731     erlast = errmax
05732 
05733     call qc25o ( f, a1, b1, domega, integr, nrmom, maxp1, 0, area1, &
05734       error1, nev, resabs, defab1, momcom, chebmo )
05735 
05736     neval = neval+nev
05737 
05738     call qc25o ( f, a2, b2, domega, integr, nrmom, maxp1, 1, area2, &
05739       error2, nev, resabs, defab2, momcom, chebmo )
05740 
05741     neval = neval+nev
05742 !
05743 !  Improve previous approximations to integral and error and
05744 !  test for accuracy.
05745 !
05746     area12 = area1+area2
05747     erro12 = error1+error2
05748     errsum = errsum+erro12-errmax
05749     area = area+area12-rlist(maxerr)
05750     if ( defab1 == error1 .or. defab2 == error2 ) go to 25
05751     if ( abs(rlist(maxerr)-area12) > 1.0e-05*abs(area12) &
05752     .or. erro12 < 9.9e-01*errmax ) go to 20
05753     if ( extrap ) iroff2 = iroff2+1
05754 
05755     if ( .not.extrap ) then
05756       iroff1 = iroff1+1
05757     end if
05758 
05759 20  continue
05760 
05761     if ( last > 10.and.erro12 > errmax ) iroff3 = iroff3+1
05762 
05763 25  continue
05764 
05765     rlist(maxerr) = area1
05766     rlist(last) = area2
05767     nnlog(maxerr) = nrmom
05768     nnlog(last) = nrmom
05769     errbnd = max ( epsabs,epsrel*abs(area))
05770 !
05771 !  Test for roundoff error and eventually set error flag
05772 !
05773     if ( iroff1+iroff2 >= 10 .or. iroff3 >= 20 ) ier = 2
05774 
05775     if ( iroff2 >= 5) ierro = 3
05776 !
05777 !  Set error flag in the case that the number of subintervals
05778 !  equals limit.
05779 !
05780     if ( last == limit ) then
05781       ier = 1
05782     end if
05783 !
05784 !  Set error flag in the case of bad integrand behavior at
05785 !  a point of the integration range.
05786 !
05787     if ( max ( abs(a1),abs(b2)) <= (1.0e+00+1.0e+03* epsilon ( a1 ) ) &
05788     *(abs(a2)+1.0e+03* tiny ( a2 ) )) then
05789       ier = 4
05790     end if
05791 !
05792 !  Append the newly-created intervals to the list.
05793 !
05794     if ( error2 <= error1 ) then
05795       alist(last) = a2
05796       blist(maxerr) = b1
05797       blist(last) = b2
05798       elist(maxerr) = error1
05799       elist(last) = error2
05800     else
05801       alist(maxerr) = a2
05802       alist(last) = a1
05803       blist(last) = b1
05804       rlist(maxerr) = area2
05805       rlist(last) = area1
05806       elist(maxerr) = error2
05807       elist(last) = error1
05808     end if
05809 !
05810 !  Call QSORT to maintain the descending ordering
05811 !  in the list of error estimates and select the subinterval
05812 !  with nrmax-th largest error estimate (to be bisected next).
05813 !
05814 
05815     call qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, errmax, elist, iord, nrmax )
05816 
05817     if ( errsum <= errbnd ) then
05818       go to 170
05819     end if
05820 
05821     if ( ier /= 0 ) then
05822       exit
05823     end if
05824 
05825     if ( last == 2 .and. extall ) go to 120
05826 
05827     if ( noext ) then
05828       cycle
05829     end if
05830 
05831     if ( .not. extall ) go to 50
05832     erlarg = erlarg-erlast
05833     if ( abs(b1-a1) > small ) erlarg = erlarg+erro12
05834     if ( extrap ) go to 70
05835 !
05836 !  Test whether the interval to be bisected next is the
05837 !  smallest interval.
05838 !
05839 50  continue
05840 
05841     width = abs(blist(maxerr)-alist(maxerr))
05842 
05843     if ( width > small ) then
05844       cycle
05845     end if
05846 
05847     if ( extall ) go to 60
05848 !
05849 !  Test whether we can start with the extrapolation procedure
05850 !  (we do this if we integrate over the next interval with
05851 !  use of a Gauss-Kronrod rule - see QC25O).
05852 !
05853     small = small*5.0e-01
05854 
05855     if ( 2.5e-01*width*domega > 2.0e+00 ) then
05856       cycle
05857     end if
05858 
05859     extall = .true.
05860     go to 130
05861 
05862 60  continue
05863 
05864     extrap = .true.
05865     nrmax = 2
05866 
05867 70  continue
05868 
05869     if ( ierro == 3 .or. erlarg <= ertest ) go to 90
05870 !
05871 !  The smallest interval has the largest error.
05872 !  Before bisecting decrease the sum of the errors over the
05873 !  larger intervals (ERLARG) and perform extrapolation.
05874 !
05875     jupbnd = last
05876 
05877     if ( last > (limit/2+2) ) then
05878       jupbnd = limit+3-last
05879     end if
05880 
05881     id = nrmax
05882 
05883     do k = id, jupbnd
05884       maxerr = iord(nrmax)
05885       errmax = elist(maxerr)
05886       if ( abs(blist(maxerr)-alist(maxerr)) > small ) go to 140
05887       nrmax = nrmax+1
05888     end do
05889 !
05890 !  Perform extrapolation.
05891 !
05892 90  continue
05893 
05894     numrl2 = numrl2+1
05895     rlist2(numrl2) = area
05896 
05897     if ( numrl2 < 3 ) go to 110
05898 
05899     call qextr ( numrl2, rlist2, reseps, abseps, res3la, nres )
05900     ktmin = ktmin+1
05901 
05902     if ( ktmin > 5.and.abserr < 1.0e-03*errsum ) then
05903       ier = 5
05904     end if
05905 
05906     if ( abseps >= abserr ) go to 100
05907 
05908     ktmin = 0
05909     abserr = abseps
05910     result = reseps
05911     correc = erlarg
05912     ertest = max ( epsabs, epsrel*abs(reseps))
05913 
05914     if ( abserr <= ertest ) then
05915       exit
05916     end if
05917 !
05918 !  Prepare bisection of the smallest interval.
05919 !
05920 100 continue
05921 
05922     if ( numrl2 == 1 ) then
05923       noext = .true.
05924     end if
05925 
05926     if ( ier == 5 ) then
05927       exit
05928     end if
05929 
05930 110 continue
05931 
05932     maxerr = iord(1)
05933     errmax = elist(maxerr)
05934     nrmax = 1
05935     extrap = .false.
05936     small = small*5.0e-01
05937     erlarg = errsum
05938     cycle
05939 
05940 120 continue
05941 
05942     small = small * 5.0e-01
05943     numrl2 = numrl2 + 1
05944     rlist2(numrl2) = area
05945 
05946 130 continue
05947 
05948     ertest = errbnd
05949     erlarg = errsum
05950 
05951 140 continue
05952 
05953   end do
05954 !
05955 !  set the final result.
05956 !
05957   if ( abserr == huge ( abserr ) .or. nres == 0 ) then
05958     go to 170
05959   end if
05960 
05961   if ( ier+ierro == 0 ) go to 165
05962   if ( ierro == 3 ) abserr = abserr+correc
05963   if ( ier == 0 ) ier = 3
05964   if ( result /= 0.0e+00.and.area /= 0.0e+00 ) go to 160
05965   if ( abserr > errsum ) go to 170
05966   if ( area == 0.0e+00 ) go to 190
05967   go to 165
05968 
05969 160 continue
05970 
05971   if ( abserr/abs(result) > errsum/abs(area) ) go to 170
05972 !
05973 !  Test on divergence.
05974 !
05975   165 continue
05976 
05977   if ( ksgn == (-1) .and. max ( abs(result),abs(area)) <=  &
05978    defabs*1.0e-02 ) go to 190
05979 
05980   if ( 1.0e-02 > (result/area) .or. (result/area) > 1.0e+02 &
05981    .or. errsum >= abs(area) ) ier = 6
05982 
05983   go to 190
05984 !
05985 !  Compute global integral sum.
05986 !
05987 170 continue
05988 
05989   result = sum ( rlist(1:last) )
05990 
05991   abserr = errsum
05992 
05993 190 continue
05994 
05995   if (ier > 2) ier=ier-1
05996 
05997 200 continue
05998 
05999   if ( integr == 2 .and. omega < 0.0e+00 ) then
06000     result = -result
06001   end if
06002 
06003   return
06004 end
06005 subroutine qk15 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, resabs, resasc )
06006 
06007 !*****************************************************************************80
06008 !
06009 !! QK15 carries out a 15 point Gauss-Kronrod quadrature rule.
06010 !
06011 !  Discussion:
06012 !
06013 !    This routine approximates
06014 !      I = integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) dx
06015 !    with an error estimate, and
06016 !      J = integral ( A <= X <= B ) | F(X) | dx
06017 !
06018 !  Author:
06019 !
06020 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06021 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
06022 !
06023 !  Reference:
06024 !
06025 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06026 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
06027 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
06028 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
06029 !
06030 !  Parameters:
06031 !
06032 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
06033 !      function f ( x )
06034 !      real f
06035 !      real x
06036 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
06037 !
06038 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
06039 !
06040 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
06041 !    RESULT is computed by applying the 15-point Kronrod rule (RESK) 
06042 !    obtained by optimal addition of abscissae to the 7-point Gauss rule 
06043 !    (RESG).
06044 !
06045 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of | I - RESULT |.
06046 !
06047 !    Output, real RESABS, approximation to the integral of the absolute
06048 !    value of F.
06049 !
06050 !    Output, real RESASC, approximation to the integral | F-I/(B-A) | 
06051 !    over [A,B].
06052 !
06053 !  Local Parameters:
06054 !
06055 !           the abscissae and weights are given for the interval (-1,1).
06056 !           because of symmetry only the positive abscissae and their
06057 !           corresponding weights are given.
06058 !
06059 !           xgk    - abscissae of the 15-point Kronrod rule
06060 !                    xgk(2), xgk(4), ...  abscissae of the 7-point
06061 !                    Gauss rule
06062 !                    xgk(1), xgk(3), ...  abscissae which are optimally
06063 !                    added to the 7-point Gauss rule
06064 !
06065 !           wgk    - weights of the 15-point Kronrod rule
06066 !
06067 !           wg     - weights of the 7-point Gauss rule
06068 !
06069 !           centr  - mid point of the interval
06070 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval
06071 !           absc   - abscissa
06072 !           fval*  - function value
06073 !           resg   - result of the 7-point Gauss formula
06074 !           resk   - result of the 15-point Kronrod formula
06075 !           reskh  - approximation to the mean value of f over (a,b),
06076 !                    i.e. to i/(b-a)
06077 !
06078   implicit none
06079 
06080   real a
06081   real absc
06082   real abserr
06083   real b
06084   real centr
06085   real dhlgth
06086   real, external :: f
06087   real fc
06088   real fsum
06089   real fval1
06090   real fval2
06091   real fv1(7)
06092   real fv2(7)
06093   real hlgth
06094   integer j
06095   integer jtw
06096   integer jtwm1
06097   real resabs
06098   real resasc
06099   real resg
06100   real resk
06101   real reskh
06102   real result
06103   real wg(4)
06104   real wgk(8)
06105   real xgk(8)
06106 
06107   data xgk(1),xgk(2),xgk(3),xgk(4),xgk(5),xgk(6),xgk(7),xgk(8)/ &
06108        9.914553711208126e-01,   9.491079123427585e-01, &
06109        8.648644233597691e-01,   7.415311855993944e-01, &
06110        5.860872354676911e-01,   4.058451513773972e-01, &
06111        2.077849550078985e-01,   0.0e+00              /
06112   data wgk(1),wgk(2),wgk(3),wgk(4),wgk(5),wgk(6),wgk(7),wgk(8)/ &
06113        2.293532201052922e-02,   6.309209262997855e-02, &
06114        1.047900103222502e-01,   1.406532597155259e-01, &
06115        1.690047266392679e-01,   1.903505780647854e-01, &
06116        2.044329400752989e-01,   2.094821410847278e-01/
06117   data wg(1),wg(2),wg(3),wg(4)/ &
06118        1.294849661688697e-01,   2.797053914892767e-01, &
06119        3.818300505051189e-01,   4.179591836734694e-01/
06120 !
06121   centr = 5.0e-01*(a+b)
06122   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(b-a)
06123   dhlgth = abs(hlgth)
06124 !
06125 !  Compute the 15-point Kronrod approximation to the integral,
06126 !  and estimate the absolute error.
06127 !
06128   fc = f(centr)
06129   resg = fc*wg(4)
06130   resk = fc*wgk(8)
06131   resabs = abs(resk)
06132 
06133   do j = 1, 3
06134     jtw = j*2
06135     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtw)
06136     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
06137     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
06138     fv1(jtw) = fval1
06139     fv2(jtw) = fval2
06140     fsum = fval1+fval2
06141     resg = resg+wg(j)*fsum
06142     resk = resk+wgk(jtw)*fsum
06143     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtw)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06144   end do
06145 
06146   do j = 1, 4
06147     jtwm1 = j*2-1
06148     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtwm1)
06149     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
06150     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
06151     fv1(jtwm1) = fval1
06152     fv2(jtwm1) = fval2
06153     fsum = fval1+fval2
06154     resk = resk+wgk(jtwm1)*fsum
06155     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtwm1)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06156   end do
06157 
06158   reskh = resk * 5.0e-01
06159   resasc = wgk(8)*abs(fc-reskh)
06160 
06161   do j = 1, 7
06162     resasc = resasc+wgk(j)*(abs(fv1(j)-reskh)+abs(fv2(j)-reskh))
06163   end do
06164 
06165   result = resk*hlgth
06166   resabs = resabs*dhlgth
06167   resasc = resasc*dhlgth
06168   abserr = abs((resk-resg)*hlgth)
06169 
06170   if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00.and.abserr /= 0.0e+00 ) then
06171     abserr = resasc*min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
06172   end if
06173 
06174   if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) / (5.0e+01* epsilon ( resabs ) ) ) then
06175     abserr = max (( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01)*resabs,abserr)
06176   end if
06177 
06178   return
06179 end
06180 subroutine qk15i ( f, boun, inf, a, b, result, abserr, resabs, resasc )
06181 
06182 !*****************************************************************************80
06183 !
06184 !! QK15I applies a 15 point Gauss-Kronrod quadrature on an infinite interval.
06185 !
06186 !  Discussion:
06187 !
06188 !    The original infinite integration range is mapped onto the interval 
06189 !    (0,1) and (a,b) is a part of (0,1).  The routine then computes:
06190 !
06191 !    i = integral of transformed integrand over (a,b),
06192 !    j = integral of abs(transformed integrand) over (a,b).
06193 !
06194 !  Author:
06195 !
06196 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06197 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
06198 !
06199 !  Reference:
06200 !
06201 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06202 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
06203 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
06204 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
06205 !
06206 !  Parameters:
06207 !
06208 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
06209 !      function f ( x )
06210 !      real f
06211 !      real x
06212 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
06213 !
06214 !    Input, real BOUN, the finite bound of the original integration range,
06215 !    or zero if INF is 2.
06216 !
06217 !    Input, integer INF, indicates the type of the interval.
06218 !    -1: the original interval is (-infinity,BOUN),
06219 !    +1, the original interval is (BOUN,+infinity),
06220 !    +2, the original interval is (-infinity,+infinity) and
06221 !    the integral is computed as the sum of two integrals, one 
06222 !    over (-infinity,0) and one over (0,+infinity).
06223 !
06224 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration, over a subrange of [0,1].
06225 !
06226 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
06227 !    RESULT is computed by applying the 15-point Kronrod rule (RESK) obtained 
06228 !    by optimal addition of abscissae to the 7-point Gauss rule (RESG).
06229 !
06230 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of | I - RESULT |.
06231 !
06232 !    Output, real RESABS, approximation to the integral of the absolute
06233 !    value of F.
06234 !
06235 !    Output, real RESASC, approximation to the integral of the
06236 !    transformated integrand | F-I/(B-A) | over [A,B].
06237 !
06238 !  Local Parameters:
06239 !
06240 !           centr  - mid point of the interval
06241 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval
06242 !           absc*  - abscissa
06243 !           tabsc* - transformed abscissa
06244 !           fval*  - function value
06245 !           resg   - result of the 7-point Gauss formula
06246 !           resk   - result of the 15-point Kronrod formula
06247 !           reskh  - approximation to the mean value of the transformed
06248 !                    integrand over (a,b), i.e. to i/(b-a)
06249 !
06250   implicit none
06251 
06252   real a
06253   real absc
06254   real absc1
06255   real absc2
06256   real abserr
06257   real b
06258   real boun
06259   real centr
06260   real dinf
06261   real, external :: f
06262   real fc
06263   real fsum
06264   real fval1
06265   real fval2
06266   real fv1(7)
06267   real fv2(7)
06268   real hlgth
06269   integer inf
06270   integer j
06271   real resabs
06272   real resasc
06273   real resg
06274   real resk
06275   real reskh
06276   real result
06277   real tabsc1
06278   real tabsc2
06279   real wg(8)
06280   real wgk(8)
06281   real xgk(8)
06282 !
06283 !  the abscissae and weights are supplied for the interval
06284 !  (-1,1).  because of symmetry only the positive abscissae and
06285 !  their corresponding weights are given.
06286 !
06287 !           xgk    - abscissae of the 15-point Kronrod rule
06288 !                    xgk(2), xgk(4), ... abscissae of the 7-point Gauss
06289 !                    rule
06290 !                    xgk(1), xgk(3), ...  abscissae which are optimally
06291 !                    added to the 7-point Gauss rule
06292 !
06293 !           wgk    - weights of the 15-point Kronrod rule
06294 !
06295 !           wg     - weights of the 7-point Gauss rule, corresponding
06296 !                    to the abscissae xgk(2), xgk(4), ...
06297 !                    wg(1), wg(3), ... are set to zero.
06298 !
06299   data xgk(1),xgk(2),xgk(3),xgk(4),xgk(5),xgk(6),xgk(7),xgk(8)/ &
06300        9.914553711208126e-01,     9.491079123427585e-01, &
06301        8.648644233597691e-01,     7.415311855993944e-01, &
06302        5.860872354676911e-01,     4.058451513773972e-01, &
06303        2.077849550078985e-01,     0.0000000000000000e+00/
06304 
06305   data wgk(1),wgk(2),wgk(3),wgk(4),wgk(5),wgk(6),wgk(7),wgk(8)/ &
06306        2.293532201052922e-02,     6.309209262997855e-02, &
06307        1.047900103222502e-01,     1.406532597155259e-01, &
06308        1.690047266392679e-01,     1.903505780647854e-01, &
06309        2.044329400752989e-01,     2.094821410847278e-01/
06310 
06311   data wg(1),wg(2),wg(3),wg(4),wg(5),wg(6),wg(7),wg(8)/ &
06312        0.0000000000000000e+00,     1.294849661688697e-01, &
06313        0.0000000000000000e+00,     2.797053914892767e-01, &
06314        0.0000000000000000e+00,     3.818300505051189e-01, &
06315        0.0000000000000000e+00,     4.179591836734694e-01/
06316 
06317   dinf = min ( 1, inf )
06318 
06319   centr = 5.0e-01*(a+b)
06320   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(b-a)
06321   tabsc1 = boun+dinf*(1.0e+00-centr)/centr
06322   fval1 = f(tabsc1)
06323   if ( inf == 2 ) fval1 = fval1+f(-tabsc1)
06324   fc = (fval1/centr)/centr
06325 !
06326 !  Compute the 15-point Kronrod approximation to the integral,
06327 !  and estimate the error.
06328 !
06329   resg = wg(8)*fc
06330   resk = wgk(8)*fc
06331   resabs = abs(resk)
06332 
06333   do j = 1, 7
06334 
06335     absc = hlgth*xgk(j)
06336     absc1 = centr-absc
06337     absc2 = centr+absc
06338     tabsc1 = boun+dinf*(1.0e+00-absc1)/absc1
06339     tabsc2 = boun+dinf*(1.0e+00-absc2)/absc2
06340     fval1 = f(tabsc1)
06341     fval2 = f(tabsc2)
06342 
06343     if ( inf == 2 ) then
06344       fval1 = fval1+f(-tabsc1)
06345       fval2 = fval2+f(-tabsc2)
06346     end if
06347 
06348     fval1 = (fval1/absc1)/absc1
06349     fval2 = (fval2/absc2)/absc2
06350     fv1(j) = fval1
06351     fv2(j) = fval2
06352     fsum = fval1+fval2
06353     resg = resg+wg(j)*fsum
06354     resk = resk+wgk(j)*fsum
06355     resabs = resabs+wgk(j)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06356   end do
06357 
06358   reskh = resk * 5.0e-01
06359   resasc = wgk(8) * abs(fc-reskh)
06360 
06361   do j = 1, 7
06362     resasc = resasc + wgk(j)*(abs(fv1(j)-reskh)+abs(fv2(j)-reskh))
06363   end do
06364 
06365   result = resk * hlgth
06366   resasc = resasc * hlgth
06367   resabs = resabs * hlgth
06368   abserr = abs ( ( resk - resg ) * hlgth )
06369 
06370   if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00.and.abserr /= 0.0e+00) then
06371     abserr = resasc* min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
06372   end if
06373 
06374   if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) / ( 5.0e+01 * epsilon ( resabs ) ) ) then
06375     abserr = max (( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01)*resabs,abserr)
06376   end if
06377 
06378   return
06379 end
06380 subroutine qk15w ( f, w, p1, p2, p3, p4, kp, a, b, result, abserr, resabs, &
06381   resasc )
06382 
06383 !*****************************************************************************80
06384 !
06385 !! QK15W applies a 15 point Gauss-Kronrod rule for a weighted integrand.
06386 !
06387 !  Discussion:
06388 !
06389 !    This routine approximates 
06390 !      i = integral of f*w over (a,b), 
06391 !    with error estimate, and
06392 !      j = integral of abs(f*w) over (a,b)
06393 !
06394 !  Author:
06395 !
06396 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06397 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
06398 !
06399 !  Reference:
06400 !
06401 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06402 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
06403 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
06404 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
06405 !
06406 !  Parameters:
06407 !
06408 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
06409 !      function f ( x )
06410 !      real f
06411 !      real x
06412 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
06413 !
06414 !              w      - real
06415 !                       function subprogram defining the integrand
06416 !                       weight function w(x). the actual name for w
06417 !                       needs to be declared e x t e r n a l in the
06418 !                       calling program.
06419 !
06420 !    ?, real P1, P2, P3, P4, parameters in the weight function
06421 !
06422 !    Input, integer KP, key for indicating the type of weight function
06423 !
06424 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
06425 !
06426 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
06427 !    RESULT is computed by applying the 15-point Kronrod rule (RESK) obtained by
06428 !    optimal addition of abscissae to the 7-point Gauss rule (RESG).
06429 !
06430 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of | I - RESULT |.
06431 !
06432 !    Output, real RESABS, approximation to the integral of the absolute
06433 !    value of F.
06434 !
06435 !    Output, real RESASC, approximation to the integral | F-I/(B-A) | 
06436 !    over [A,B].
06437 !
06438 !  Local Parameters:
06439 !
06440 !           centr  - mid point of the interval
06441 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval
06442 !           absc*  - abscissa
06443 !           fval*  - function value
06444 !           resg   - result of the 7-point Gauss formula
06445 !           resk   - result of the 15-point Kronrod formula
06446 !           reskh  - approximation to the mean value of f*w over (a,b),
06447 !                    i.e. to i/(b-a)
06448 !
06449   implicit none
06450 
06451   real a
06452   real absc
06453   real absc1
06454   real absc2
06455   real abserr
06456   real b
06457   real centr
06458   real dhlgth
06459   real, external :: f
06460   real fc
06461   real fsum
06462   real fval1
06463   real fval2
06464   real fv1(7)
06465   real fv2(7)
06466   real hlgth
06467   integer j
06468   integer jtw
06469   integer jtwm1
06470   integer kp
06471   real p1
06472   real p2
06473   real p3
06474   real p4
06475   real resabs
06476   real resasc
06477   real resg
06478   real resk
06479   real reskh
06480   real result
06481   real, external :: w
06482   real, dimension ( 4 ) :: wg = (/ 
06483     1.294849661688697e-01,     2.797053914892767e-01, 
06484     3.818300505051889e-01,     4.179591836734694e-01 /)
06485   real wgk(8)
06486   real xgk(8)
06487 !
06488 !  the abscissae and weights are given for the interval (-1,1).
06489 !  because of symmetry only the positive abscissae and their
06490 !  corresponding weights are given.
06491 !
06492 !           xgk    - abscissae of the 15-point Gauss-Kronrod rule
06493 !                    xgk(2), xgk(4), ... abscissae of the 7-point Gauss
06494 !                    rule
06495 !                    xgk(1), xgk(3), ... abscissae which are optimally
06496 !                    added to the 7-point Gauss rule
06497 !
06498 !           wgk    - weights of the 15-point Gauss-Kronrod rule
06499 !
06500 !           wg     - weights of the 7-point Gauss rule
06501 !
06502   data xgk(1),xgk(2),xgk(3),xgk(4),xgk(5),xgk(6),xgk(7),xgk(8)/ &
06503        9.914553711208126e-01,     9.491079123427585e-01, &
06504        8.648644233597691e-01,     7.415311855993944e-01, &
06505        5.860872354676911e-01,     4.058451513773972e-01, &
06506        2.077849550789850e-01,     0.000000000000000e+00/
06507 
06508   data wgk(1),wgk(2),wgk(3),wgk(4),wgk(5),wgk(6),wgk(7),wgk(8)/ &
06509        2.293532201052922e-02,     6.309209262997855e-02, &
06510        1.047900103222502e-01,     1.406532597155259e-01, &
06511        1.690047266392679e-01,     1.903505780647854e-01, &
06512        2.044329400752989e-01,     2.094821410847278e-01/
06513 !
06514   centr = 5.0e-01*(a+b)
06515   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(b-a)
06516   dhlgth = abs(hlgth)
06517 !
06518 !  Compute the 15-point Kronrod approximation to the integral,
06519 !  and estimate the error.
06520 !
06521   fc = f(centr)*w(centr,p1,p2,p3,p4,kp)
06522   resg = wg(4)*fc
06523   resk = wgk(8)*fc
06524   resabs = abs(resk)
06525 
06526   do j = 1, 3
06527     jtw = j*2
06528     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtw)
06529     absc1 = centr-absc
06530     absc2 = centr+absc
06531     fval1 = f(absc1)*w(absc1,p1,p2,p3,p4,kp)
06532     fval2 = f(absc2)*w(absc2,p1,p2,p3,p4,kp)
06533     fv1(jtw) = fval1
06534     fv2(jtw) = fval2
06535     fsum = fval1+fval2
06536     resg = resg+wg(j)*fsum
06537     resk = resk+wgk(jtw)*fsum
06538     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtw)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06539   end do
06540 
06541   do j = 1, 4
06542     jtwm1 = j*2-1
06543     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtwm1)
06544     absc1 = centr-absc
06545     absc2 = centr+absc
06546     fval1 = f(absc1)*w(absc1,p1,p2,p3,p4,kp)
06547     fval2 = f(absc2)*w(absc2,p1,p2,p3,p4,kp)
06548     fv1(jtwm1) = fval1
06549     fv2(jtwm1) = fval2
06550     fsum = fval1+fval2
06551     resk = resk+wgk(jtwm1)*fsum
06552     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtwm1)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06553   end do
06554 
06555   reskh = resk*5.0e-01
06556   resasc = wgk(8)*abs(fc-reskh)
06557 
06558   do j = 1, 7
06559     resasc = resasc+wgk(j)*(abs(fv1(j)-reskh)+abs(fv2(j)-reskh))
06560   end do
06561 
06562   result = resk*hlgth
06563   resabs = resabs*dhlgth
06564   resasc = resasc*dhlgth
06565   abserr = abs((resk-resg)*hlgth)
06566 
06567   if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00.and.abserr /= 0.0e+00) then
06568     abserr = resasc*min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
06569   end if
06570 
06571   if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) /(5.0e+01* epsilon ( resabs ) ) ) then
06572     abserr = max ( ( epsilon ( resabs ) * 5.0e+01)*resabs,abserr)
06573   end if
06574 
06575   return
06576 end
06577 subroutine qk21 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, resabs, resasc )
06578 
06579 !*****************************************************************************80
06580 !
06581 !! QK21 carries out a 21 point Gauss-Kronrod quadrature rule.
06582 !
06583 !  Discussion:
06584 !
06585 !    This routine approximates
06586 !      I = integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) dx
06587 !    with an error estimate, and
06588 !      J = integral ( A <= X <= B ) | F(X) | dx
06589 !
06590 !  Author:
06591 !
06592 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06593 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
06594 !
06595 !  Reference:
06596 !
06597 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
06598 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
06599 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
06600 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
06601 !
06602 !  Parameters:
06603 !
06604 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
06605 !      function f ( x )
06606 !      real f
06607 !      real x
06608 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
06609 !
06610 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
06611 !
06612 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
06613 !    RESULT is computed by applying the 21-point Kronrod rule (resk) 
06614 !    obtained by optimal addition of abscissae to the 10-point Gauss 
06615 !    rule (resg).
06616 !
06617 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of | I - RESULT |.
06618 !
06619 !    Output, real RESABS, approximation to the integral of the absolute
06620 !    value of F.
06621 !
06622 !    Output, real RESASC, approximation to the integral | F-I/(B-A) | 
06623 !    over [A,B].
06624 !
06625   implicit none
06626 
06627   real a
06628   real absc
06629   real abserr
06630   real b
06631   real centr
06632   real dhlgth
06633   real, external :: f
06634   real fc
06635   real fsum
06636   real fval1
06637   real fval2
06638   real fv1(10)
06639   real fv2(10)
06640   real hlgth
06641   integer j
06642   integer jtw
06643   integer jtwm1
06644   real resabs
06645   real resasc
06646   real resg
06647   real resk
06648   real reskh
06649   real result
06650   real wg(5)
06651   real wgk(11)
06652   real xgk(11)
06653 !
06654 !           the abscissae and weights are given for the interval (-1,1).
06655 !           because of symmetry only the positive abscissae and their
06656 !           corresponding weights are given.
06657 !
06658 !           xgk    - abscissae of the 21-point Kronrod rule
06659 !                    xgk(2), xgk(4), ...  abscissae of the 10-point
06660 !                    Gauss rule
06661 !                    xgk(1), xgk(3), ...  abscissae which are optimally
06662 !                    added to the 10-point Gauss rule
06663 !
06664 !           wgk    - weights of the 21-point Kronrod rule
06665 !
06666 !           wg     - weights of the 10-point Gauss rule
06667 !
06668   data xgk(1),xgk(2),xgk(3),xgk(4),xgk(5),xgk(6),xgk(7),xgk(8), &
06669     xgk(9),xgk(10),xgk(11)/ &
06670        9.956571630258081e-01,     9.739065285171717e-01, &
06671        9.301574913557082e-01,     8.650633666889845e-01, &
06672        7.808177265864169e-01,     6.794095682990244e-01, &
06673        5.627571346686047e-01,     4.333953941292472e-01, &
06674        2.943928627014602e-01,     1.488743389816312e-01, &
06675        0.000000000000000e+00/
06676 !
06677   data wgk(1),wgk(2),wgk(3),wgk(4),wgk(5),wgk(6),wgk(7),wgk(8), &
06678     wgk(9),wgk(10),wgk(11)/ &
06679        1.169463886737187e-02,     3.255816230796473e-02, &
06680        5.475589657435200e-02,     7.503967481091995e-02, &
06681        9.312545458369761e-02,     1.093871588022976e-01, &
06682        1.234919762620659e-01,     1.347092173114733e-01, &
06683        1.427759385770601e-01,     1.477391049013385e-01, &
06684        1.494455540029169e-01/
06685 !
06686   data wg(1),wg(2),wg(3),wg(4),wg(5)/ &
06687        6.667134430868814e-02,     1.494513491505806e-01, &
06688        2.190863625159820e-01,     2.692667193099964e-01, &
06689        2.955242247147529e-01/
06690 !
06691 !
06692 !           list of major variables
06693 !
06694 !           centr  - mid point of the interval
06695 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval
06696 !           absc   - abscissa
06697 !           fval*  - function value
06698 !           resg   - result of the 10-point Gauss formula
06699 !           resk   - result of the 21-point Kronrod formula
06700 !           reskh  - approximation to the mean value of f over (a,b),
06701 !                    i.e. to i/(b-a)
06702 !
06703   centr = 5.0e-01*(a+b)
06704   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(b-a)
06705   dhlgth = abs(hlgth)
06706 !
06707 !  Compute the 21-point Kronrod approximation to the
06708 !  integral, and estimate the absolute error.
06709 !
06710   resg = 0.0e+00
06711   fc = f(centr)
06712   resk = wgk(11)*fc
06713   resabs = abs(resk)
06714 
06715   do j = 1, 5
06716     jtw = 2*j
06717     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtw)
06718     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
06719     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
06720     fv1(jtw) = fval1
06721     fv2(jtw) = fval2
06722     fsum = fval1+fval2
06723     resg = resg+wg(j)*fsum
06724     resk = resk+wgk(jtw)*fsum
06725     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtw)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06726   end do
06727 
06728   do j = 1, 5
06729     jtwm1 = 2*j-1
06730     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtwm1)
06731     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
06732     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
06733     fv1(jtwm1) = fval1
06734     fv2(jtwm1) = fval2
06735     fsum = fval1+fval2
06736     resk = resk+wgk(jtwm1)*fsum
06737     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtwm1)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06738   end do
06739 
06740   reskh = resk*5.0e-01
06741   resasc = wgk(11)*abs(fc-reskh)
06742 
06743   do j = 1, 10
06744     resasc = resasc+wgk(j)*(abs(fv1(j)-reskh)+abs(fv2(j)-reskh))
06745   end do
06746 
06747   result = resk*hlgth
06748   resabs = resabs*dhlgth
06749   resasc = resasc*dhlgth
06750   abserr = abs((resk-resg)*hlgth)
06751 
06752   if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00.and.abserr /= 0.0e+00) then
06753     abserr = resasc*min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
06754   end if
06755 
06756   if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) /(5.0e+01* epsilon ( resabs ) )) then
06757     abserr = max (( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01)*resabs,abserr)
06758   end if
06759 
06760   return
06761 end

06782 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger,

06848 !                    added to the 15-point Gauss rule
06849 !

06856        9.980022986933971e-01,   9.879925180204854e-01, &

06858        8.972645323440819e-01,   8.482065834104272e-01, &

06861        4.850818636402397e-01,   3.941513470775634e-01, &

06865     wgk(9),wgk(10),wgk(11),wgk(12),wgk(13),wgk(14),wgk(15),wgk(16)/ &

06875        3.075324199611727e-02,   7.036604748810812e-02, &
06876        1.071592204671719e-01,   1.395706779261543e-01, &

06915   end do
06916 
06917   do j = 1, 8
06918     jtwm1 = j*2-1
06919     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtwm1)
06920     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
06921     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
06922     fv1(jtwm1) = fval1
06923     fv2(jtwm1) = fval2
06924     fsum = fval1+fval2
06925     resk = resk+wgk(jtwm1)*fsum
06926     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtwm1)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
06927   end do
06928 
06929   reskh = resk*5.0e-01
06930   resasc = wgk(16)*abs(fc-reskh)
06931

06945     abserr = max (( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01)*resabs,abserr)
06946   end if
06947 
06948   return
06949 end

06960 !    with an error estimate, and
06961 !      J = integral ( A <= X <= B ) | F(X) | dx
06962 !
06963 !  Author:
06964 !

06997 !    over [A,B].

07000 !
07001 !           centr  - mid point of the interval
07002 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval
07003 !           absc   - abscissa
07004 !           fval*  - function value
07005 !           resg   - result of the 20-point Gauss formula
07006 !           resk   - result of the 41-point Kronrod formula

07022   real fval2

07044 !                    xgk(2), xgk(4), ...  abscissae of the 20-point
07045 !                    Gauss rule
07046 !                    xgk(1), xgk(3), ...  abscissae which are optimally
07047 !                    added to the 20-point Gauss rule
