07080        7.660071191799966e-02/
07081   data wg(1),wg(2),wg(3),wg(4),wg(5),wg(6),wg(7),wg(8),wg(9),wg(10)/ &
07082        1.761400713915212e-02,   4.060142980038694e-02, &
07083        6.267204833410906e-02,   8.327674157670475e-02, &
07084        1.019301198172404e-01,   1.181945319615184e-01, &
07085        1.316886384491766e-01,   1.420961093183821e-01, &
07086        1.491729864726037e-01,   1.527533871307259e-01/
07087 !
07088   centr = 5.0e-01*(a+b)
07089   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(b-a)
07090   dhlgth = abs(hlgth)
07091 !
07092 !  Compute 41-point Gauss-Kronrod approximation to the
07093 !  the integral, and estimate the absolute error.
07094 !
07095   resg = 0.0e+00
07096   fc = f(centr)
07097   resk = wgk(21)*fc
07098   resabs = abs(resk)
07099 
07100   do j = 1, 10
07101     jtw = j*2
07102     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtw)
07103     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
07104     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
07105     fv1(jtw) = fval1
07106     fv2(jtw) = fval2
07107     fsum = fval1+fval2
07108     resg = resg+wg(j)*fsum
07109     resk = resk+wgk(jtw)*fsum
07110     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtw)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
07111   end do
07112 
07113   do j = 1, 10
07114     jtwm1 = j*2-1
07115     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtwm1)
07116     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
07117     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
07118     fv1(jtwm1) = fval1
07119     fv2(jtwm1) = fval2
07120     fsum = fval1+fval2
07121     resk = resk+wgk(jtwm1)*fsum
07122     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtwm1)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
07123   end do
07124 
07125   reskh = resk*5.0e-01
07126   resasc = wgk(21)*abs(fc-reskh)
07127 
07128   do j = 1, 20
07129     resasc = resasc+wgk(j)*(abs(fv1(j)-reskh)+abs(fv2(j)-reskh))
07130   end do
07131 
07132   result = resk*hlgth
07133   resabs = resabs*dhlgth
07134   resasc = resasc*dhlgth
07135   abserr = abs((resk-resg)*hlgth)
07136 
07137   if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00.and.abserr /= 0.0e+00) &
07138     abserr = resasc*min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
07139 
07140   if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) /(5.0e+01* epsilon ( resabs ) )) then
07141     abserr = max (( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01)*resabs,abserr)
07142   end if
07143 
07144   return
07145 end
07146 subroutine qk51 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, resabs, resasc )
07147 
07148 !*****************************************************************************80
07149 !
07150 !! QK51 carries out a 51 point Gauss-Kronrod quadrature rule.
07151 !
07152 !  Discussion:
07153 !
07154 !    This routine approximates
07155 !      I = integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) dx
07156 !    with an error estimate, and
07157 !      J = integral ( A <= X <= B ) | F(X) | dx
07158 !
07159 !  Author:
07160 !
07161 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
07162 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
07163 !
07164 !  Reference:
07165 !
07166 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
07167 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
07168 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
07169 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
07170 !
07171 !  Parameters:
07172 !
07173 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
07174 !      function f ( x )
07175 !      real f
07176 !      real x
07177 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
07178 !
07179 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
07180 !
07181 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
07182 !                       result is computed by applying the 51-point
07183 !                       Kronrod rule (resk) obtained by optimal addition
07184 !                       of abscissae to the 25-point Gauss rule (resg).
07185 !
07186 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of | I - RESULT |.
07187 !
07188 !    Output, real RESABS, approximation to the integral of the absolute
07189 !    value of F.
07190 !
07191 !    Output, real RESASC, approximation to the integral | F-I/(B-A) | 
07192 !    over [A,B].
07193 !
07194 !  Local Parameters:
07195 !
07196 !           centr  - mid point of the interval
07197 !           hlgth  - half-length of the interval
07198 !           absc   - abscissa
07199 !           fval*  - function value
07200 !           resg   - result of the 25-point Gauss formula
07201 !           resk   - result of the 51-point Kronrod formula
07202 !           reskh  - approximation to the mean value of f over (a,b),
07203 !                    i.e. to i/(b-a)
07204 !
07205   implicit none
07206 
07207   real a
07208   real absc
07209   real abserr
07210   real b
07211   real centr
07212   real dhlgth
07213   real, external :: f
07214   real fc
07215   real fsum
07216   real fval1
07217   real fval2
07218   real fv1(25)
07219   real fv2(25)
07220   real hlgth
07221   integer j
07222   integer jtw
07223   integer jtwm1
07224   real resabs
07225   real resasc
07226   real resg
07227   real resk
07228   real reskh
07229   real result
07230   real wg(13)
07231   real wgk(26)
07232   real xgk(26)
07233 !
07234 !           the abscissae and weights are given for the interval (-1,1).
07235 !           because of symmetry only the positive abscissae and their
07236 !           corresponding weights are given.
07237 !
07238 !           xgk    - abscissae of the 51-point Kronrod rule
07239 !                    xgk(2), xgk(4), ...  abscissae of the 25-point
07240 !                    Gauss rule
07241 !                    xgk(1), xgk(3), ...  abscissae which are optimally
07242 !                    added to the 25-point Gauss rule
07243 !
07244 !           wgk    - weights of the 51-point Kronrod rule
07245 !
07246 !           wg     - weights of the 25-point Gauss rule
07247 !
07248   data xgk(1),xgk(2),xgk(3),xgk(4),xgk(5),xgk(6),xgk(7),xgk(8), &
07249     xgk(9),xgk(10),xgk(11),xgk(12),xgk(13),xgk(14)/ &
07250        9.992621049926098e-01,   9.955569697904981e-01, &
07251        9.880357945340772e-01,   9.766639214595175e-01, &
07252        9.616149864258425e-01,   9.429745712289743e-01, &
07253        9.207471152817016e-01,   8.949919978782754e-01, &
07254        8.658470652932756e-01,   8.334426287608340e-01, &
07255        7.978737979985001e-01,   7.592592630373576e-01, &
07256        7.177664068130844e-01,   6.735663684734684e-01/
07257    data xgk(15),xgk(16),xgk(17),xgk(18),xgk(19),xgk(20),xgk(21), &
07258     xgk(22),xgk(23),xgk(24),xgk(25),xgk(26)/ &
07259        6.268100990103174e-01,   5.776629302412230e-01, &
07260        5.263252843347192e-01,   4.730027314457150e-01, &
07261        4.178853821930377e-01,   3.611723058093878e-01, &
07262        3.030895389311078e-01,   2.438668837209884e-01, &
07263        1.837189394210489e-01,   1.228646926107104e-01, &
07264        6.154448300568508e-02,   0.0e+00               /
07265   data wgk(1),wgk(2),wgk(3),wgk(4),wgk(5),wgk(6),wgk(7),wgk(8), &
07266     wgk(9),wgk(10),wgk(11),wgk(12),wgk(13),wgk(14)/ &
07267        1.987383892330316e-03,   5.561932135356714e-03, &
07268        9.473973386174152e-03,   1.323622919557167e-02, &
07269        1.684781770912830e-02,   2.043537114588284e-02, &
07270        2.400994560695322e-02,   2.747531758785174e-02, &
07271        3.079230016738749e-02,   3.400213027432934e-02, &
07272        3.711627148341554e-02,   4.008382550403238e-02, &
07273        4.287284502017005e-02,   4.550291304992179e-02/
07274    data wgk(15),wgk(16),wgk(17),wgk(18),wgk(19),wgk(20),wgk(21), &
07275     wgk(22),wgk(23),wgk(24),wgk(25),wgk(26)/ &
07276        4.798253713883671e-02,   5.027767908071567e-02, &
07277        5.236288580640748e-02,   5.425112988854549e-02, &
07278        5.595081122041232e-02,   5.743711636156783e-02, &
07279        5.868968002239421e-02,   5.972034032417406e-02, &
07280        6.053945537604586e-02,   6.112850971705305e-02, &
07281        6.147118987142532e-02,   6.158081806783294e-02/
07282   data wg(1),wg(2),wg(3),wg(4),wg(5),wg(6),wg(7),wg(8),wg(9),wg(10), &
07283     wg(11),wg(12),wg(13)/ &
07284        1.139379850102629e-02,   2.635498661503214e-02, &
07285        4.093915670130631e-02,   5.490469597583519e-02, &
07286        6.803833381235692e-02,   8.014070033500102e-02, &
07287        9.102826198296365e-02,   1.005359490670506e-01, &
07288        1.085196244742637e-01,   1.148582591457116e-01, &
07289        1.194557635357848e-01,   1.222424429903100e-01, &
07290        1.231760537267155e-01/
07291 !
07292   centr = 5.0e-01*(a+b)
07293   hlgth = 5.0e-01*(b-a)
07294   dhlgth = abs(hlgth)
07295 !
07296 !  Compute the 51-point Kronrod approximation to the integral,
07297 !  and estimate the absolute error.
07298 !
07299   fc = f(centr)
07300   resg = wg(13)*fc
07301   resk = wgk(26)*fc
07302   resabs = abs(resk)
07303 
07304   do j = 1, 12
07305     jtw = j*2
07306     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtw)
07307     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
07308     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
07309     fv1(jtw) = fval1
07310     fv2(jtw) = fval2
07311     fsum = fval1+fval2
07312     resg = resg+wg(j)*fsum
07313     resk = resk+wgk(jtw)*fsum
07314     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtw)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
07315   end do
07316 
07317   do j = 1, 13
07318     jtwm1 = j*2-1
07319     absc = hlgth*xgk(jtwm1)
07320     fval1 = f(centr-absc)
07321     fval2 = f(centr+absc)
07322     fv1(jtwm1) = fval1
07323     fv2(jtwm1) = fval2
07324     fsum = fval1+fval2
07325     resk = resk+wgk(jtwm1)*fsum
07326     resabs = resabs+wgk(jtwm1)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
07327   end do
07328 
07329   reskh = resk*5.0e-01
07330   resasc = wgk(26)*abs(fc-reskh)
07331 
07332   do j = 1, 25
07333     resasc = resasc+wgk(j)*(abs(fv1(j)-reskh)+abs(fv2(j)-reskh))
07334   end do
07335 
07336   result = resk*hlgth
07337   resabs = resabs*dhlgth
07338   resasc = resasc*dhlgth
07339   abserr = abs((resk-resg)*hlgth)
07340 
07341   if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00.and.abserr /= 0.0e+00) then
07342     abserr = resasc*min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
07343   end if
07344 
07345   if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) / (5.0e+01* epsilon ( resabs ) ) ) then
07346     abserr = max (( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01)*resabs,abserr)
07347   end if
07348 
07349   return
07350 end
07351 subroutine qk61 ( f, a, b, result, abserr, resabs, resasc ) 
07352 
07353 !*****************************************************************************80
07354 !
07355 !! QK61 carries out a 61 point Gauss-Kronrod quadrature rule.
07356 !
07357 !  Discussion:
07358 !
07359 !    This routine approximates
07360 !      I = integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) dx
07361 !    with an error estimate, and
07362 !      J = integral ( A <= X <= B ) | F(X) | dx
07363 !

07365 !

07371 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger,

07422   real fval2

07550   end do
07551 
07552   result = resk*hlgth
07553   resabs = resabs*dhlgth
07554   resasc = resasc*dhlgth
07555   abserr = abs((resk-resg)*hlgth)
07556 
07557   if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00 .and. abserr /= 0.0e+00) then
07558     abserr = resasc*min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
07559   end if
07560 
07561   if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) / (5.0e+01* epsilon ( resabs ) )) then
07562     abserr = max ( ( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01)*resabs, abserr )
07563   end if
07564 
07565   return
07566 end
07567 subroutine qmomo ( alfa, beta, ri, rj, rg, rh, integr )
07568 
07569 !*****************************************************************************80
07570 !
07571 !! QMOMO computes modified Chebyshev moments.
07572 !
07573 !  Discussion:
07574 !
07575 !    This routine computes modified Chebyshev moments.
07576 !    The K-th modified Chebyshev moment is defined as the
07577 !    integral over (-1,1) of W(X)*T(K,X), where T(K,X) is the
07578 !    Chebyshev polynomial of degree K.
07579 !
07580 !  Author:
07581 !
07582 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
07583 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
07584 !
07585 !  Reference:
07586 !
07587 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
07588 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
07589 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
07590 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
07591 !
07592 !  Parameters:
07593 !
07594 !    Input, real ALFA, a parameter in the weight function w(x), ALFA > -1.
07595 !
07596 !    Input, real BETA, a parameter in the weight function w(x), BETA > -1.
07597 !
07598 !           ri     - real
07599 !                    vector of dimension 25
07600 !                    ri(k) is the integral over (-1,1) of
07601 !                    (1+x)**alfa*t(k-1,x), k = 1, ..., 25.
07602 !
07603 !           rj     - real
07604 !                    vector of dimension 25
07605 !                    rj(k) is the integral over (-1,1) of
07606 !                    (1-x)**beta*t(k-1,x), k = 1, ..., 25.
07607 !
07608 !           rg     - real
07609 !                    vector of dimension 25
07610 !                    rg(k) is the integral over (-1,1) of
07611 !                    (1+x)**alfa*log((1+x)/2)*t(k-1,x), k = 1, ...,25.
07612 !
07613 !           rh     - real
07614 !                    vector of dimension 25
07615 !                    rh(k) is the integral over (-1,1) of
07616 !                    (1-x)**beta*log((1-x)/2)*t(k-1,x), k = 1, ..., 25.
07617 !
07618 !           integr - integer
07619 !                    input parameter indicating the modified moments
07620 !                    to be computed
07621 !                    integr = 1 compute ri, rj
07622 !                           = 2 compute ri, rj, rg
07623 !                           = 3 compute ri, rj, rh
07624 !                           = 4 compute ri, rj, rg, rh
07625 !
07626   implicit none
07627 
07628   real alfa
07629   real alfp1
07630   real alfp2
07631   real an
07632   real anm1
07633   real beta
07634   real betp1
07635   real betp2
07636   integer i
07637   integer im1
07638   integer integr
07639   real ralf
07640   real rbet
07641   real rg(25)
07642   real rh(25)
07643   real ri(25)
07644   real rj(25)
07645 !
07646   alfp1 = alfa+1.0e+00
07647   betp1 = beta+1.0e+00
07648   alfp2 = alfa+2.0e+00
07649   betp2 = beta+2.0e+00
07650   ralf = 2.0e+00**alfp1
07651   rbet = 2.0e+00**betp1
07652 !
07653 !  Compute RI, RJ using a forward recurrence relation.
07654 !
07655   ri(1) = ralf/alfp1
07656   rj(1) = rbet/betp1
07657   ri(2) = ri(1)*alfa/alfp2
07658   rj(2) = rj(1)*beta/betp2
07659   an = 2.0e+00
07660   anm1 = 1.0e+00
07661 
07662   do i = 3, 25
07663     ri(i) = -(ralf+an*(an-alfp2)*ri(i-1))/(anm1*(an+alfp1))
07664     rj(i) = -(rbet+an*(an-betp2)*rj(i-1))/(anm1*(an+betp1))
07665     anm1 = an
07666     an = an+1.0e+00
07667   end do
07668 
07669   if ( integr == 1 ) go to 70
07670   if ( integr == 3 ) go to 40
07671 !
07672 !  Compute RG using a forward recurrence relation.
07673 !
07674   rg(1) = -ri(1)/alfp1
07675   rg(2) = -(ralf+ralf)/(alfp2*alfp2)-rg(1)
07676   an = 2.0e+00
07677   anm1 = 1.0e+00
07678   im1 = 2
07679 
07680   do i = 3, 25
07681     rg(i) = -(an*(an-alfp2)*rg(im1)-an*ri(im1)+anm1*ri(i))/ &
07682     (anm1*(an+alfp1))
07683     anm1 = an
07684     an = an+1.0e+00
07685     im1 = i
07686   end do
07687 
07688   if ( integr == 2 ) go to 70
07689 !
07690 !  Compute RH using a forward recurrence relation.
07691 !
07692 40 continue
07693 
07694   rh(1) = -rj(1) / betp1
07695   rh(2) = -(rbet+rbet)/(betp2*betp2)-rh(1)
07696   an = 2.0e+00
07697   anm1 = 1.0e+00
07698   im1 = 2
07699 
07700   do i = 3, 25
07701     rh(i) = -(an*(an-betp2)*rh(im1)-an*rj(im1)+ &
07702     anm1*rj(i))/(anm1*(an+betp1))
07703     anm1 = an
07704     an = an+1.0e+00
07705     im1 = i
07706   end do
07707 
07708   do i = 2, 25, 2
07709     rh(i) = -rh(i)
07710   end do
07711 
07712    70 continue
07713 
07714   do i = 2, 25, 2
07715     rj(i) = -rj(i)
07716   end do
07717 
07718 !  90 continue
07719 
07720   return
07721 end
07722 subroutine qng ( f, a, b, epsabs, epsrel, result, abserr, neval, ier )
07723 
07724 !*****************************************************************************80
07725 !
07726 !! QNG estimates an integral, using non-adaptive integration.
07727 !
07728 !  Discussion:
07729 !
07730 !    The routine calculates an approximation RESULT to a definite integral   
07731 !      I = integral of F over (A,B),
07732 !    hopefully satisfying
07733 !      || I - RESULT || <= max ( EPSABS, EPSREL * ||I|| ).
07734 !
07735 !    The routine is a simple non-adaptive automatic integrator, based on
07736 !    a sequence of rules with increasing degree of algebraic
07737 !    precision (Patterson, 1968).
07738 !
07739 !  Author:
07740 !
07741 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
07742 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
07743 !
07744 !  Reference:
07745 !
07746 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
07747 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
07748 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
07749 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
07750 !
07751 !  Parameters:
07752 !
07753 !    Input, external real F, the name of the function routine, of the form
07754 !      function f ( x )
07755 !      real f
07756 !      real x
07757 !    which evaluates the integrand function.
07758 !
07759 !    Input, real A, B, the limits of integration.
07760 !
07761 !    Input, real EPSABS, EPSREL, the absolute and relative accuracy requested.
07762 !
07763 !    Output, real RESULT, the estimated value of the integral.
07764 !    RESULT is obtained by applying the 21-point Gauss-Kronrod rule (RES21)
07765 !    obtained  by optimal addition of abscissae to the 10-point Gauss rule
07766 !    (RES10), or by applying the 43-point rule (RES43) obtained by optimal
07767 !    addition of abscissae to the 21-point Gauss-Kronrod rule, or by 
07768 !    applying the 87-point rule (RES87) obtained by optimal addition of
07769 !    abscissae to the 43-point rule.
07770 !
07771 !    Output, real ABSERR, an estimate of || I - RESULT ||.
07772 !
07773 !    Output, integer NEVAL, the number of times the integral was evaluated.
07774 !
07775 !           ier    - ier = 0 normal and reliable termination of the
07776 !                            routine. it is assumed that the requested
07777 !                            accuracy has been achieved.
07778 !                    ier > 0 abnormal termination of the routine. it is
07779 !                            assumed that the requested accuracy has
07780 !                            not been achieved.
07781 !                    ier = 1 the maximum number of steps has been
07782 !                            executed. the integral is probably too
07783 !                            difficult to be calculated by qng.
07784 !                        = 6 the input is invalid, because
07785 !                            epsabs < 0 and epsrel < 0,
07786 !                            result, abserr and neval are set to zero.
07787 !
07788 !  Local Parameters:
07789 !
07790 !           centr  - mid point of the integration interval
07791 !           hlgth  - half-length of the integration interval
07792 !           fcentr - function value at mid point
07793 !           absc   - abscissa
07794 !           fval   - function value
07795 !           savfun - array of function values which have already
07796 !                    been computed
07797 !           res10  - 10-point Gauss result
07798 !           res21  - 21-point Kronrod result
07799 !           res43  - 43-point result
07800 !           res87  - 87-point result
07801 !           resabs - approximation to the integral of abs(f)
07802 !           resasc - approximation to the integral of abs(f-i/(b-a))
07803 !
07804   implicit none
07805 
07806   real a
07807   real absc
07808   real abserr
07809   real b
07810   real centr
07811   real dhlgth
07812   real epsabs
07813   real epsrel
07814   real, external :: f
07815   real fcentr
07816   real fval
07817   real fval1
07818   real fval2
07819   real fv1(5)
07820   real fv2(5)
07821   real fv3(5)
07822   real fv4(5)
07823   real hlgth
07824   integer ier
07825   integer ipx
07826   integer k
07827   integer l
07828   integer neval
07829   real result
07830   real res10
07831   real res21
07832   real res43
07833   real res87
07834   real resabs
07835   real resasc
07836   real reskh
07837   real savfun(21)
07838   real w10(5)
07839   real w21a(5)
07840   real w21b(6)
07841   real w43a(10)
07842   real w43b(12)
07843   real w87a(21)
07844   real w87b(23)
07845   real x1(5)
07846   real x2(5)
07847   real x3(11)
07848   real x4(22)
07849 !
07850 !           the following data statements contain the abscissae
07851 !           and weights of the integration rules used.
07852 !
07853 !           x1      abscissae common to the 10-, 21-, 43- and 87-point
07854 !                   rule
07855 !           x2      abscissae common to the 21-, 43- and 87-point rule
07856 !           x3      abscissae common to the 43- and 87-point rule
07857 !           x4      abscissae of the 87-point rule
07858 !           w10     weights of the 10-point formula
07859 !           w21a    weights of the 21-point formula for abscissae x1
07860 !           w21b    weights of the 21-point formula for abscissae x2
07861 !           w43a    weights of the 43-point formula for absissae x1, x3
07862 !           w43b    weights of the 43-point formula for abscissae x3
07863 !           w87a    weights of the 87-point formula for abscissae x1,
07864 !                   x2 and x3
07865 !           w87b    weights of the 87-point formula for abscissae x4
07866 !
07867   data x1(1),x1(2),x1(3),x1(4),x1(5)/ &
07868        9.739065285171717e-01,     8.650633666889845e-01, &
07869        6.794095682990244e-01,     4.333953941292472e-01, &
07870        1.488743389816312e-01/
07871   data x2(1),x2(2),x2(3),x2(4),x2(5)/ &
07872        9.956571630258081e-01,     9.301574913557082e-01, &
07873        7.808177265864169e-01,     5.627571346686047e-01, &
07874        2.943928627014602e-01/
07875   data x3(1),x3(2),x3(3),x3(4),x3(5),x3(6),x3(7),x3(8),x3(9),x3(10), &
07876     x3(11)/ &
07877        9.993333609019321e-01,     9.874334029080889e-01, &
07878        9.548079348142663e-01,     9.001486957483283e-01, &
07879        8.251983149831142e-01,     7.321483889893050e-01, &
07880        6.228479705377252e-01,     4.994795740710565e-01, &
07881        3.649016613465808e-01,     2.222549197766013e-01, &
07882        7.465061746138332e-02/
07883   data x4(1),x4(2),x4(3),x4(4),x4(5),x4(6),x4(7),x4(8),x4(9),x4(10), &
07884     x4(11),x4(12),x4(13),x4(14),x4(15),x4(16),x4(17),x4(18),x4(19), &
07885     x4(20),x4(21),x4(22)/         9.999029772627292e-01, &
07886        9.979898959866787e-01,     9.921754978606872e-01, &
07887        9.813581635727128e-01,     9.650576238583846e-01, &
07888        9.431676131336706e-01,     9.158064146855072e-01, &
07889        8.832216577713165e-01,     8.457107484624157e-01, &
07890        8.035576580352310e-01,     7.570057306854956e-01, &
07891        7.062732097873218e-01,     6.515894665011779e-01, &
07892        5.932233740579611e-01,     5.314936059708319e-01, &
07893        4.667636230420228e-01,     3.994248478592188e-01, &
07894        3.298748771061883e-01,     2.585035592021616e-01, &
07895        1.856953965683467e-01,     1.118422131799075e-01, &
07896        3.735212339461987e-02/
07897   data w10(1),w10(2),w10(3),w10(4),w10(5)/ &
07898        6.667134430868814e-02,     1.494513491505806e-01, &
07899        2.190863625159820e-01,     2.692667193099964e-01, &
07900        2.955242247147529e-01/
07901   data w21a(1),w21a(2),w21a(3),w21a(4),w21a(5)/ &
07902        3.255816230796473e-02,     7.503967481091995e-02, &
07903        1.093871588022976e-01,     1.347092173114733e-01, &
07904        1.477391049013385e-01/
07905   data w21b(1),w21b(2),w21b(3),w21b(4),w21b(5),w21b(6)/ &
07906        1.169463886737187e-02,     5.475589657435200e-02, &
07907        9.312545458369761e-02,     1.234919762620659e-01, &
07908        1.427759385770601e-01,     1.494455540029169e-01/
07909   data w43a(1),w43a(2),w43a(3),w43a(4),w43a(5),w43a(6),w43a(7), &
07910     w43a(8),w43a(9),w43a(10)/     1.629673428966656e-02, &
07911        3.752287612086950e-02,     5.469490205825544e-02, &
07912        6.735541460947809e-02,     7.387019963239395e-02, &
07913        5.768556059769796e-03,     2.737189059324884e-02, &
07914        4.656082691042883e-02,     6.174499520144256e-02, &
07915        7.138726726869340e-02/
07916   data w43b(1),w43b(2),w43b(3),w43b(4),w43b(5),w43b(6),w43b(7), &
07917     w43b(8),w43b(9),w43b(10),w43b(11),w43b(12)/ &
07918        1.844477640212414e-03,     1.079868958589165e-02, &
07919        2.189536386779543e-02,     3.259746397534569e-02, &
07920        4.216313793519181e-02,     5.074193960018458e-02, &
07921        5.837939554261925e-02,     6.474640495144589e-02, &
07922        6.956619791235648e-02,     7.282444147183321e-02, &
07923        7.450775101417512e-02,     7.472214751740301e-02/
07924   data w87a(1),w87a(2),w87a(3),w87a(4),w87a(5),w87a(6),w87a(7), &
07925     w87a(8),w87a(9),w87a(10),w87a(11),w87a(12),w87a(13),w87a(14), &
07926     w87a(15),w87a(16),w87a(17),w87a(18),w87a(19),w87a(20),w87a(21)/ &
07927        8.148377384149173e-03,     1.876143820156282e-02, &
07928        2.734745105005229e-02,     3.367770731163793e-02, &
07929        3.693509982042791e-02,     2.884872430211531e-03, &
07930        1.368594602271270e-02,     2.328041350288831e-02, &
07931        3.087249761171336e-02,     3.569363363941877e-02, &
07932        9.152833452022414e-04,     5.399280219300471e-03, &
07933        1.094767960111893e-02,     1.629873169678734e-02, &
07934        2.108156888920384e-02,     2.537096976925383e-02, &
07935        2.918969775647575e-02,     3.237320246720279e-02, &
07936        3.478309895036514e-02,     3.641222073135179e-02, &
07937        3.725387550304771e-02/
07938   data w87b(1),w87b(2),w87b(3),w87b(4),w87b(5),w87b(6),w87b(7), &
07939     w87b(8),w87b(9),w87b(10),w87b(11),w87b(12),w87b(13),w87b(14), &
07940     w87b(15),w87b(16),w87b(17),w87b(18),w87b(19),w87b(20),w87b(21), &
07941     w87b(22),w87b(23)/            2.741455637620724e-04, &
07942        1.807124155057943e-03,     4.096869282759165e-03, &
07943        6.758290051847379e-03,     9.549957672201647e-03, &
07944        1.232944765224485e-02,     1.501044734638895e-02, &
07945        1.754896798624319e-02,     1.993803778644089e-02, &
07946        2.219493596101229e-02,     2.433914712600081e-02, &
07947        2.637450541483921e-02,     2.828691078877120e-02, &
07948        3.005258112809270e-02,     3.164675137143993e-02, &
07949        3.305041341997850e-02,     3.425509970422606e-02, &
07950        3.526241266015668e-02,     3.607698962288870e-02, &
07951        3.669860449845609e-02,     3.712054926983258e-02, &
07952        3.733422875193504e-02,     3.736107376267902e-02/
07953 !
07954 !  Test on validity of parameters.
07955 !
07956   result = 0.0e+00
07957   abserr = 0.0e+00
07958   neval = 0
07959 
07960   if ( epsabs < 0.0e+00 .and. epsrel < 0.0e+00 ) then
07961     ier = 6
07962     return
07963   end if
07964 
07965   hlgth = 5.0e-01 * ( b - a )
07966   dhlgth = abs ( hlgth )
07967   centr = 5.0e-01 * ( b + a )
07968   fcentr = f(centr)
07969   neval = 21
07970   ier = 1
07971 !
07972 !  Compute the integral using the 10- and 21-point formula.
07973 !
07974   do l = 1, 3
07975 
07976     if ( l == 1 ) then
07977 
07978       res10 = 0.0e+00
07979       res21 = w21b(6) * fcentr
07980       resabs = w21b(6) * abs(fcentr)
07981 
07982       do k = 1, 5
07983         absc = hlgth * x1(k)
07984         fval1 = f(centr+absc)
07985         fval2 = f(centr-absc)
07986         fval = fval1 + fval2
07987         res10 = res10 + w10(k)*fval
07988         res21 = res21 + w21a(k)*fval
07989         resabs = resabs + w21a(k)*(abs(fval1)+abs(fval2))
07990         savfun(k) = fval
07991         fv1(k) = fval1
07992         fv2(k) = fval2
07993       end do
07994 
07995       ipx = 5
07996 
07997       do k = 1, 5
07998         ipx = ipx + 1
07999         absc = hlgth * x2(k)
08000         fval1 = f(centr+absc)
08001         fval2 = f(centr-absc)
08002         fval = fval1 + fval2
08003         res21 = res21 + w21b(k) * fval
08004         resabs = resabs + w21b(k) * ( abs ( fval1 ) + abs ( fval2 ) )
08005         savfun(ipx) = fval
08006         fv3(k) = fval1
08007         fv4(k) = fval2
08008       end do
08009 !
08010 !  Test for convergence.
08011 !
08012       result = res21 * hlgth
08013       resabs = resabs * dhlgth
08014       reskh = 5.0e-01 * res21
08015       resasc = w21b(6) * abs ( fcentr - reskh )
08016 
08017       do k = 1, 5
08018         resasc = resasc+w21a(k)*(abs(fv1(k)-reskh)+abs(fv2(k)-reskh)) &
08019                      +w21b(k)*(abs(fv3(k)-reskh)+abs(fv4(k)-reskh))
08020       end do
08021 
08022       abserr = abs ( ( res21 - res10 ) * hlgth )
08023       resasc = resasc * dhlgth
08024 !
08025 !  Compute the integral using the 43-point formula.
08026 !
08027     else if ( l == 2 ) then
08028 
08029       res43 = w43b(12)*fcentr
08030       neval = 43
08031 
08032       do k = 1, 10
08033         res43 = res43 + savfun(k) * w43a(k)
08034       end do
08035 
08036       do k = 1, 11
08037         ipx = ipx + 1
08038         absc = hlgth * x3(k)
08039         fval = f(absc+centr) + f(centr-absc)
08040         res43 = res43 + fval * w43b(k)
08041         savfun(ipx) = fval
08042       end do
08043 !
08044 !  Test for convergence.
08045 !
08046       result = res43 * hlgth
08047       abserr = abs((res43-res21)*hlgth)
08048 !
08049 !  Compute the integral using the 87-point formula.
08050 !
08051     else if ( l == 3 ) then
08052 
08053       res87 = w87b(23) * fcentr
08054       neval = 87
08055 
08056       do k = 1, 21
08057         res87 = res87 + savfun(k) * w87a(k)
08058       end do
08059 
08060       do k = 1, 22
08061         absc = hlgth * x4(k)
08062         res87 = res87 + w87b(k) * ( f(absc+centr) + f(centr-absc) )
08063       end do
08064 
08065       result = res87 * hlgth
08066       abserr = abs ( ( res87 - res43) * hlgth )
08067 
08068     end if
08069 
08070     if ( resasc /= 0.0e+00.and.abserr /= 0.0e+00 ) then
08071       abserr = resasc * min ( 1.0e+00,(2.0e+02*abserr/resasc)**1.5e+00)
08072     end if
08073 
08074     if ( resabs > tiny ( resabs ) / ( 5.0e+01 * epsilon ( resabs ) ) ) then
08075       abserr = max (( epsilon ( resabs ) *5.0e+01) * resabs, abserr )
08076     end if
08077 
08078     if ( abserr <= max ( epsabs, epsrel*abs(result))) then
08079       ier = 0
08080     end if
08081 
08082     if ( ier == 0 ) then
08083       exit
08084     end if
08085 
08086   end do
08087 
08088   return
08089 end
08090 subroutine qsort ( limit, last, maxerr, ermax, elist, iord, nrmax )
08091 
08092 !*****************************************************************************80
08093 !
08094 !! QSORT maintains the order of a list of local error estimates.
08095 !
08096 !  Discussion:
08097 !
08098 !    This routine maintains the descending ordering in the list of the 
08099 !    local error estimates resulting from the interval subdivision process. 
08100 !    At each call two error estimates are inserted using the sequential 
08101 !    search top-down for the largest error estimate and bottom-up for the
08102 !    smallest error estimate.
08103 !
08104 !  Author:
08105 !
08106 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08107 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
08108 !
08109 !  Reference:
08110 !
08111 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08112 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
08113 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
08114 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
08115 !
08116 !  Parameters:
08117 !
08118 !    Input, integer LIMIT, the maximum number of error estimates the list can
08119 !    contain.
08120 !
08121 !    Input, integer LAST, the current number of error estimates.
08122 !
08123 !    Input/output, integer MAXERR, the index in the list of the NRMAX-th 
08124 !    largest error.
08125 !
08126 !    Output, real ERMAX, the NRMAX-th largest error = ELIST(MAXERR).
08127 !
08128 !    Input, real ELIST(LIMIT), contains the error estimates.
08129 !
08130 !    Input/output, integer IORD(LAST).  The first K elements contain 
08131 !    pointers to the error estimates such that ELIST(IORD(1)) through
08132 !    ELIST(IORD(K)) form a decreasing sequence, with
08133 !      K = LAST 
08134 !    if 
08135 !      LAST <= (LIMIT/2+2), 
08136 !    and otherwise
08137 !      K = LIMIT+1-LAST.
08138 !
08139 !    Input/output, integer NRMAX.
08140 !
08141   implicit none
08142 
08143   integer last
08144 
08145   real elist(last)
08146   real ermax
08147   real errmax
08148   real errmin
08149   integer i
08150   integer ibeg
08151   integer iord(last)
08152   integer isucc
08153   integer j
08154   integer jbnd
08155   integer jupbn
08156   integer k
08157   integer limit
08158   integer maxerr
08159   integer nrmax
08160 !
08161 !  Check whether the list contains more than two error estimates.
08162 !
08163   if ( last <= 2 ) then
08164     iord(1) = 1
08165     iord(2) = 2
08166     go to 90
08167   end if
08168 !
08169 !  This part of the routine is only executed if, due to a
08170 !  difficult integrand, subdivision increased the error
08171 !  estimate. in the normal case the insert procedure should
08172 !  start after the nrmax-th largest error estimate.
08173 !
08174   errmax = elist(maxerr)
08175 
08176   do i = 1, nrmax-1
08177 
08178     isucc = iord(nrmax-1)
08179 
08180     if ( errmax <= elist(isucc) ) then
08181       exit
08182     end if
08183 
08184     iord(nrmax) = isucc
08185     nrmax = nrmax-1
08186 
08187   end do
08188 !
08189 !  Compute the number of elements in the list to be maintained
08190 !  in descending order.  This number depends on the number of
08191 !  subdivisions still allowed.
08192 !
08193   jupbn = last
08194 
08195   if ( (limit/2+2) < last ) then
08196     jupbn = limit+3-last
08197   end if
08198 
08199   errmin = elist(last)
08200 !
08201 !  Insert errmax by traversing the list top-down, starting
08202 !  comparison from the element elist(iord(nrmax+1)).
08203 !
08204   jbnd = jupbn-1
08205   ibeg = nrmax+1
08206 
08207   do i = ibeg, jbnd
08208     isucc = iord(i)
08209     if ( elist(isucc) <= errmax ) then
08210       go to 60
08211     end if
08212     iord(i-1) = isucc
08213   end do
08214 
08215   iord(jbnd) = maxerr
08216   iord(jupbn) = last
08217   go to 90
08218 !
08219 !  Insert errmin by traversing the list bottom-up.
08220 !
08221 60 continue
08222 
08223   iord(i-1) = maxerr
08224   k = jbnd
08225 
08226   do j = i, jbnd
08227     isucc = iord(k)
08228     if ( errmin < elist(isucc) ) then
08229       go to 80
08230     end if
08231     iord(k+1) = isucc
08232     k = k-1
08233   end do
08234 
08235   iord(i) = last
08236   go to 90
08237 
08238 80 continue
08239 
08240   iord(k+1) = last
08241 !
08242 !  Set maxerr and ermax.
08243 !
08244 90 continue
08245 
08246   maxerr = iord(nrmax)
08247   ermax = elist(maxerr)
08248 
08249   return
08250 end
08251 function qwgtc ( x, c, p2, p3, p4, kp )
08252 
08253 !*****************************************************************************80
08254 !
08255 !! QWGTC defines the weight function used by QC25C.
08256 !
08257 !  Discussion:
08258 !
08259 !    The weight function has the form 1 / ( X - C ).
08260 !
08261 !  Author:
08262 !
08263 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08264 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
08265 !
08266 !  Reference:
08267 !
08268 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08269 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
08270 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
08271 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
08272 !
08273 !  Parameters:
08274 !
08275 !    Input, real X, the point at which the weight function is evaluated.
08276 !
08277 !    Input, real C, the location of the singularity.
08278 !
08279 !    Input, real P2, P3, P4, parameters that are not used.
08280 !
08281 !    Input, integer KP, a parameter that is not used.
08282 !
08283 !    Output, real QWGTC, the value of the weight function at X.
08284 !
08285   implicit none
08286 
08287   real c
08288   integer kp
08289   real p2
08290   real p3
08291   real p4
08292   real qwgtc
08293   real x
08294 
08295   qwgtc = 1.0E+00 / ( x - c )
08296 
08297   return
08298 end
08299 function qwgto ( x, omega, p2, p3, p4, integr )
08300 
08301 !*****************************************************************************80
08302 !
08303 !! QWGTO defines the weight functions used by QC25O.
08304 !
08305 !  Author:
08306 !
08307 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08308 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
08309 !
08310 !  Reference:
08311 !
08312 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08313 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
08314 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
08315 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
08316 !
08317 !  Parameters:
08318 !
08319 !    Input, real X, the point at which the weight function is evaluated.
08320 !
08321 !    Input, real OMEGA, the factor multiplying X.
08322 !
08323 !    Input, real P2, P3, P4, parameters that are not used.
08324 !
08325 !    Input, integer INTEGR, specifies which weight function is used:
08326 !    1. W(X) = cos ( OMEGA * X )
08327 !    2, W(X) = sin ( OMEGA * X )
08328 !
08329 !    Output, real QWGTO, the value of the weight function at X.
08330 !
08331   implicit none
08332 
08333   integer integr
08334   real omega
08335   real p2
08336   real p3
08337   real p4
08338   real qwgto
08339   real x
08340 
08341   if ( integr == 1 ) then
08342     qwgto = cos ( omega * x )
08343   else if ( integr == 2 ) then
08344     qwgto = sin ( omega * x )
08345   end if
08346 
08347   return
08348 end
08349 function qwgts ( x, a, b, alfa, beta, integr )
08350 
08351 !*****************************************************************************80
08352 !
08353 !! QWGTS defines the weight functions used by QC25S.
08354 !
08355 !  Author:
08356 !
08357 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08358 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner
08359 !
08360 !  Reference:
08361 !
08362 !    Robert Piessens, Elise de Doncker-Kapenger, 
08363 !    Christian Ueberhuber, David Kahaner,
08364 !    QUADPACK, a Subroutine Package for Automatic Integration,
08365 !    Springer Verlag, 1983
08366 !
08367 !  Parameters:
08368 !
08369 !    Input, real X, the point at which the weight function is evaluated.
08370 !
08371 !    Input, real A, B, the endpoints of the integration interval.
08372 !
08373 !    Input, real ALFA, BETA, exponents that occur in the weight function.
08374 !
08375 !    Input, integer INTEGR, specifies which weight function is used:
08376 !    1. W(X) = (X-A)**ALFA * (B-X)**BETA
08377 !    2, W(X) = (X-A)**ALFA * (B-X)**BETA * log (X-A)
08378 !    3, W(X) = (X-A)**ALFA * (B-X)**BETA * log (B-X)
08379 !    4, W(X) = (X-A)**ALFA * (B-X)**BETA * log (X-A) * log(B-X)
08380 !
08381 !    Output, real QWGTS, the value of the weight function at X.
08382 !
08383   implicit none
08384 
08385   real a
08386   real alfa
08387   real b
08388   real beta
08389   integer integr
08390   real qwgts
08391   real x
08392 
08393   if ( integr == 1 ) then
08394     qwgts = ( x - a )**alfa * ( b - x )**beta
08395   else if ( integr == 2 ) then
08396     qwgts = ( x - a )**alfa * ( b - x )**beta * log ( x - a )
08397   else if ( integr == 3 ) then
08398     qwgts = ( x - a )**alfa * ( b - x )**beta * log ( b - x )
08399   else if ( integr == 4 ) then
08400     qwgts = ( x - a )**alfa * ( b - x )**beta * log ( x - a ) * log ( b - x )
08401   end if
08402 
08403   return
08404 end
08405 subroutine timestamp ( )
08406 
08407 !*****************************************************************************80*
08408 !
08409 !! TIMESTAMP prints the current YMDHMS date as a time stamp.
08410 !
08411 !  Example:
08412 !
08413 !    May 31 2001   9:45:54.872 AM
08414 !
08415 !  Modified:
08416 !
08417 !    31 May 2001
08418 !
08419 !  Author:
08420 !
08421 !    John Burkardt
08422 !
08423 !  Parameters:
08424 !
08425 !    None
08426 !
08427   implicit none
08428 
08429   character ( len = 8 ) ampm
08430   integer d
08431   character ( len = 8 ) date
08432   integer h
08433   integer m
08434   integer mm
08435   character ( len = 9 ), parameter, dimension(12) :: month = (/ 
08436     'January  ', 'February ', 'March    ', 'April    ', 
08437     'May      ', 'June     ', 'July     ', 'August   ', 
08438     'September', 'October  ', 'November ', 'December ' /)
08439   integer n
08440   integer s
08441   character ( len = 10 )  time
08442   integer values(8)
08443   integer y
08444   character ( len = 5 ) zone
08445 
08446   call date_and_time ( date, time, zone, values )
08447 
08448   y = values(1)
08449   m = values(2)
08450   d = values(3)
08451   h = values(5)
08452   n = values(6)
08453   s = values(7)
08454   mm = values(8)
08455 
08456   if ( h < 12 ) then
08457     ampm = 'AM'
08458   else if ( h == 12 ) then
08459     if ( n == 0 .and. s == 0 ) then
08460       ampm = 'Noon'
08461     else
08462       ampm = 'PM'
08463     end if
08464   else
08465     h = h - 12
08466     if ( h < 12 ) then
08467       ampm = 'PM'
08468     else if ( h == 12 ) then
08469       if ( n == 0 .and. s == 0 ) then
08470         ampm = 'Midnight'
08471       else
08472         ampm = 'AM'
08473       end if
08474     end if
08475   end if
08476 
08477   write ( *, '(a,1x,i2,1x,i4,2x,i2,a1,i2.2,a1,i2.2,a1,i3.3,1x,a)' ) &
08478     trim ( month(m) ), d, y, h, ':', n, ':', s, '.', mm, trim ( ampm )
08479 
08480   return
08481 end
